<M e>and conciliated by supplications,
<M h> וּמִתְפַּיֵּס בְּתַחֲנוּנִים
<M e>be appeased and conciliated
<M h> הִתְרַצֶּה וְהִתְפַּיֵּס
<M e>to an afflicted generation,
<M h> לְדוֹר עָנִי
<M e>for there is none else to help.
<M h> כִּי אֵין עוֹזֵר:
<M t1>Our Father, our King!
<M h> אָבִֽינוּ מַלְכֵּֽנוּ
<M e>be gracious to us and answer us
<M h> חָנֵּֽנוּ וַעֲנֵֽנוּ
<M e>for we have no [good] deeds,
<M h> כִּי אֵין בָּֽנוּ מַעֲשִׂים
<M e>deal with us charitably and kindly
<M h> עֲשֵׂה עִמָּֽנוּ צְדָקָה וָחֶֽסֶד
<M e>and deliver us.
<M h> וְהוֹשִׁיעֵֽנוּ:
<M tex><M t1>As for us, we know not what to do;
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ לֺא נֵדַע מַה נַּעֲשֶׂה
<M e>but our eyes are upon You.<M tnt>
<M h> כִּי עָלֶֽיךָ עֵינֵֽינוּ:
<M e>Remember Your mercies, Adonoy,
<M h> זְכֹר רַחֲמֶֽיךָ יְהֹוָה
<M e>and kindnesses
<M h> וַחֲסָדֶֽיךָ
<M e>for
<M h> כִּי
<M e>they are from the beginning of the world.<M tnt>
<M h> מֵעוֹלָם הֵֽמָּה:
<M e>Adonoy! may Your kindness be upon us,
<M h> יְהִי חַסְדְּ֒ךָ יְהֹוָה עָלֵֽינוּ
<M e>as we have waited for You.<M tnt>
<M h> כַּאֲשֶׁר יִחַֽלְנוּ לָךְ:
<M e>Remember not the sins of our ancestors;<M tnt>
<M h> אַל תִּזְכָּר לָֽנוּ עֲוֹנוֹת רִאשׁוֹנִים
<M e>let Your mercy come swiftly toward us,<M tnt>
<M h> מַהֵר יְקַדְּ֒מֽוּנוּ רַחֲמֶֽיךָ
<M e>for we have been brought very low.
<M h> כִּי דַלּֽוֹנוּ מְאֹד:
<M e>Help us for the Name of Adonoy
<M h> עֶזְרֵֽנוּ בְּשֵׁם יְהֹוָה
<M e>Creator of Heaven and earth.
<M h> עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַֽיִם וְאָֽרֶץ:
<M e>Be gracious to us, Adonoy, be gracious to us
<M h> חָנֵּֽנוּ יְהֹוָה חָנֵּֽנוּ
<M e>for we are saturated with humiliation.<M tnt>
<M h> כִּי-רַב שָׂבַֽעְנוּ בוּז:
<M e>[Even] in anger
<M h> בְּרֺֽגֶז
<M e>remember to have compassion.<M tnt>
<M h> רַחֵם תִּזְכּוֹר:
<M e>[Even] in anger
<M h> בְּרֹֽגֶז
<M e>remember the binding of Isaac.
<M h> עַקֵדָה תִּזְכּוֹר,
<M e>Even in anger
<M h> בְּרֹֽגֶז
<xx><M tex><M e>remember the uprightness of Jacob
<M h> תְּמִימוֹת תִּזְכּוֹר:
<M e>Adonoy deliver [us]
<M h> יְהֹוָה הוֹשִֽׁיעָה,
<M e>the King will answer us on the day we call.
<M h> הַמֶּֽלֶךְ יַעֲנֵֽנוּ בְיוֹם קָרְאֵֽנוּ:
<M e>For He knows of what we are made;
<M h> כִּי הוּא יָדַע יִצְרֵֽנוּ
<M e>He is mindful that we are but dust.<M tnt>
<M h> זָכוּר כִּי עָפָר אֲנָֽחְנוּ:
<M e>Help us, God of our deliverance,
<M h> <M chaz> עָזְ֒רֵֽנוּ אֱלֺהֵי יִשְׁעֵֽנוּ
<M e>for the sake of the glory of Your Name;
<M h> עַל-דְּבַר כְּבוֹד-שְׁמֶֽךָ
<M e>save us and atone our sins,<M tnt>
<M h> וְהַצִּילֵֽנוּ וְכַפֵּר עַל-חַטֹּאתֵֽינוּ
<M e>for the sake of Your Name.<M tnt>
<M h> לְמַֽעַן שְׁמֶֽךָ:
<M e><M in>The</i> Chazzan<i> recites the Half Kaddish<FC>

<@02>Reading of the Torah
<@02>קריאת התורה
<M in>(Weekdays)<FC>
<M ex><EM><EN>The following paragraph is said on Mondays and Thursdays except on Rosh Chodesh, the eve of Pesach, Tishah b’Av, Chanukah, the 14th and 15th Adar and Adar Sheni (Purim and Purim Katan), the eve of Yom Kippur, and it is also omitted in the house of a mourner.<FL>
<EM><EN>This prayer is recited while standing, as it includes a form of viduy (<i>confession</i>) which must be said while standing.<FL>
<EM><EN>On Mondays and Thursdays, as we are about to open the Ark to take out the Seifer Torah for public reading, we realize that we have transgressed much that is written in the Torah and are unworthy even to take it into our hands. Aware of our inadequacy and unworthiness, we utter the words, "Almighty who is slow to anger etc.<NS>.<NS>.<NS>.", appealing to Him for forgiveness.<FL>
<M t2>Almighty who is slow to anger
<M h> <M newbold> אֵל אֶֽרֶךְ אַפַּֽיִם <M reg>
<M e>and full of compassion,
<M h> וּמָלֵא רַחֲמִים,
<M e>do not hide Your presence from us.
<M h> אַל-תַּסְתֵּר פָּנֶֽיךָ מִמֶּֽנוּ:
<M tex><M e>Adonoy, spare Your people<M tnt>
<M h> חֽוּסָה יְהֹוָה עַל-יִשְׂרָאֵל עַמֶּֽךָ
<M e>and save us from all evil.
<M h> וְהַצִּילֵֽנוּ מִכָּל-רָע:
<M e>We have sinned against You, Master,
<M h> חָטָֽאנוּ לְךָ אָדוֹן,
<M e>forgive us, please,
<M h> סְלַח נָא
<M e>in keeping with Your abundant mercy,
<M h> כְּרוֹב רַחֲמֶֽיךָ
<M e>Almighty.
<M h> אֵל:
<M ex><EM><EN>Moses and the Elders with him ordained that the Torah be read in public on Shabbos, Monday and Thursday mornings. The Talmud (<i>Maseches Baba Kama</i> 82), notes that Ezra later instituted that three men should be called up to read a total of at least ten verses from the Torah. He also enacted that the Torah be read at the Shabbos Mincha (afternoon) service. When the Torah is removed from the Ark, great care is taken to honor it. It is escorted by as many people as possible from the moment it is taken out of the Ark until it is placed on the reading table. We embrace and kiss the Torah during the procession and refrain from idle chatter. While the Torah is being read, you must be silent and listen to each word.<FL>
<M in>When the Holy Ark is opened, the following is said:<FC>
<M t2>Whenever the Ark traveled,
<M h> <M newbold> וַיְהִי בִּנְ֒סֹֽעַ <M reg> הָאָרֹן
<M e>Moses would say: "Rise, Adonoy
<M h> וַיּֽאמֶר משֶׁה קוּמָה יְהֹוָה
<M e>and let Your enemies be scattered,
<M h> וְיָפֻֽצוּ אֹיְ֒בֶֽיךָ
<M e>and those who hate You, flee before You."
<M h> וְיָנֻֽסוּ מְשַׂנְאֶֽיךָ מִפָּנֶֽיךָ:
<M e>For from Zion will go forth the Torah,
<M h> כִּי מִצִּיּוֹן תֵּצֵא תוֹרָה
<M e>and the word of Adonoy from Jerusalem.
<M h> וּדְ֒בַר יְהֹוָה מִירוּשָׁלָֽםִ:
<M e>Blessed is He Who gave the Torah
<M h> בָּרוּךְ שֶׁנָּתַן תּוֹרָה
<M e>to His people Israel in His holiness.
<M h> לְעַמּוֹ יִשְׂרָאֵל בִּקְ֒דֻשָּׁתוֹ:
<xx><M tex><M ex><EM><EN>The following prayer is taken from the <i>Zohar</i> (<i>Parshas Vayakhail</i>), the basic text of Kabbalah which was written by the Mishnaic sage Rabbi Shimon bar Yochai. The <i>Zohar</i> states, "When the Torah is taken out to be read before the congregation, the heavenly gates of mercy are opened, and the Divine love is aroused; therefore one should say the following prayer.<FL>
<M t1>Blessed is the Name
<M h> <M newbold> בְּרִיךְ שְׁמֵהּ <M reg>
<M e>of the Master of the universe.
<M h> דְּמָרֵא עָלְ֒מָא
<M e>Blessed is Your crown and Your place.
<M h> בְּרִיךְ כִּתְרָךְ וְאַתְרָךְ,
<M e>May Your good will [be]
<M h> יְהֵא רְעוּתָךְ
<M e>with Your people Israel forever.
<M h> עִם עַמָּךְ יִשְׂרָאֵל לְעָלָם,
<M e>The redemption of Your right hand
<M h> וּפֻרְקַן יְמִינָךְ
<M e>show Your people in Your Holy Temple.
<M h> אַחֲזֵי לְעַמָּךְ בְּבֵית מַקְדְּ֒שָׁךְ
<M e>Bestow on us Your excellent light,
<M h> וּלְ֒אַמְטוּיֵי לָנָא מִטּוּב נְהוֹרָךְ
<M e>and accept our prayer with compassion.
<M h> וּלְ֒קַבֵּל צְלוֹתָֽנָא בְּרַחֲמִין,
<M e>May it be Your will
<M h> יְהֵא רַעֲוָא קֳדָמָךְ
<M e>to prolong our lives in well-being.
<M h> דְּתוֹרִיךְ לָן חַיִּין בְּטִיבוּתָא,
<M e>Let me be counted
<M h> וְלֶהֱוֵי אֲנָא פְקִידָא
<M e>among the righteous,
<M h> בְּגוֹ צַדִּיקַיָּא,
<M e>so that You will have compassion on me
<M h> לְמִרְחַם עָלַי
<M e>and protect me and all that is mine,
<M h> וּלְ֒מִנְטַר יָתִי וְיַת כָּל דִּי לִי
<M e>and all that belongs to Your people, Israel.
<M h> וְדִי לְעַמָּךְ יִשְׂרָאֵל,
<M e>You are He
<M h> אַנְתְּ הוּא
<M e>Who nourishes all and maintains all;
<M h> זָן לְכֹלָּא וּמְ֒פַרְנֵס לְכֹלָּא,
<M e>You are He Who rules over all;
<M h> אַנְתְּ הוּא שַׁלִּיט עַל כֹּלָּא,
<M e>You are He Who rules over kings,
<M h> אַנְתְּ הוּא דְּשַׁלִּיט עַל מַלְ֒כַיָּא
<M e>and the kingdom is Yours.
<M h> וּמַלְ֒כוּתָא דִּילָךְ הִיא,
<M e>I am a servant
<M h> אֲנָא עַבְדָּא
<M e>of the Holy One, blessed is He,
<M h> דְקוּדְשָׁא בְּרִיךְ הוּא
<M tex><M e>I bow before Him
<M h> דְּסָגִֽידְנָא קַמֵּהּ
<M e>and before the honor of His Torah
<M h> וּמִקַּמֵּהּ דִּיקַר אוֹרַיְ֒תֵהּ
<M e>at all times.
<M h> בְּכָל עִדָּן וְעִדָּן,
<M e>Not in man do I put my trust,
<M h> לָא עַל אֱנָשׁ רָחִיצְנָא,
<M e>nor do I rely on any angel;
<M h> וְלָא עַל בַּר אֱלָהִין סָמִיכְנָא,
<M e>but only in the God of heaven,
<M h> אֶלָּא בֶּאֱלָהָא דִשְׁ֒מַיָּא,
<M e>Who is the true God,
<M h> דְּהוּא אֱלָהָא קְשׁוֹט,
<M e>Whose Torah is truth,
<M h> וְאוֹרַיְ֒תֵהּ קְשׁוֹט,
<M e>Whose prophets are true,
<M h> וּנְ֒בִיאוֹהִי קְשׁוֹט,
<M e>and Who performs many deeds
<M h> וּמַסְגֵּא לְמֶעְבַּד
<M e>of goodness and truth.
<M h> טַבְוָן וּקְ֒שׁוֹט,
<M e>In Him I put my trust
<M h> בֵּהּ אֲנָא רָחִיץ
<M e>and to His holy, honored Name
<M h> וְלִשְׁ֒מֵהּ קַדִּישָׁא יַקִּירָא
<M e>I utter praises.
<M h> אֲנָא אֵמַר תֻּשְׁבְּחָן,
<M e>May it be Your will
<M h> <M chaz> יְהֵא רַעֲוָא קֳדָמָךְ
<M e>to open my heart to Torah,
<M h> דְּתִפְתַּח לִבָּאִי בְּאוֹרַיְ֒תָא,
<M e>and to fulfill the desires of my heart,

<M e>for goodness, for life, and for peace.
<M h> לְטַב וּלְ֒חַיִּין וְלִשְׁ֒לָם:

<@02>Birchas Hagomeil
<@02>ברכת הגומל
<M ex><EM><EN>Rav says, (<i>Maseches Berachos</i> 54) that four are obligated to offer thanks: persons who have safely completed a sea or land journey, or who have recovered from a serious illness, or have been released from captivity. One who is obligated to recite the blessing of thanksgiving should do so at the Torah-scroll after the blessing that follows the Torah reading. It is proper not to delay the recital of the blessing for more than three days.<FL>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם
<M e>Who bestows goodness upon the guilty,
<M h> הַגּוֹמֵל לְחַיָּבִים טוֹבוֹת
<M e>Who has bestowed every goodness upon me.
<M h> שֶׁגְּ֒מָלַֽנִי כָּל טוֹב:
<M tex><M in>The congregation responds:<FC>
<M t2>He Who has bestowed goodness upon you,
<M h> מִי שֶׁגְּ֒מָלְ֒ךָ טוֹב
<M e>may He bestow every goodness upon you,
<M h> הוּא יִגְמָלְ֒ךָ כָּל-טוֹב
<M e>forever.
<M h> סֶֽלָה:

<M in>Blessing by the father of a Bar Mitzvah<FC>
<M in>The following blessing is said by the father of a Bar Mitzvah, after the lad has been called to the Torah and has recited the blessing following the reading:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed (are You)
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרוּךְ <M reg>
<M e>who has released me
<M h> שֶׁפְּ֒טָרַֽנִי
<M e>from the punishment<M tnt> of this [boy].
<M h> מֵעָנְשׁוֹ שֶׁל זֶה:
<M in>When the reading of the Torah is concluded, the Half Kaddish is recited by the Reader. The Torah is then raised so that the congregation can see the script, and the congregation exclaims:<FC>
<M t2>This is the Torah which Moses placed
<M h> <M newbold> וְזֹאת הַתּוֹרָה <M reg> אֲשֶׁר שָׂם משֶׁה
<M e>before the children of Israel
<M h> לִפְ֒נֵי בְּנֵי יִשְׂרָאֵל
<M e>at Adonoy’s command by the hand of Moses.
<M h> עַל פִּי יְהֹוָה בְּיַד משֶׁה:
<xx><M tex><M t2>It is a tree of life
<M h> עֵץ חַיִּים הִיא
<M e>to those who grasp to it,
<M h> לַמַּחֲזִיקִים בָּהּ
<M e>and those who support it are fortunate.
<M h> וְתוֹמְ֒כֶֽיהָ מְאֻשָּׁר:
<M e>Its ways are ways of pleasantness,
<M h> דְּרָכֶֽיהָ דַּרְ֒כֵי נֹֽעַם
<M e>and all its paths are peace.
<M h> וְכָל נְתִיבוֹתֶֽיהָ שָׁלוֹם:
<M e>Long life is at its right,
<M h> אֹֽרֶךְ יָמִים בִּימִינָהּ
<M e>at its left, riches and honor.
<M h> בִּשְׂ֒מֹאלָהּ עֽשֶׁר וְכָבוֹד:
<M e>Adonoy desired,
<M h> יְהֹוָה חָפֵץ
<M e>for the sake of His righteousness,
<M h> לְמַֽעַן צִדְקוֹ
<M e>to make the Torah great and to glorify it.
<M h> יַגְדִּיל תּוֹרָה וְיַאְדִּיר:

<@02>אשרי ובא לציון

<M e>and extol Your Name forever and ever.
<M h> וַאֲהַלְ֒לָה שִׁמְ֒ךָ לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M e>Adonoy is great and highly extolled,
<M h> גָּדוֹל יְהֹוָה וּמְ֒הֻלָּל מְאֹד
<M e>and His greatness is unfathomable.
<M h> וְלִגְ֒דֻלָּתוֹ אֵין חֵֽקֶר:
<M e>One generation to another
<M h> דּוֹר לְדוֹר
<M e>will praise Your works
<M h> יְשַׁבַּח מַעֲשֶׂיךָ
<M e>and Your mighty acts they will declare.
<M h> וּגְ֒בוּרֹתֶֽיךָ יַגִּֽידוּ:
<M e>The splendor of Your glorious majesty,
<M h> הֲדַר כְּבוֹד הוֹדֶֽךָ
<M e>and the words of Your wonders I will speak.
<M h> וְדִבְ֒רֵי נִפְלְ֒אֹתֶֽיךָ אָשִֽׂיחָה:
<M e>Of Your awesome might, they will speak,
<M h> וֶעֱזוּז נוֹרְ֒אוֹתֶֽיךָ יֹאמֵֽרוּ
<M e>and Your greatness I will recount.
<M h> וּגְ֒דֻלָּתְ֒ךָ אֲסַפְּ֒רֶֽנָּה:
<M e>Mention of Your bountifulness
<M h> זֵֽכֶר רַב-טוּבְ֒ךָ
<M e>they will express,
<M h> יַבִּֽיעוּ
<M e>and in Your righteousness joyfully exult.
<M h> וְצִדְ֒קָתְ֒ךָ יְרַנֵּֽנוּ:
<M e>Adonoy is gracious and compassionate,
<M h> חַנּוּן וְרַחוּם יְהֹוָה
<M e>slow to anger and great in kindliness.
<M h> אֶֽרֶךְ אַפַּֽיִם וּגְ֒דָל-חָֽסֶד:
<M e>Adonoy is good to all,
<M h> טוֹב-יְהֹוָה לַכֹּל
<M tex><M e>His mercy encompasses all His works.
<M h> וְרַחֲמָיו עַל-כָּל-מַעֲשָׂיו:
<M e>All Your works will thank You, Adonoy,
<M h> יוֹדֽוּךָ יְהֹוָה כָּל-מַעֲשֶֽׂיךָ
<M e>and Your pious ones will bless You.
<M h> וַחֲסִידֶֽיךָ יְבָרְ֒כֽוּכָה:
<M e>Of the honor of Your kingship, they will speak
<M h> כְּבוֹד מַלְ֒כוּתְ֒ךָ יֹאמֵֽרוּ
<M e>and Your might they will declare.
<M h> וּגְ֒בוּרָתְ֒ךָ יְדַבֵּֽרוּ:
<M e>To reveal to men His mighty acts,
<M h> לְהוֹדִֽיעַ לִבְ֒נֵי הָאָדָם גְּבוּרֹתָיו
<M e>and the glorious splendor of His kingship.
<M h> וּכְ֒בוֹד הֲדַר מַלְ֒כוּתוֹ:
<M e>Your kingship is the kingship for all times,
<M h> מַלְ֒כוּתְ֒ךָ מַלְ֒כוּת כָּל-עֹלָמִים
<M e>and Your dominion is in every generation.
<M h> וּמֶמְשַׁלְתְּ֒ךָ בְּכָל-דּוֹר וָדֹר:
<M e>Adonoy supports all the fallen,
<M h> סוֹמֵךְ יְהֹוָה לְכָל-הַנֹּפְ֒לִים
<M e>and straightens all the bent.
<M h> וְזוֹקֵף לְכָל-הַכְּ֒פוּפִים:
<M e>The eyes of all look expectantly to You,
<M h> עֵינֵי-כֹל אֵלֶֽיךָ יְשַׂבֵּֽרוּ
<M e>and You give them
<M h> וְאַתָּה נוֹתֵן-לָהֶם
<M e>their food at its proper time.
<M h> אֶת-אָכְלָם בְּעִתּוֹ:
<M e>You open Your hand
<M h> פּוֹתֵֽחַ אֶת-יָדֶֽךָ
<M e>and satisfy the desire of every living being.
<M h> וּמַשְׂבִּֽיעַ לְכָל-חַי רָצוֹן:
<M e>Adonoy is just in all His ways,
<M h> צַדִּיק יְהֹוָה בְּכָל-דְּרָכָיו
<M e>and benevolent in all His deeds.
<M h> וְחָסִיד בְּכָל-מַעֲשָׂיו:
<M e>Adonoy is near to all who call upon Him,
<M h> קָרוֹב יְהֹוָה לְכָל-קֹרְ֒אָיו
<M e>to all who call upon Him in truth.
<M h> לְכֹל אֲשֶׁר יִקְרָאֻֽהוּ בֶאֱמֶת:
<M e>The will of those who fear Him He fulfills;
<M h> רְצוֹן-יְרֵאָיו יַעֲשֶׂה
<M e>He hears their cry and delivers them.
<M h> וְאֶת-שַׁוְעָתָם יִשְׁמַע וְיוֹשִׁיעֵם:
<M e>Adonoy watches over all those who love Him,
<M h> שׁוֹמֵר יְהֹוָה אֶת-כָּל-אֹהֲבָיו
<M e>and will destroy all the wicked.
<M h> וְאֵת כָּל-הָרְ֒שָׁעִים יַשְׁמִיד:
<M e>Praise of Adonoy, my mouth will declare,
<M h> <M chaz> תְּהִלַּת יְהֹוָה יְדַבֶּר פִּי
<M e>and all flesh will bless
<M h> וִיבָרֵךְ כָּל-בָּשָׂר
<M e>His holy Name forever and ever.
<M h> שֵׁם קָדְשׁוֹ לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M e>And we will bless God
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ נְבָרֵךְ יָהּ
<xx><M tex><M e>from now on forever.
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד-עוֹלָם
<M e>Praise God.
<M h> הַלְ֒לוּיָהּ:
<M in>Psalm 20 is omitted on the following days: Rosh Chodesh, the day before Yom Kippur, Chanukah, both days of Purim, the day before Passover, the intermediate days of the Festivals (Chol HaMoed), and Tisha b’Av. It is also omitted when prayers are recited in the house of a mourner, the entire month of Nisssan, Pesach Sheni (14th of Iyar) Lag-b’omer, from Rosh Codesh Sivan through the twelfth of the month i.e., 5 days after Shavuoth, the Fifteenth of av, from Erev Yom Kippur until the end of Tishre, the Fifteenth of Shevat, when there is a circumcision in the Synagogue, or when a bride groom during the seven days of his wedding celebration is present.<FC>
<M ex><EM><EN>According to Rabbi S.R. Hirsch, this psalm is addressed to David by the people of Israel. It is a testimonial of trust that the people have in the Divinely-appointed king, who is accustomed to victory and triumph. At the same time, it proclaims the eternal truth that the victories which our king wins for our people are to be attributed not to his bravery, nor to his sword, nor to his soldiers, but solely to his relationship with God, His Sanctuary, and His Law.<FL>
<M t1>To Him Who grants victory, a Psalm of David
<M h> <M newbold> לַמְ֒נַצֵּֽחַ <M reg> מִזְמוֹר לְדָוִד:
<M e>May Adonoy answer you
<M h> יַעַנְ֒ךָ יְהֹוָה
<M e>on the day of distress;
<M h> בְּיוֹם צָרָה
<M e>May the Name of Jacob’s<M tnt> God fortify you.
<M h> יְשַׂגֶּבְ֒ךָ שֵׁם אֱלֺהֵי יַעֲקֹב:
<M e>May He send your help from the Sanctuary,<M tnt>
<M h> יִשְׁלַח עֶזְרְךָ מִקֹּֽדֶשׁ
<M e>and support you from Zion.
<M h> וּמִצִּיּוֹן יִסְעָדֶֽךָּ:
<xx><M tex><M e>May He remember all your meal-offerings,
<M h> יִזְכֹּר כָּל מִנְחֹתֶֽיךָ
<M e>and accept your burnt sacrifices<M tnt>, Selah.
<M h> וְעוֹלָתְ֒ךָ יְדַשְּׁ֒נֶה סֶּֽלָה:
<M e>May He grant you what your heart desires,
<M h> יִתֶּן לְךָ כִלְ֒בָבֶֽךָ
<M e>and fulfill all your plans.
<M h> וְכָל עֲצָתְ֒ךָ יְמַלֵּא:
<M e>We will sing at Your deliverance,
<M h> נְרַנְּ֒נָה בִּישׁוּעָתֶֽךָ
<M e>and in the Name of our God,
<M h> וּבְ֒שֵׁם אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>raise our banners;
<M h> נִדְגֹּל
<M e>May Adonoy fulfill all your wishes.
<M h> יְמַלֵּא יְהֹוָה כָּל מִשְׁאֲלוֹתֶֽיךָ:
<M e>Now I know
<M h> עַתָּה יָדַֽעְתִּי
<M e>that Adonoy has delivered His anointed one,
<M h> כִּי הוֹשִֽׁיעַ יְהֹוָה מְשִׁיחוֹ
<M e>He will answer him from His holy heavens
<M h> יַעֲנֵֽהוּ מִשְּׁ֒מֵי קָדְשׁוֹ
<M e>with the mighty deliverance
<M h> בִּגְ֒בוּרוֹת יֵֽשַׁע
<M e>of His right hand.
<M h> יְמִינוֹ:
<M e>Some [rely] upon chariots
<M h> אֵֽלֶּה בָרֶֽכֶב
<M e>and some upon horses,
<M h> וְאֵֽלֶּה בַסּוּסִים
<M e>but as for us,
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ
<M e>upon the Name of Adonoy, our God, we call.
<M h> בְּשֵׁם יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ נַזְכִּיר:
<M e>They have bowed down and fallen,
<M h> <M chaz> הֵֽמָּה כָּרְ֒עוּ וְנָפָֽלוּ
<M e>but we have risen and stand firm.
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ קַֽמְנוּ וַנִּתְעוֹדָד:
<M e>Adonoy, deliver [us],
<M h> יְהֹוָה הוֹשִׁיעָה
<M e>the King will answer us on the day we call.
<M h> הַמֶּֽלֶךְ יַעֲנֵֽנוּ בְיוֹם קָרְ֒אֵֽנוּ:
<iw 3><M ex><EM><EN>This portion, known as <i>Kedushas d’Sidra,</i> was introduced at the conclusion of the morning service to accomodate those who came to the synagogue too late to hear the <i>Kedushah</i> in <i>Shemoneh Esrei.</i> The Talmud (<i>Maseches Sotah</i> 49a) declares that the world is preserved solely by virtue of this <i>Kedushah,</i> and by the virtue of our answering, "May His great Name," which is part<fj>
<xx><M tex><M ex>of the <i>Kaddish</i> recited following the study of the Aggadah. Because of its importance, a vernacular translation in Aramaic was added, so that even those ignorant of Hebrew would understand the sacred words.<FL>
<M t1>The Redeemer shall come to Zion
<M h> <M newbold> וּבָא לְצִיּוֹן <M reg> גּוֹאֵל
<M e>and to those of Jacob who repent from sin,
<M h> וּלְ֒שָׁבֵי פֶֽשַׁע בְּיַעֲקֹב
<M e>says Adonoy.
<M h> נְאֻם יְהֹוָה:
<M e>As for Me, this is My covenant with them,
<M h> וַאֲנִי זֹאת בְּרִיתִי אֹתָם
<M e>said Adonoy:
<M h> אָמַר יְהֹוָה
<M e>My spirit which is upon you,
<M h> רוּחִי אֲשֶׁר עָלֶֽיךָ
<M e>and My words
<M h> וּדְ֒בָרַי
<M e>which I have put in your mouth
<M h> אֲשֶׁר שַֽׂמְתִּי בְּפִֽיךָ
<M e>shall not depart from your mouth,
<M h> לֺא יָמֽוּשׁוּ מִפִּֽיךָ
<M e>nor from the mouth of your children,
<M h> וּמִפִּי זַרְעֲךָ
<M e>nor from the mouth
<M h> וּמִפִּי
<M e>of your children’s children,
<M h> זֶֽרַע זַרְעֲךָ
<M e>said Adonoy---
<M h> אָמַר יְהֹוָה
<M e>from now to eternity.

<M h> וְאַתָּה קָדוֹשׁ

<M e>as You have sworn to our fathers

<M e>from the days of old.<M tnt>
<M h> מִֽימֵי קֶֽדֶם:
<M e>Blessed is my Master day by day;

<M e>Adonoy of Hosts,

<M h> הַמֶּֽלֶךְ יַעֲנֵֽנוּ בְיוֹם קָרְ֒אֵֽנוּ:
<M e>Blessed is He, our God,

<M h> הוּא יִפְתַּח לִבֵּֽנוּ בְּתוֹרָתוֹ
<M e>and instill in our heart love and awe of Him,

<M e>to do His will and serve Him

<M h> לִשְׁ֒נֵי יְמוֹת הַמָּשִֽׁיחַ

<M e>and those who support it are fortunate.<M tnt>
<M h> וְתוֹמְ֒כֶֽיהָ מְאֻשָּׁר:
<M e>Its ways are ways of pleasantness
<M h> <M chaz> דְּרָכֶֽיהָ דַּרְ֒כֵי נֹֽעַם
<M e>and all its paths are peace.<M tnt>
<M h> וְכָל נְתִיבוֹתֶֽיהָ שָׁלוֹם:
<M e>Cause us to return to you, Adonoy,
<M h> הֲשִׁיבֵֽנוּ יְהֹוָה אֵלֶֽיךָ
<M e>and we shall return;
<M h> וְנָשׁוּבָה
<M e>renew our days as of old.<M tnt>
<M h> חַדֵּשׁ יָמֵֽינוּ כְּקֶֽדֶם:
<xx><M tex><M in>On days in which Tachanun is not said, "A prayer of David," is omitted, and we begin "House of Jacob," (p. 000). On days in which "Almighty who is slow to anger," (p. 000) is not said, continue with the Psalm for the appropriate day (pp. 000-000).<FC>
<M t2>A prayer of David.
<M h> תְּפִלָּה לְדָוִד
<M e>Incline Your ear Adonay, and answer me,
<M h> הַטֵּה-יְהֺוָה אָזְנְךָ עֲנֵֽנִי
<M e>for poor and needy am I.
<M h> כִּי-עָנִי וְאֶבְיוֹן אָֽנִי:
<M e>Preserve my soul for I am devoted,
<M h> שָׁמְ֒רָה נַפְשִׁי כִּי-חָסִיד אָֽנִי
<M e>deliver Your servant, my God,
<M h> הוֹשַׁע עַבְדְּךָ אַתָּה אֱלֹהַי
<M e>who trusts in You.
<M h> הַבּוֹטֵֽחַ אֵלֶֽיךָ:
<M e>Be gracious to me my Master,
<M h> חָנֵּֽנִי אֲדֹנָי
<M e>for to You I cry out all the day.
<M h> כִּי-אֵלֶֽיךָ אֶקְרָא כָּל-הַיּוֹם:
<M e>Make glad the soul of Your servant,
<M h> שַׂמֵּֽחַ נֶֽפֶשׁ עַבְדֶּֽךָ
<M e>for, to You, my Master,
<M h> כִּי-אֵלֶֽיךָ אֲדֹנָי
<M e>I lift up my soul.
<M h> נַפְשִׁי אֶשָּׂא:
<M e>For You, my Master,
<M h> כִּי-אַתָּה אֲדֹנָי
<M e>are good and forgiving,
<M h> טוֹב וְסַלָּח
<M e>and abounding in kindness
<M h> וְרַב-חֶֽסֶד
<M e>to all who call upon You.
<M h> לְכָל-קֹרְ֒אֶֽיךָ:
<M e>Give ear, Adonoy, to my prayer,
<M h> הַאֲזִֽינָה יְהֺוָה תְּפִלָּתִי
<M e>and listen to the voice of my supplications.
<M h> וְהַקְשִֽׁיבָה בְּקוֹל תַּחֲנוּנוֹתָי:
<M e>In the day of my distress I call out to You,
<M h> בְּיוֹם צָרָתִי אֶקְרָאֶֽךָּ
<M e>for You will answer me.
<M h> כִּי תַעֲנֵֽנִי:
<M e>There is none like You
<M h> אֵין-כָּמֽוֹךָ
<M e>among gods, my Master,
<M h> בָאֱלֹהִים | אֲדֹנָי
<M e>and there is nothing like Your works.
<M h> וְאֵין כְּמַעֲשֶֽׂיךָ:
<M e>All nations which You have made
<M h> כָּל-גּוֹיִם אֲשֶׁר עָשִֽׂיתָ
<M e>will come and bow down
<M h> יָבֽוֹאוּ וְיִשְׁתַּחֲווּ
<M e>before You, my Master,
<M h> לְפָנֶֽיךָ אֲדֹנָי
<M tex><M e>and they will give honor to Your Name.
<M h> וִיכַבְּ֒דוּ לִשְׁמֶֽךָ:
<M e>For You are great
<M h> כִּי-גָדוֹל אַתָּה
<M e>and do wondrous things,
<M h> וְעֹשֵׂה נִפְלָאוֹת
<M e>You alone God.
<M h> אַתָּה אֱלֹהִים לְבַדֶּֽךָ:
<M e>Teach me, Adonoy, Your way
<M h> הוֹרֵֽנִי יְהֺוָה דַּרְכֶּֽךָ
<M e>that I may walk in Your truth;
<M h> אֲהַלֵּךְ בַּאֲמִתֶּֽךָ
<M e>let me be of one heart to fear Your Name.
<M h> יַחֵד לְבָבִי לְיִרְאָה שְׁמֶֽךָ:
<M e>I will thank You, my Master, my God,
<M h> אוֹדְ֒ךָ אֲדֹנָי אֱלֹהַי
<M e>with all my heart,
<M h> בְּכָל-לְבָבִי
<M e>and I will glorify Your Name, forever.
<M h> וַאֲכַבְּ֒דָה שִׁמְ֒ךָ לְעוֹלָם:
<M e>For Your kindness
<M h> כִּי-חַסְדְּךָ
<M e>has been great toward me,
<M h> גָּדוֹל עָלָי
<M e>and You have rescued my soul
<M h> וְהִצַּֽלְתָּ נַפְשִׁי
<M e>from the lowest depths of the grave.
<M h> מִשְּׁ֒אוֹל תַּחְתִּיָּה:
<M e>God, the insolent have risen up against me,
<M h> אֱלֹהִים זֵדִים קָֽמוּ-עָלַי
<M e>and a company of violent men
<M h> וַעֲדַת עָרִיצִים
<M e>have sought my soul,
<M h> בִּקְ֒שׁוּ נַפְשִׁי
<M e>and they have not set [the fear of] You
<M h> וְלֹא שָׂמֽוּךָ
<M e>before them.
<M h> לְנֶגְדָּם:
<M e>But You, my Master,
<M h> וְאַתָּה אֲדֹנָי
<M e>are the Almighty Who is Merciful
<M h> אֵל-רַחוּם
<M e>and Gracious,
<M h> וְחַנּוּן
<M e>Slow to Anger and Full of Kindness and Truth.
<M h> אֶֽרֶךְ אַפַּֽיִם וְרַב-חֶֽסֶד וֶאֱמֶת:
<M e>Turn to me and be gracious to me,
<M h> פְּנֵה אֵלַי וְחָנֵּֽנִי
<M e>give Your strength to Your servant,
<M h> תְּנָה-עֻזְּ֒ךָ לְעַבְדֶּֽךָ
<M e>and deliver the son of Your handmaid.
<M h> וְהוֹשִֽׁיעָה לְבֶן-אֲמָתֶֽךָ:
<M e>Give me a sign of Your kindness,
<M h> עֲשֵׂה-עִמִּי אוֹת לְטוֹבָה
<M e>that my enemies may see it and be ashamed,
<M h> וְיִרְאוּ שׂנְ֒אַי וְיֵבֽשׁוּ
<M tex><M e>for You, Adonoy, have helped me
<M h> כִּי-אַתָּה יְהֺוָה עֲזַרְתַּֽנִי
<M e>and comforted me.
<M h> וְנִחַמְתָּֽנִי:
<M t1>House of Jacob,
<M h> <M newbold> בֵּית יַעֲקֹב <M reg>
<M e>Come let us walk in the light of Adonoy.
<M h> לְכוּ וְנֵלְ֒כָה בְּאוֹר יְהוָֹה:
<M e>For all the nations
<M h> כִּי כָּל-הָעַמִּים
<M e>walk in the name of its god,
<M h> יֵֽלְ֒כוּ אִישׁ בְּשֵׁם אֱלֺֽהָיו,
<M e>but we walk in the Name of Adonoy,
<M h> וַֽאֲנַֽחְנוּ נֵלֵךְ בְּשֵׁם-יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, forever.
<M h> אֱלֹהֵֽינוּ לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M e>May Adonoy, our God, be with us
<M h> יְהִי יְהוָֹה אֱלֹהֵֽינוּ עִמָּֽנוּ
<M e>as He was with our fathers,
<M h> כַּֽאֲשֶׁר הָיָה עִם-אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ,
<M e>may He not forsake us nor abandon us,
<M h> אַל-יַֽעַזְ֒בֵֽנוּ וְאַל-יִטְּ֒שֵֽׁנוּ:
<M e>that He may turn our hearts to Him,
<M h> לְהַטּוֹת לְבָבֵֽנוּ אֵלָיו,
<M e>to walk in all His ways,
<M h> לָלֶֽכֶת בְּכָל-דְּרָכָיו,
<M e>to preserve His commandments, His statutes,
<M h> וְלִשְׁמֹר מִצְוֹתָיו, וְחֻקָּיו,
<M e>and His precepts,
<M h> וּמִשְׁפָּטָיו,
<M e>which He commanded our fathers.
<M h> אֲשֶׁר צִוּה אֶת-אֲבֹתֵֽינוּ:
<M e>May these words of mine
<M h> וְיִהְיוּ דְבָרַי אֵֽלֶּה
<M e>[with] which I have prayed
<M h> אֲשֶׁר הִתְחַנַּֽנְתִּי
<M e>before Adonoy,
<M h> לִפְ֒נֵי יְהוָֹה,
<M e>be near to Adonoy, our God
<M h> קְרֹבִים אֶל יְהוָֹה אֱלֹהֵֽינוּ
<M e>by day and night;
<M h> יוֹמָם וָלָֽיְלָה,
<M e>that He provide the needs of his servant
<M h> לַעֲשׂוֹת מִשְׁפַּט עַבְדּוֹ,
<M e>and the needs of His people Israel
<M h> וּמִשְׁפַּט עַמּוֹ יִשְׂרָאֵל
<M e>each day.
<M h> דְּבַר-יוֹם בְּיוֹמוֹ:
<M e>In order that it become known
<M h> לְמַֽעַן דַּֽעַת
<M e>to all the peoples of the earth
<M h> כָּל-עַמֵּי הָאָֽרֶץ,
<M e>that Adonoy is God---
<M h> כִּי יְהוָֹה הוּא הָֽאֱלֹהִים,
<M e>there is nothing else.
<M h> אֵין עוֹד:
<M tex><M t1>A Song of Ascents of David.
<M h> שִׁיר הַמַּעֲלוֹת לְדָוִד
<M e>"Had it not been for Adonoy
<M h> לוּלֵי יְהֺוָה
<M e>Who was for us,"
<M h> שֶׁהָֽיָה לָֽנוּ
<M e>let Israel now say.
<M h> יֹֽאמַר-נָא יִשְׂרָאֵל:
<M e>"Had it not been for Adonoy
<M h> לוּלֵי יְהֺוָה
<M e>Who was for us,
<M h> שֶׁהָֽיָה לָֽנוּ
<M e>when men rose up against us.
<M h> בְּקוּם עָלֵֽינוּ אָדָם:
<M e>They would have then swallowed us alive,
<M h> אֲזַי חַיִּים בְּלָעֽוּנוּ
<M e>when their wrath blazed against us.
<M h> בַּחֲרוֹת אַפָּם בָּֽנוּ:
<M e>The waters would have then swept us away,
<M h> אֲזַי הַמַּֽיִם שְׁטָפֽוּנוּ
<M e>affliction would have passed over our soul.
<M h> נַֽחְלָה עָבַר עַל-נַפְשֵֽׁנוּ:
<M e>Then over our soul would have gone
<M h> אֲזַי עָבַר עַל-נַפְשֵֽׁנוּ
<M e>the impetuous waters.
<M h> הַמַּֽיִם הַזֵּידוֹנִים:
<M e>Blessed is Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ יְהֺוָה
<M e>Who did not give us
<M h> שֶׁלֹּא נְתָנָֽנוּ
<M e>as prey to their teeth.
<M h> טֶֽרֶף לְשִׁנֵּיהֶם:
<M e>Our soul escaped as a bird
<M h> נַפְשֵֽׁנוּ כְּצִפּוֹר
<M e>out of the fowler’s snare;
<M h> נִמְלְטָה מִפַּח יוֹקְ֒שִׁים
<M e>the snare is broken
<M h> הַפַּח נִשְׁבָּר
<M e>and we escaped.
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ נִמְלָֽטְ֒נוּ:
<M e>Our help is in the Name of Adonoy,
<M h> עֶזְרֵֽנוּ בְּשֵׁם יְהֺוָה
<M e>Maker of heaven and earth."

<@02>Psalm of the Day
<@02>שיר של יום
<M ex><EM><EN>The custom of reciting a different psalm each day of the week originated in the Temple. The <i>Mishnah</i> (<i>Maseches Tamid</i> 7:4) describes the psalms which were chanted by the Levites each day during the service.<FL>
<pb><M in>On Sunday:<FC>
<M t2>Today is the first day of the week,
<M h> הַיּוֹם יוֹם רִאשׁוֹן בַּשַּׁבָּת
<M e>on which the Levites used to recite
<M h> שֶׁבּוֹ הָיוּ הַלְ֒וִיִּם אוֹמְ֒רִים
<M e>in the Holy Temple:
<M h> בְּבֵית הַמִּקְדָּשׁ:
<M t1>A psalm of David:
<M h> לְדָוִד מִזְמוֹר
<M e>the earth is Adonoy’s
<M h> לַיהוָֹה הָאָֽרֶץ
<M e>and the fullness thereof,<M tnt>
<M h> וּמְ֒לוֹאָהּ
<M e>the inhabited world
<M h> תֵּבֵל
<M e>and those who dwell in it.
<M h> וְיֽשְׁ֒בֵי בָהּ:
<M e>For He founded it upon the seas,
<M h> כִּי הוּא עַל יַמִּים יְסָדָהּ
<M e>and established it upon rivers.
<M h> וְעַל נְהָרוֹת יְכוֹנְ֒נֶֽהָ:
<M e>Who may ascend the mountain<M tnt> of Adonoy,
<M h> מִי יַעֲלֶה בְהַר יְהֹוָה
<M e>and who may stand
<M h> וּמִי יָקוּם
<M e>in the place of His holiness?
<M h> בִּמְ֒קוֹם קָדְשׁוֹ:
<M e>The clean of hands and the pure of heart,
<M h> נְקִי כַפַּֽיִם וּבַר לֵבָב
<M e>who has not borne My soul in vain,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר לֺא נָשָׂא לַשָּׁוְא נַפְשִׁי
<M e>and has not sworn deceitfully.<M tnt>
<M h> וְלֺא נִשְׁבַּע לְמִרְמָה:
<M e>He will bear Adonoy’s blessing<M tnt>
<M h> יִשָּׂא בְרָכָה מֵאֵת יְהֹוָה
<M e>and righteousness
<M h> וּצְ֒דָקָה
<M e>from the God of his deliverance.
<M h> מֵאֱלֺהֵי יִשְׁעוֹ:
<xx><M tex><M e>This is the generation of those who seek Him,
<M h> זֶה דּוֹר דּוֹרְ֒שָׁיו
<M e>the seekers of Your Presence,
<M h> מְבַקְ֒שֵׁי פָנֶֽיךָ
<M e>[God of] Jacob,<M tnt> <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> יַעֲקֹב סֶֽלָה:
<M e>Lift up your heads, gates,
<M h> שְׂאוּ שְׁעָרִים רָאשֵׁיכֶם
<M e>and be uplifted
<M h> וְהִנָּשְׂ֒אוּ
<M e>[you] entranceways to eternity,
<M h> פִּתְ֒חֵי עוֹלָם
<M e>so that the King of Glory may enter.
<M h> וְיָבוֹא מֶֽלֶךְ הַכָּבוֹד:
<M e>Who is this King of Glory?
<M h> מִי זֶה מֶֽלֶךְ הַכָּבוֹד
<M e>Adonoy, strong and mighty;
<M h> יְהֹוָה עִזּוּז וְגִבּוֹר
<M e>Adonoy, the Mighty One in battle.
<M h> יְהֹוָה גִּבּוֹר מִלְחָמָה:
<M e>Lift up your heads, gates,
<M h> שְׂאוּ שְׁעָרִים רָאשֵׁיכֶם
<M e>and lift, entranceways to eternity,
<M h> וּשְׂ֒אוּ פִּתְ֒חֵי עוֹלָם
<M e>so that the King of Glory may enter.
<M h> וְיָבוֹא מֶֽלֶךְ הַכָּבוֹד:
<M e>Who is He, this King of Glory?
<M h> <M chaz> מִי הוּא זֶה מֶֽלֶךְ הַכָּבוֹד
<M e>Adonoy of hosts,
<M h> יְהֹוָה צְבָאוֹת
<M e>He is the King of Glory, <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> הוּא מֶֽלֶךְ הַכָּבוֹד סֶֽלָה:

<AF 6:4;10><M innoa>On Monday:<FC>
<M t2>Today is the second day of the week,
<M h> הַיּוֹם יוֹם שֵׁנִי בַּשַּׁבָּת
<M e>on which the Levites used to recite
<M h> שֶׁבּוֹ הָיוּ הַלְ֒וִיִּם אוֹמְ֒רִים
<M e>in the Holy Temple:
<M h> בְּבֵית הַמִּקְדָּשׁ:
<M t2>A song, a psalm by the sons of Korach.<M tnt>
<M h> שִׁיר מִזְמוֹר לִבְ֒נֵי קֹֽרַח:
<xx><M tex><M e>Adonoy is great and highly extolled
<M h> גָּדוֹל יְהֹוָה וּמְ֒הֻלָּל מְאֹד
<M e>in the city of our God,
<M h> בְּעִיר אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>the mountain of His Sanctuary.
<M h> הַר קָדְשׁוֹ:
<M e>Beautiful in its panoramic vista,
<M h> יְפֵה נוֹף
<M e>the joy of all the earth is Mount Zion,
<M h> מְשׂוֹשׂ כָּל הָאָֽרֶץ הַר צִיּוֹן
<M e>on the northern extremities (of Jerusalem);<M tnt>
<M h> יַרְכְּתֵי צָפוֹן
<M e>the city of the great King.<M tnt>
<M h> קִרְיַת מֶֽלֶךְ רָב:
<M e>God, in its palaces,
<M h> אֱלֺהִים בְּאַרְמְנוֹתֶֽיהָ
<M e>has become known as a Stronghold.
<M h> נוֹדַע לְמִשְׂגָּב:
<M e>For behold, the kings assembled,<M tnt>
<M h> כִּי הִנֵּה הַמְּ֒לָכִים נוֹעֲדוּ
<M e>they passed by together.
<M h> עָבְ֒רוּ יַחְדָּו:
<M e>They saw and were astounded,<M tnt>
<M h> הֵֽמָּה רָאוּ כֵּן תָּמָֽהוּ
<M e>they panicked and fled in haste.
<M h> נִבְהֲלוּ נֶחְפָּֽזוּ:
<M e>Trembling siezed them there,
<M h> רְעָדָה אֲחָזָֽתַם שָׁם
<M e>like the pangs of a woman in labor.
<M h> חִיל כַּיּוֹלֵדָה:
<xx><M tex><M e>With an east wind
<M h> בְּרֽוּחַ קָדִים
<M e>You smashed the ships of Tarshish.
<M h> תְּשַׁבֵּר אֳנִיּוֹת תַּרְשִׁישׁ:
<M e>As we heard, so we saw
<M h> כַּאֲשֶׁר שָׁמַֽעְנוּ כֵּן רָאִֽינוּ
<M e>in the city of Adonoy of hosts,
<M h> בְּעִיר יְהֹוָה צְבָאוֹת
<M e>in the city of our God;
<M h> בְּעִיר אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>may God establish it for eternity, <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> אֱלֺהִים יְכוֹנְ֒נֶֽהָ עַד עוֹלָם סֶֽלָה:
<M e>We hoped, God, for Your lovingkindness
<M h> דִּמִּֽינוּ אֱלֺהִים חַסְדֶּֽךָ
<M e>in the midst of Your Sanctuary.
<M h> בְּקֶֽרֶב הֵיכָלֶֽךָ:
<M e>As Your Name, God, so is Your praise---<M tnt>
<M h> כְּשִׁמְךָ אֱלֺהִים כֵּן תְּהִלָּתְ֒ךָ
<M e>to the ends of the earth;
<M h> עַל קַצְוֵי אֶֽרֶץ
<M e>Your right hand is full of righteousness.
<M h> צֶֽדֶק מָלְ֒אָה יְמִינֶֽךָ:
<M e>Let Mount Zion rejoice,
<M h> יִשְׂמַח הַר צִיּוֹן
<M e>let the daughters<M tnt> of Judah exult,
<M h> תָּגֵֽלְנָה בְּנוֹת יְהוּדָה
<M e>because of Your judgments.
<M h> לְמַֽעַן מִשְׁפָּטֶֽיךָ:
<M e>Rally around Zion and encircle her,
<M h> סֹֽבּוּ צִיּוֹן וְהַקִּיפֽוּהָ
<M e>count her towers.
<M h> סִפְ֒רוּ מִגְדָּלֶֽיהָ:
<M e>Consider well her ramparts,
<M h> שִֽׁיתוּ לִבְּ֒כֶם לְחֵילָה
<M e>raise high her citadels,
<M h> פַּסְּ֒גוּ אַרְמְ֒נוֹתֶֽיהָ
<M e>that you may recount it to future generations.
<M h> לְמַֽעַן תְּסַפְּ֒רוּ לְדוֹר אַחֲרוֹן:
<M e>That this is God, our God
<M h> <M chaz> כִּי זֶה אֱלֺהִים אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>forever and ever,
<M h> עוֹלָם וָעֶד
<M e>He will lead us like children.<M tnt>
<M h> הוּא יְנַהֲגֵֽנוּ עַל מוּת:
<M in>(Deliver us<ns>.<ns>.<ns>., p. 000; Mourner’s Kaddish, p. 000.)<FC>

<M t2>Today is the third day of the week,
<M h> הַיּוֹם יוֹם שְׁלִישִׁי בַּשַּׁבָּת
<M e>on which the Levites used to recite
<M h> שֶׁבּוֹ הָיוּ הַלְ֒וִיִּם אוֹמְ֒רִים
<M e>in the Holy Temple:
<M h> בְּבֵית הַמִּקְדָּשׁ:
<M t1>A psalm of Assaf<k 2><M tnt>
<M h> מִזְמוֹר לְאָסָף
<M e>God stands
<M h> אֱלֺהִים נִצָּב
<M e>in the congregation of the Almighty,<M tnt>
<M h> בַּעֲדַת אֵל
<M e>in the midst of the judges He gives judgement.
<M h> בְּקֶֽרֶב אֱלֺהִים יִשְׁפֹּט:
<M e>How long will you judge lawlessly
<M h> עַד מָתַי תִּשְׁפְּטוּ עָֽוֶל
<M e>and show partiality to the wicked forever?
<M h> וּפְ֒נֵי רְשָׁעִים תִּשְׂ֒אוּ סֶֽלָה:
<M e>Render justice to the lowly and the orphan,
<M h> שִׁפְ֒טוּ דָל וְיָתוֹם
<M e>deal righteously with the poor and destitute.
<M h> עָנִי וָרָשׁ הַצְדִּֽיקוּ:
<M e>Rescue the lowly and the needy,
<M h> פַּלְּ֒טוּ דַל וְאֶבְיוֹן
<M e>save them from the hand of the wicked.
<M h> מִיַּד רְשָׁעִים הַצִּֽילוּ:
<M e>They neither know nor understand,<M tnt>
<M h> לֺא יָדְ֒עוּ וְלֺא יָבִֽינוּ
<M e>they walk along in darkness,
<M h> בַּחֲשֵׁכָה יִתְהַלָּֽכוּ
<M e>all the foundations of the earth are shaken.<M tnt>
<M h> יִמּֽוֹטוּ כָּל מֽוֹסְ֒דֵי אָֽרֶץ:
<M e>I had said "You are godlike beings,
<M h> אֲנִי אָמַֽרְתִּי אֱלֺהִים אַתֶּם
<xx><M tex><M e>all of you, sons of the Most High."
<M h> וּבְ֒נֵי עֶלְיוֹן כֻּלְּ֒כֶם:
<M e>Nevertheless, you shall die like men,
<M h> אָכֵן כְּאָדָם תְּמוּתוּן
<M e>and fall like one of the princes.
<M h> וּכְ֒אַחַד הַשָּׂרִים תִּפֹּֽלוּ:
<M e>Arise, God, judge the earth,
<M h> <M chaz> קוּמָה אֱלֺהִים שָׁפְ֒טָה הָאָרֶץ
<M e>for You will inherit all the nations.
<M h> כִּי אַתָּה תִנְחַל בְּכָל הַגּוֹיִם:

<M t2>Today is the fourth day of the week,
<M h> הַיּוֹם יוֹם רְבִיעִי בַּשַּׁבָּת
<M e>on which the Levites used to recite
<M h> שֶׁבּוֹ הָיוּ הַלְ֒וִיִּם אוֹמְ֒רִים
<M e>in the Holy Temple:
<M h> בְּבֵית הַמִּקְדָּשׁ:
<M t1>Almighty of vengeance, Adonoy,<M tnt>
<M h> אֵל נְקָמוֹת יְהֹוָה
<M e>Almighty of vengeance, reveal Yourself.
<M h> אֵל נְקָמוֹת הוֹפִֽיעַ:
<M e>Arise Judge of the earth,
<M h> הִנָּשֵׂא שֹׁפֵט הָאָֽרֶץ
<M e>repay the arrogant their just reward.
<M h> הָשֵׁב גְּמוּל עַל גֵּאִים:
<M e>How long shall the wicked---
<M h> עַד מָתַי רְשָׁעִים
<M e>Adonoy---
<M h> יְהֹוָה
<M e>how long shall the wicked exult?
<M h> עַד מָתַי רְשָׁעִים יַעֲלֺֽזוּ:
<M e>They express, they speak with arrogance;
<M h> יַבִּֽיעוּ יְדַבְּ֒רוּ עָתָק
<M e>all the evildoers are boastful.
<M h> יִתְאַמְּ֒רוּ כָּל פֹּֽעֲלֵי אָֽוֶן:
<M e>Adonoy, they crush Your people
<M h> עַמְּ֒ךָ יְהֹוָה יְדַכְּ֒אוּ
<M e>and Your heritage they oppress.
<M h> וְנַחֲלָתְ֒ךָ יְעַנּוּ:
<M e>The widow and stranger they kill,
<M h> אַלְמָנָה וְגֵר יַהֲרֹֽגוּ
<xx><M tex><M e>and orphans they murder.
<M h> וִיתוֹמִים יְרַצֵּֽחוּ:
<M e>And they say, "God does not see,
<M h> וַיֹּאמְ֒רוּ לֺא יִרְאֶה יָהּ
<M e>the God of Jacob is not concerned."
<M h> וְלֺא יָבִין אֱלֺהֵי יַעֲקֹב:
<M e>Consider,
<M h> בִּֽינוּ
<M e>[you] stupid [ones] among the people,---
<M h> בֹּעֲרִים בָּעָם
<M e>and you fools when will you become wise?
<M h> וּכְ֒סִילִים מָתַי תַּשְׂכִּֽילוּ:
<M e>He Who implanted the ear, does He not hear?
<M h> הֲנֹֽטַע אֹֽזֶן הֲלֺא יִשְׁמָע
<M e>He Who formed the eye, does He not see?
<M h> אִם יוֹצֵר עַֽיִן הֲלֺא יַבִּיט:
<M e>He Who chastises nations,
<M h> הֲיֹסֵר גּוֹיִם
<M e>does He not reprove---
<M h> הֲלֺא יוֹכִֽיחַ
<M e>He that teaches man knowledge?
<M h> הַמְ֒לַמֵּד אָדָם דָּֽעַת:
<M e>Adonoy knows the thoughts of men,
<M h> יְהֹוָה יֹדֵֽעַ מַחְשְׁ֒בוֹת אָדָם
<M e>that they are vanity.
<M h> כִּי הֵֽמָּה הָֽבֶל:
<M e>Fortunate is the man
<M h> אַשְׁרֵי הַגֶּֽבֶר
<M e>whom You chastise, God,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר תְּיַסְּ֒רֶֽנּוּ יָהּ
<M e>and whom You instruct from Your Torah.
<M h> וּמִתּוֹרָתְ֒ךָ תְלַמְּ֒דֶֽנּוּ:
<M e>To grant him tranquility from days of evil,
<M h> לְהַשְׁקִיט לוֹ מִֽימֵי רָע
<M e>until the pit is dug for the wicked.
<M h> עַד יִכָּרֶה לָרָשָׁע שָֽׁחַת:
<M e>for Adonoy will not abandon His people
<M h> כִּי לֺא יִטּשׁ יְהֹוָה עַמּוֹ
<M e>and His inheritance, He will not forsake.
<M h> וְנַחֲלָתוֹ לֺא יַעֲזֹב:
<M e>For justice shall return unto righteousness,
<M h> כִּי עַד צֶֽדֶק יָשׁוּב מִשְׁפָּט
<M e>and all the upright in heart will follow it.
<M h> וְאַחֲרָיו כָּל יִשְׁ֒רֵי לֵב:
<M e>Who will rise up for me against the wicked,
<M h> מִי יָקוּם לִי עִם מְרֵעִים
<M e>who will stand up for me
<M h> מִי יִתְיַצֵּב לִי
<M e>against the evildoers?
<M h> עִם פֹּֽעֲלֵי אָֽוֶן:
<M e>Had Adonoy not been my help,
<M h> לוּלֵי יְהֹוָה עֶזְרָֽתָה לִּי
<M e>in an instant
<M h> כִּמְ֒עַט
<M e>my soul would have dwelt in the silent grave.
<M h> שָׁכְ֒נָה דוּמָה נַפְשִׁי:
<M tex><M e>If [Whenever] I said, my foot has slipped,
<M h> אִם אָמַֽרְתִּי מָֽטָה רַגְלִי
<M e>Your kindliness, Adonoy upheld me.
<M h> חַסְדְּךָ יְהֹוָה יִסְעָדֵֽנִי:
<M e>When (worrisome) thoughts multiply
<M h> בְּרֹב שַׂרְעַפַּי
<M e>within me,
<M h> בְּקִרְבִּי
<M e>Your consolations soothe my soul.
<M h> תַּנְחוּמֶֽיךָ יְשַׁעַשְׁ֒עוּ נַפְשִׁי:
<M e>Can a tribunal of evil have accord with You---
<M h> הַיְ֒חָבְרְךָ כִּסֵּא הַוּוֹת
<M e>[a tribunal] that makes iniquity into law?
<M h> יֹצֵר עָמָל עֲלֵי חֹק:
<M e>They gang up against the life of the righteous,
<M h> יָגֽוֹדּוּ עַל נֶֽפֶשׁ צַדִּיק
<M e>and blood of the innocent they condemn.
<M h> וְדָם נָקִי יַרְשִֽׁיעוּ:
<M e>Adonoy has been my stronghold,
<M h> וַיְ֒הִי יְהֹוָה לִי לְמִשְׂגָּב
<M e>my God the Rock of my refuge.
<M h> וֵאלֺהַי לְצוּר מַחְסִי:
<M e>He turns their violence against them,
<M h> וַיָּֽשֶׁב עֲלֵיהֶם אֶת אוֹנָם
<M e>and with their own wickedness
<M h> וּבְ֒רָעָתָם
<M e>destroys them;
<M h> יַצְמִיתֵם
<M e>Adonoy, my God, destroys them.
<M h> יַצְמִיתֵם יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ:
<M e>Come let us sing to Adonoy;
<M h> לְכוּ נְרַנְּ֒נָה לַיהוָֹה
<M e>let us shout for joy
<M h> נָרִֽיעָה
<M e>to the Rock of our Deliverance.<M tnt>
<M h> לְצוּר יִשְׁעֵֽנוּ:
<M e>Let us greet Him with thanksgiving;
<M h> <M chaz> נְקַדְּ֒מָה פָנָיו בְּתוֹדָה
<M e>with song let us shout for joy to Him.
<M h> בִּזְמִרוֹת נָרִֽיעַ לוֹ:
<M e>for a great Almighty is Adonoy;
<M h> כִּי אֵל גָּדוֹל יְהֹוָה
<M e>a great King over all godlike beings.
<M h> וּמֶֽלֶךְ גָּדוֹל עַל כָּל אֱלֺהִים:

<M h> כִּנּוֹר נָעִים עִם נָֽבֶל:
<M e>Blow the <i>shofar</i> on the <i>Rosh Chodesh,</i>

<M h> בַּכֶּֽסֶה לְיוֹם חַגֵּֽנוּ:

<M e>to give thanks to Your holy Name,
<M h> לְהוֹדוֹת לְשֵׁם קָדְשֶֽׁךָ
<M e>to be extolled in Your praise.

<M ex><EM><EN>The following psalm (104) is recited in many synagogues on Rosh Chodesh days, following the daily psalm.<FL>
<M t2>My soul, bless Adonoy;
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרְ֒כִי נַפְשִׁי <M reg> אֶת-יְהֹוָה
<M e>Adonoy, my God, You are greatly exalted;
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהַי גָּדַֽלְתָּ מְאֹד,
<M e>with beauty and splendor
<M h> הוֹד וְהָדָר
<M e>are You clothed.
<M h> לָבָֽשְׁתָּ:
<M e>Enwrapped in light, garment-like,
<M h> עֹֽטֶה אוֹר כַּשַּׂלְמָה,
<M e>He spreads out the heavens like a curtain.
<M h> נוֹטֶה שָׁמַֽיִם כַּיְ֒רִיעָה:
<M e>He Who covers
<M h> הַמְ֒קָרֶה
<M e>His upper chambers with water,<M tnt>
<M h> בַמַּֽיִם עֲלִיּוֹתָיו
<M e>He Who makes clouds His chariot,
<M h> הַשָּׂם-עָבִים רְכוּבוֹ,
<M e>He Who walks upon wings of wind.
<M h> הַמְ֒הַלֵּךְ עַל-כַּנְ֒פֵי-רֽוּחַ:
<M e>He Who makes winds His messengers,
<M h> עֹשֶׂה מַלְאָכָיו רוּחוֹת,
<M e>flaming fires His servants.
<M h> מְשָׁרְ֒תָיו אֵשׁ לֺהֵט:
<M e>He Who established the earth
<M h> יָסַד אֶֽרֶץ
<M e>upon its foundations,
<M h> עַל-מְכוֹנֶֽיהָ,
<M e>[so] that it shall never be moved.
<M h> בַּל-תִּמּוֹט עוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M e>The deep,
<M h> תְּהוֹם
<M e>He covered as with a garment;<M tnt>
<M h> כַּלְּ֒בוּשׁ כִּסִּיתוֹ,
<M e>the waters remain on mountains.<M tnt>
<M h> עַל-הָרִים יַֽעַמְ֒דוּ מָֽיִם:
<M e>At Your shout they retreated,
<M h> מִן-גַּעֲרָתְ֒ךָ יְנוּסוּן,
<xx><M tex><M e>at Your thunderous voice
<M h> מִן-קוֹל רַעַמְ֒ךָ
<M e>they hastened away.<M tnt>
<M h> יֵחָפֵזוּן:
<M e>They go up mountains, down into valleys,
<M h> יַעֲלוּ הָרִים יֵרְ֒דוּ בְקָעוֹת,
<M e>to the specific place You founded for them.
<M h> אֶל-מְקוֹם זֶה יָסַֽדְתָּ לָהֶם:
<M e>You set a boundary<M tnt>
<M h> גְּבוּל-שַֽׂמְתָּ
<M e>[which] they may not cross,
<M h> בַּל-יַעֲבֹרוּן,
<M e>lest they return to cover the earth.
<M h> בַּל-יְשֻׁבוּן לְכַסּוֹת הָאָֽרֶץ:
<M e>He Who sends springs into streams
<M h> הַמְ֒שַׁלֵּֽחַ מַעְיָנִים בַּנְּ֒חָלִים,
<M e>to flow between the mountains;
<M h> בֵּין הָרִים יְהַלֵּכוּן:
<M e>to water all the beasts of the fields;
<M h> יַשְׁקוּ כָּל-חַיְ֒תוֹ שָׂדָי,
<M e>the wild ones quench their thirst.
<M h> יִשְׁבְּרוּ פְרָאִים צְמָאָם:
<M e>Over them dwell the birds of the sky,
<M h> עֲלֵיהֶם עוֹף-הַשָּׁמַֽיִם יִשְׁכּוֹן,
<M e>from among the branches, they give voice.
<M h> מִבֵּין עֳפָאִים יִתְּ֒נוּ-קוֹל:
<M e>[You] Who waters the mountains
<M h> מַשְׁקֶה הָרִים
<M e>from His upper chambers,<M tnt>
<M h> מֵעֲלִיּוֹתָיו,
<M e>from the fruit of Your works<M tnt>
<M h> מִפְּ֒רִי מַעֲשֶֽׂיךָ
<M e>the earth is sated.
<M h> תִּשְׂבַּע הָאָֽרֶץ:
<M e>[You] Who causes grass to sprout for cattle,
<M h> מַצְמִֽיחַ חָצִיר לַבְּ֒הֵמָה
<M e>and vegetation for the labor of man,
<M h> וְעֵֽשֶׂב לַעֲבֹדַת הָאָדָם,
<M e>to bring forth bread from the earth;
<M h> לְהוֹצִיא לֶֽחֶם מִן-הָאָֽרֶץ:
<M e>wine to cheer the heart of man,
<M h> וְיַֽיִן יְשַׂמַּח לְבַב-אֱנוֹשׁ
<M e>to make [his] face shine from oil,
<M h> לְהַצְהִיל פָּנִים מִשָּֽׁמֶן,
<M e>and bread to sustain the heart of man.
<M h> וְלֶֽחֶם לְבַב-אֱנוֹשׁ יִסְעָד:
<xx><M tex><M e>Adonoy’s trees are sated,<M tnt>
<M h> יִשְׂבְּ֒עוּ עֲצֵי יְהֹוָה
<M e>the cedars of Lebanon that He planted;
<M h> אַרְ֒זֵי לְבָנוֹן אֲשֶׁר נָטָע:
<M e>where birds make their nests,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר-שָׁם צִפֳּרִים יְקַנֵּֽנוּ,
<M e>the stork---the firs are her home.
<M h> חֲסִידָה בְּרוֹשִׁים בֵּיתָהּ:
<M e>The high mountains [are] for the wild goats,
<M h> הָרִים הַגְּ֒בֹהִים לַיְּ֒עֵלִים,
<M e>the rocks a refuge for the rabbits.
<M h> סְלָעִים מַחְסֶה לַשְּׁ֒פַנִּים:
<M e>He made the moon to fix seasons
<M h> עָשָׂה יָרֵֽחַ לְמוֹעֲדִים
<M e>the sun knows its place to set.
<M h> שֶֽׁמֶשׁ יָדַע מְבוֹאוֹ:
<M e>You make darkness and night comes,
<M h> תָּֽשֶׁת חֽשֶׁךְ וִיהִי לָֽיְלָה,
<M e>in which move about
<M h> בּוֹ-תִרְמֹשׂ
<M e>all the beasts of the forest.
<M h> כָּל-חַֽיְ֒תוֹ-יָֽעַר:
<M e>---The young lions roar for prey,
<M h> הַכְּ֒פִירִים שֹׁאֲגִים לַטָּֽרֶף,
<M e>and seek their food from the Almighty.
<M h> וּלְ֒בַקֵּשׁ מֵאֵל אָכְלָם:
<M e>[When] the sun rises, they gather
<M h> תִּזְרַח הַשֶּֽׁמֶשׁ יֵאָסֵפוּן,
<M e>and come into their dens to lie.
<M h> וְאֶל-מְעוֹנֹתָם יִרְבָּצוּן:
<M e>Man goes out to his work,
<M h> יֵצֵא אָדָם לְפָעֳלוֹ,
<M e>to his labor until evening.
<M h> וְלַעֲבֹדָתוֹ עֲדֵי-עָֽרֶב:
<M e>How many are Your works, Adonoy!
<M h> מָה-רַבּוּ מַעֲשֶֽׂיךָ יְהֹוָה
<M e>You made them all with wisdom;
<M h> כֻּלָּם בְּחָכְמָה עָשִֽׂיתָ,
<M e>the earth is full of Your possessions!
<M h> מָלְ֒אָה הָאָֽרֶץ קִנְיָנֶֽךָ:
<M e>This sea, great and wide---
<M h> זֶה הַיָּם גָּדוֹל וּרְ֒חַב יָדָֽיִם
<M e>therein are innumerable creeping things,
<M h> שָׁם-רֶֽמֶשׂ וְאֵין מִסְפָּר,
<M e>animals small and great.
<M h> חַיּוֹת קְטַנּוֹת עִם-גְּדֹלוֹת:
<M e>There ships travel;
<M h> שָׁם אֳנִיּוֹת יְהַלֵּכוּן,
<M e>this Leviathan<M tnt>
<M h> לִוְיָתָן זֶה
<xx><M tex><M e>You formed to frolic with.
<M h> יָצַֽרְתָּ לְשַֽׂחֶק-בּוֹ:
<M e>They all look to You expectantly,
<M h> כֻּלָּם אֵלֶֽיךָ יְשַׂבֵּרוּן,
<M e>to provide their food in its time.
<M h> לָתֵת אָכְלָם בְּעִתּוֹ:
<M e>[When] You give it to them,
<M h> תִּתֵּן לָהֶם
<M e>they gather it in;
<M h> יִלְקֹטוּן,
<M e>[when] You open Your hand,
<M h> תִּפְתַּח יָדְ֒ךָ
<M e>they are sated with goodness.
<M h> יִשְׂבְּעוּן טוֹב:
<M e>Whey You hide Your face,<M tnt>
<M h> תַּסְתִּיר פָּנֶֽיךָ
<M e>they are panic-stricken;
<M h> יִבָּהֵלוּן
<M e>When You gather in their breath, they perish,
<M h> תֹּסֵף רוּחָם יִגְוָעוּן,
<M e>and to their dust they return.
<M h> וְאֶל-עֲפָרָם יְשׁוּבוּן:
<M e>When You send Your spirit,<M tnt>
<M h> תְּשַׁלַּח רוּחֲךָ
<M e>they will be created [anew];
<M h> יִבָּרֵאוּן,
<M e>and You will renew the face of the earth.
<M h> וּתְ֒חַדֵּשׁ פְּנֵי אֲדָמָה:
<M e>The glory of Adonoy will endure forever,
<M h> יְהִי כְבוֹד יְהֹוָה לְעוֹלָם,
<M e>Adonoy will rejoice in His works---
<M h> יִשְׂמַח יְהֹוָה בְּמַעֲשָׂיו:
<M e>Who gazes upon the earth and it trembles;
<M h> הַמַּבִּיט לָאָֽרֶץ וַתִּרְעָד,
<M e>Who touches the mountains and they erupt.
<M h> יִגַּע בֶּהָרִים וְיֶעֱשָֽׁנוּ:
<M e>I will sing to Adonoy with my life;
<M h> אָשִֽׁירָה לַּיהוָֹה בְּחַיָּי,
<M e>I will offer hymns to my God
<M h> אֲזַמְּ֒רָה לֵאלֺהַי
<M e>as long as I am alive.
<M h> בְּעוֹדִי:
<M e>May my words be pleasant to Him;
<M h> יֶעֱרַב עָלָיו שִׂיחִי,
<M e>I will rejoice in Adonoy.<M tnt>
<M h> אָנֹכִי אֶשְׂמַח בַּיהוָֹה:
<M e>Sin will be excised from the earth,
<M h> <M chaz> יִתַּֽמּוּ חַטָּאִים מִן-הָאָֽרֶץ
<xx><M tex><M e>and the wicked will be no more;
<M h> וּרְ֒שָׁעִים עוֹד אֵינָם
<M e>My soul bless Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרְ֒כִי נַפְשִׁי אֶת-יְהֹוָה
<M e>Praise God.
<M h> הַלְ֒לוּיָהּ:
<M in>(Mourner’s Kaddish, p. 000.)<FC>

<@02>Psalm from Rosh Chodesh Elul
<@02>לדוד ה' אורי
<M ex><EM><EN>The following psalm (27) is recited at the conclusion of services, morning and evenings, from the first day of Elul, through Shemini Atzeres. Others say only until Hoasha’na Rabbah.<FL>
<EM><EN>The psalm voices our prayer that God will be our light on Rosh Hashana enabling us to repel the darkness of sin through true repentance, and that He will be our salvation on Yom Kippur, through His compassionate atonement of our sins.<FL>
<M t1>By David:
<M h> <M newbold> לְדָוִד <M reg>
<M e>Adonoy is my light and my salvation,
<M h> יְהֹוָה אוֹרִי וְיִשְׁעִי
<M e>whom shall I fear?
<M h> מִמִּי אִירָא
<M e>Adonoy is the strength<M tnt> of my life,
<M h> יְהֹוָה מָעוֹז חַיַּי
<M e>of whom shall I be afraid?
<M h> מִמִּי אֶפְחָד:
<M e>When evildoers approach me
<M h> בִּקְ֒רֹב עָלַי מְרֵעִים
<M e>to devour my flesh---
<M h> לֶאֱכֹל אֶת בְּשָׂרִי
<M e>my tormentors and my foes
<M h> צָרַי וְאֹיְ֒בַי לִי
<M e>they stumble and fall.
<M h> הֵֽמָּה כָשְׁ֒לוּ וְנָפָֽלוּ:
<M e>If an army should encamp against me,
<M h> אִם תַּחֲנֶה עָלַי מַחֲנֶה
<M e>my heart would not fear;
<M h> לֺא יִירָא לִבִּי
<M e>if war were to rise against me,
<M h> אִם תָּקוּם עָלַי מִלְחָמָה
<xx><M tex><M e>in this<M tnt> I trust.
<M h> בְּזֹאת אֲנִי בוֹטֵֽחַ:
<M e>One thing I request of Adonoy,
<M h> אַחַת שָׁאַֽלְתִּי מֵאֵת יְהֹוָה
<M e>[only] that shall I seek,
<M h> אוֹתָהּ אֲבַקֵּשׁ
<M e>that I may dwell<M tnt> in the House of Adonoy
<M h> שִׁבְתִּי בְּבֵית יְהֹוָה
<M e>all the days of my life,
<M h> כָּל יְמֵי חַיַּי
<M e>to behold the pleasantness of Adonoy,
<M h> לַחֲזוֹת בְּנֹֽעַם יְהֹוָה
<M e>and to meditate in His Sanctuary.
<M h> וּלְ֒בַקֵּר בְּהֵיכָלוֹ:
<M e>For He will hide me in His Tabernacle<M tnt>
<M h> כִּי יִצְפְּ֒נֵֽנִי בְּסֻכֹּה
<M e>on the day of distress,
<M h> בְּיוֹם רָעָה
<M e>He will conceal me in the shelter of His Tent,
<M h> יַסְתִּרֵֽנִי בְּסֵֽתֶר אָהֳלוֹ
<M e>upon a rock He will lift me.
<M h> בְּצוּר יְרוֹמְ֒מֵֽנִי:
<M e>And now my head is raised high
<M h> וְעַתָּה יָרוּם רֹאשִׁי
<M e>above my enemies around me;<M tnt>
<M h> עַל אֹיְ֒בַי סְבִיבוֹתָי
<M e>and I will offer in His Tent,
<M h> וְאֶזְבְּחָה בְאָהֳלוֹ
<M e>sacrifices accompanied by trumpets of joy;
<M h> זִבְ֒חֵי תְרוּעָה
<M e>I will sing and chant to Adonoy.
<M h> אָשִֽׁירָה וַאֲזַמְּ֒רָה לַיהוָֹה:
<M e>Adonoy, hear my voice<M tnt> when I call;
<M h> שְׁמַע יְהֹוָה קוֹלִי אֶקְרָא
<M e>be gracious to me and answer me.
<M h> וְחָנֵּֽנִי וַעֲנֵֽנִי:
<xx><M tex><M e>Of You, my heart has said,
<M h> לְךָ אָמַר לִבִּי
<M e>"Seek My Presence";
<M h> בַּקְּ֒שׁוּ פָנָי
<M e>Your Presence, Adonoy I will seek.
<M h> אֶת פָּנֶֽיךָ יְהֹוָה אֲבַקֵּשׁ:
<M e>Conceal not Your Presence from me,
<M h> אַל תַּסְתֵּר פָּנֶֽיךָ מִמֶּֽנִּי
<M e>do not turn away Your servant in anger.
<M h> אַל תַּט בְּאַף עַבְדֶּֽךָ
<M e>You have been my help;
<M h> עֶזְרָתִי הָיִֽיתָ
<M e>neither cast me off nor abandon me,
<M h> אַל תִּטְּ֒שֵֽׁנִי וְאַל תַּעַזְ֒בֵֽנִי
<M e>God of my deliverance.
<M h> אֱלֺהֵי יִשְׁעִי:
<M e>When my father and mother abandon<M tnt> me,
<M h> כִּי אָבִי וְאִמִּי עֲזָבֽוּנִי
<M e>Adonoy will gather me up.
<M h> וַיהוָֹה יַאַסְ֒פֵֽנִי:
<M e>Adonoy, teach me Your way,
<M h> הוֹרֵֽנִי יְהֹוָה דַּרְכֶּֽךָ
<M e>and lead me in the path of uprightness,
<M h> וּנְ֒חֵֽנִי בְּאֹֽרַח מִישׁוֹר
<M e>because of my watchers.<M tnt>
<M h> לְמַֽעַן שׁוֹרְ֒רָי:
<M e>Do not deliver me
<M h> אַל תִּתְּ֒נֵֽנִי
<M e>to the will of my tormentors,
<M h> בְּנֶֽפֶשׁ צָרָי
<M e>for false witnesses have risen against me,
<M h> כִּי קָֽמוּ בִי עֵֽדֵי שֶֽׁקֶר
<M e>who breathe violence.
<M h> וִיפֵֽחַ חָמָס:
<M e>Had I not believed<M tnt> that I would see
<M h> לוּלֵא הֶאֱמַֽנְתִּי לִרְאוֹת
<M e>the goodness of Adonoy
<M h> בְּטוּב יְהֹוָה
<M e>in the land of living.<M tnt>
<M h> בְּאֶֽרֶץ חַיִּים:
<xx><M tex><M e>Hope to Adonoy,
<M h> <M chaz> קַוּה אֶל יְהֹוָה
<M e>be strong and He will give you courage;
<M h> חֲזַק וְיַאֲמֵץ לִבֶּךָ
<M e>and hope to Adonoy.
<M h> וְקַוּה אֶל יְהֹוָה:

<@02>Psalm in the House of a Mourner
<@02>מזמור לבית האבל
<M in>On days when Tachanun is said:<FC>
<M ex><EM><EN>It is customary to recite this psalm (49) in the house of a mourner during the week of mourning, following the morning and evening services. On weekdays when <i>Tachanun</i> is not said Psalm 16 (page 218) is substituted. This psalm, the final hymn of the psalms set down by the sons of Korach has significance for all mankind. Its message is that man must utilize all his material and physical resources to enhance his spiritual existence so that when his soul survives the body’s brief stay on earth it can ascend to immortality. If man fails to recognize his purpose in life and instead regards the acquisition of material wealth the primary aim of life, he forfeits his hope of immortality, and his existence will not continue beyond the grave.---<i>S.R.<i> Hirsch</i><FL>
<M t1>To Him Who grants victory,
<M h> <M newbold> לַמְ֒נַצֵּֽחַ <M reg>
<M e>a psalm by the sons of Korach.
<M h> לִבְ֒נֵי קֹֽרַח מִזְמוֹר:
<M e>Hear this all peoples,
<M h> שִׁמְ֒עוּ זֹאת כָּל-הָעַמִּים
<M e>listen all inhabitants of the decaying world!
<M h> הַאֲזִֽינוּ כָּל יֽשְׁ֒בֵי חָֽלֶד:
<M e>Sons of Adam and sons of men,<M tnt>
<M h> גַּם בְּנֵי אָדָם גַּם בְּנֵי אִישׁ
<M e>rich and poor together.
<M h> יַֽחַד עָשִׁיר וְאֶבְיוֹן:
<M e>My mouth shall speak wisdom,
<M h> פִּי יְדַבֵּר חָכְמוֹת
<xx><M tex><M e>and the meditation of my heart
<M h> וְהָגוּת לִבִּי
<M e>shall be of understanding.
<M h> תְבוּנוֹת:
<M e>I will incline my ear to a parable,
<M h> אַטֶּה לְמָשָׁל אָזְנִי
<M e>I will begin to solve,
<M h> אֶפְתַּח
<M e>to the accompaniment of a harp,
<M h> בְּכִנּוֹר
<M e>my riddle.
<M h> חִידָתִי:
<M e>Why should I fear in the days of evil?
<M h> לָֽמָּה אִירָא בִּֽימֵי רָע
<M e>The iniquity I trod upon<M tnt> surrounds me.
<M h> עֲוֹן עֲקֵבַי יְסוּבֵּֽנִי:
<M e>Those who trust in their wealth
<M h> הַבֹּטְ֒חִים עַל חֵילָם
<M e>and take pride in their great riches.<M tnt>
<M h> וּבְ֒רֹב עָשְׁרָם יִתְהַלָּֽלוּ:
<M e>A man will not redeem his brother
<M h> אָח לֺא פָדֹה יִפְדֶּה אִישׁ
<M e>neither can he give to God his ransom.<M tnt>
<M h> לֺא יִתֵּן לֵאלֺהִים כָּפְרוֹ:
<M e>The redemption of their soul is too costly
<M h> וְיֵקַר פִּדְיוֹן נַפְשָׁם
<M e>and it shall cease<M tnt> to be forever.
<M h> וְחָדַל לְעוֹלָם:
<M e>Shall he then live forever,
<M h> וִיחִי עוֹד לָנֶֽצַח
<M e>shall he never see the grave?
<M h> לֺא יִרְאֶה הַשָּֽׁחַת:
<M e>For he sees that wise men die,
<M h> כִּי יִרְאֶה חֲכָמִים יָמֽוּתוּ
<M e>the fools and senseless perish equally<M tnt>
<M h> יַֽחַד כְּסִיל וָבַֽעַר יֹאבֵֽדוּ
<xx><M tex><M e>and leave their wealth to others.
<M h> וְעָזְ֒בוּ לַאֲחֵרִים חֵילָם:
<M e>Their inner<M tnt> thoughts are
<M h> קִרְבָּם
<M e>that their houses [will last] forever,
<M h> בָּתֵּֽימוֹ לְעוֹלָם
<M e>their homes for generation after generation;
<M h> מִשְׁכְּ֒נֹתָם לְדוֹר וָדֹר
<M e>(for) they have proclaimed<M tnt> their names
<M h> קָרְ֒אוּ בִשְׁמוֹתָם
<M e>throughout the lands.
<M h> עֲלֵי אֲדָמוֹת:
<M e>But man does not endure in his splendor,
<M h> וְאָדָם בִּיקָר בַּל-יָלִין
<M e>he is likened to the silenced animals.
<M h> נִמְשַׁל כַּבְּ֒הֵמוֹת נִדְמוּ:
<M e>This is their way---
<M h> זֶה דַרְכָּם
<M e>their folly remains with them,
<M h> כֶּֽסֶל לָֽמוֹ
<M e>and [yet] their descendants
<M h> וְאַחֲרֵיהֶם
<M e>take pleasure in their speech, <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> בְּפִיהֶם יִרְצוּ סֶֽלָה:
<M e>Like sheep---they are destined for the grave;
<M h> כַּצֹּאן לִשְׁ֒אוֹל שַׁתּוּ
<M e>death shall be their shepherd,
<M h> מָֽוֶת יִרְעֵם
<M e>and the upright shall dominate them
<M h> וַיִּרְדּוּ בָם יְשָׁרִים
<M e>at morning,
<M h> לַבֹּֽקֶר
<M e>their form will be consumed in the grave;
<M h> וְצוּרָם לְבַלּוֹת שְׁאוֹל
<M e>[it will not remain] their dwelling-place.
<M h> מִזְּ֒בֻל לוֹ:
<M e>But God will redeem my soul
<M h> אַךְ-אֱלֺהִים יִפְדֶּה נַפְשִׁי
<M e>from the [grasp of] the grave,
<M h> מִיַּד שְׁאוֹל
<M e>for He will take me [to Himself] <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> כִּי יִקָּחֵֽנִי סֶֽלָה:
<M e>Fear not when a man grows rich,
<M h> אַל-תִּירָא כִּי-יַעֲשִׁר אִישׁ
<M e>when the glory of his house is increased.
<M h> כִּי-יִרְבֶּה כְּבוֹד בֵּיתוֹ:
<xx><M tex><M e>For when he dies, he shall carry nothing away,
<M h> כִּי לֺא בְמוֹתוֹ יִקַּח הַכֹּל
<M e>his glory will not descend after him.
<M h> לֺא-יֵרֵד אַחֲרָיו כְּבוֹדוֹ:
<M e>Because while he lived, he blessed his soul.
<M h> כִּי-נַפְשׁוֹ בְּחַיָּיו יְבָרֵךְ
<M e>(saying): they will praise you
<M h> וְיוֹדֻֽךָ
<M e>because you have done well for yourself.
<M h> כִּי-תֵיטִיב לָךְ:
<M e>He will join the generation of his fathers,
<M h> תָּבוֹא עַד-דּוֹר אֲבוֹתָיו
<M e>they shall not see light, for all eternity.
<M h> עַד-נֵֽצַח לֺא יִרְאוּ אוֹר:
<M e>Man with [all] his splendor,
<M h> <M chaz> אָדָם בִּיקָר
<M e>[but] without understanding<M tnt>
<M h> וְלֺא-יָבִין
<M e>is likened to the silenced animals.
<M h> נִמְשַׁל כַּבְּ֒הֵמוֹת נִדְמוּ:
<M in>(Mourner’s Kaddish, p. 000.)<FC>

<M in>On weekdays when </i>Tachanun<i> is not said,<FC>
the following is said in the house of a mourner.<FC>
<M t2>A <i>Michtam</i><M tnt> of David.
<M h> מִכְתָּם לְדָוִד
<M e>Preserve me, Almighty,
<M h> שָׁמְרֵֽנִי אֵל
<M e>for I have taken refuge in You.
<M h> כִּי-חָסִֽיתִי בָךְ:
<M e>You said to Adonoy,
<M h> אָמַֽרְתְּ לַיהֺוָה
<M e>"You are my Master,
<M h> אֲדֹנָי אָֽתָּה
<M e>I have no well-being without You."<M tnt>
<M h> טוֹבָתִי בַּל-עָלֶֽיךָ:
<xx><M tex><M e>Due to the holy that are in the earth,<M tnt>
<M h> לִקְדוֹשִׁים אֲשֶׁר-בָּאָֽרֶץ הֵֽמָּה
<M e>and the mighty,
<M h> וְאַדִּירֵי
<M e>are all my desires [fulfilled].
<M h> כָּל-חֶפְצִי-בָם:
<M e>Let their sufferings multiply,

<M e>nor carry their names

<M e>upon my lips.

<M h> וְכוֹסִי

<M e>are in pleasant places;
<M h> בַּנְּעִמִים
<M e>a beautiful inheritance is mine.
<M h> אַף-נַחֲלָת שָׁפְרָה עָלָי:
<M e>I will bless Adonoy
<M h> אֲבָרֵךְ אֶת-יְהֺוָה

<M e>even for the nights

<M h> כִּי מִימִינִי

<M h> לָכֵן שָׂמַח לִבִּי

<M h> וַיָּֽגֶל כְּבוֹדִי

<M h> אַף-בְּשָׂרִי יִשְׁכֹּן לָבֶֽטַח:

<M t1>Hope to Adonoy;

<M h> וְקַוּה אֶל יְהֹוָה:

<M e>for there is none beside You

<M h> כִּי מִי אֱלוֹהַּ מִבַּלְעֲדֵי יְהֹוָה
<M e>and who is a stronghold beside our God.

<M t1>There is none like our God.

<M h> מִי כְמַלְכֵּנוּ.

<M e>the incenese offering.
<M h> אֶת קְטֹרֶת הַסַּמִּים:
<M tex><M t1>The composition of the incense consisted of
<M h> פִּטּוּם הַקְּ֒טֺרֶת
<M e>balm, onycha,
<M h> הַצֳּרִי וְהַצִּפֹּרֶן
<M e>galbanum, and frankincense---
<M h> הַחֶלְ֒בְּנָה וְהַלְּבוֹנָה
<M e>by weight, seventy <I>maneh</I> of each;
<M h> מִשְׁקַל שִׁבְעִים שִׁבְעִים מָנָה.
<M e>myrrh, cassia,
<M h> מוֹר וּקְ֒צִיעָה
<M e>spikenard and saffron
<M h> שִׁבֹּלֶת נֵרְדְּ וְכַרְכֹּם
<M e>by weight---
<M h> מִשְׁקַל
<M e>sixteen <I>maneh</I> of each;
<M h> שִׁשָּׁה עָשָׂר שִׁשָּׁה עָשָׂר מָנֶה.
<M e>twelve <I>maneh</I> of costus,
<M h> הַקּשְׁטְ שְׁנֵים עָשָׂר
<M e>three <I>maneh</I> of aromatic bark,
<M h> וְקִלּוּפָה שְׁלֹשָׁה
<M e>and nine <I>maneh</I> of cinnamon.
<M h> וְקִנָּמוֹן תִּשְׁעָה.
<M es>[Also used in compounding the incense were:]
<M h>
<M e>Nine <I>kabin</I> of Carshina lye,
<M h> בֹּרִית כַּרְשִׁינָה תִּשְׁעָה קַבִּין.
<M e>Cyprus wine [measuring]
<M h> יֵין קַפְרִיסִין
<M e>three <I>s’in</I> and three <I>kabin</I>---
<M h> סְאִין תְּלָתָא וְקַבִּין תְּלָתָא.
<M e>if he had no Cyprus wine,
<M h> וְאִם אֵין לוֹ יֵין קַפְרִיסִין
<M e>he could used strong white wine---
<M h> מֵבִיא חֲמַר חִוּרְיָן עַתִּיק.

<M h> מֶלַח סְדוֹמִית רֹבַע הַקָב.

<M h> מַעֲלֶה עָשָׁן כָּל שֶׁהוּא.
<M e>Rabbi Nosson of Babylonia says,
<M h> רַבִּי נָתָן הַבַּבְלִי אוֹמֵר

<M h> אַף כִּפַּת הַיַּרְדֵּן כָּל שֶׁהוּא.

<M h> וְאִם נָתַן בָּהּ דְּבַשׁ פְּסָלָהּ
<M e>and if one omitted any of its spices
<M h> וְאִם חִסַּר אַחַת מִכָּל סַמָּנֶיהָ
<M e>he was liable to the death penalty."
<M h> חַיָּב מִיתָה:
<M t1>Rabbi Shimon ben Gamliel says:
<M h> רַבָּן שִׁמְעוֹן בֶּן גַּמְלִיאֵל אוֹמֵר
<M e>"The balm is nothing but sap
<M h> הַצֳּרִי אֵינוֹ אֶלָּא שְׂרָף
<M e>which drips from the balsam tree.
<M h> הַנּוֹטֵף מֵעֲצֵי הַקְּ֒טָף.
<xx><M tex><M e>Why was Carshina lye used?
<M h> בֹּרִית כַּרְשִׁינָה לָמָּה הִיא בָאָה
<M e>To refine the onycha
<M h> כְּדֵי לְיַפּוֹת בָּהּ אֶת הַצִּפֹּרֶן
<M e>in order to make it pleasant.
<M h> כְּדֵי שֶׁתְּ֒הֵא נָאָה.
<M e>Why was Cyprus wine used?
<M h> יֵין קַפְרִיסִין לָמָּה הוּא בָא
<M e>The onycha was soaked in it
<M h> כְּדֵי לִשְׁרוֹת בּוֹ אֶת הַצִּפֹּרֶן
<M e>to give it a pungent odor.
<M h> כְּדֵי שֶׁתְּ֒הֵא עַזָּה.
<M e>Though the water of Raglayim
<M h> וַהֲלֹא מֵי רַגְלַיִם
<M e>was well suited for that purpose,
<M h> יָפִין לָהּ

<M h> אֶלָּא שֶׁאֵין מַכְנִיסִין

<M h> מֵי רַגְלַיִם בַּמִּקְדָּשׁ
<M e>because it would be disrespectful.
<M h> מִפְּ֒נֵי הַכָּבוֹד:

<M t1>Rabbi Eliezer said
<M h> אָמַר רַבִּי אֶלְעָזָר

<M e>"the disciples of the wise
<M h> תַּלְמִידֵי חֲכָמִים
<M e>increase peace in the world,
<M h> מַרְבִּים שָׁלוֹם בָּעוֹלָם.

<M h> לִמּוּדֵי יְהֹוָה
<M e>and great will be the peace of your children.’
<M h> וְרַב שְׁלוֹם בָּנָֽיךְ:

<@02>Aleinu
<@02>עלינו
<M ex><EM><EN><i>Kol Bo</i> writes that Joshua authored this prayer when he captured Jericho. Taken from the Musaf service of Rosh Hashana, it serves as the closing prayer of all the daily services. As ruled by <i>Tur</i> (<i>Orach Chaim</i> 133), it is said while standing.<FL>
<M t1>It is our obligation to praise
<M h> <M newbold> עָלֵֽינוּ <M reg> לְשַׁבֵּֽחַ
<M e>the Master of all,
<M h> לַאֲדוֹן הַכֹּל
<M e>to ascribe greatness
<M h> לָתֵת גְּדֻלָּה
<M e>to the Creator of the [world in the] beginning:
<M h> לְיוֹצֵר בְּרֵאשִׁית
<M e>that He has not made us
<M h> שֶׁלֺּא עָשָֽׂנוּ
<M e>like the nations of the lands,
<M h> כְּגוֹיֵי הָאֲרָצוֹת
<M e>and has not positioned us
<M h> וְלֺא שָׂמָֽנוּ
<M e>like the families of the earth;
<M h> כְּמִשְׁפְּחוֹת הָאֲדָמָה
<M e>that He has not assigned
<M h> שֶׁלֺּא שָׂם
<M e>our portion like theirs,
<M h> חֶלְקֵֽנוּ כָּהֶם
<M e>nor our lot like that of all their multitudes.
<M h> וְגוֹרָלֵֽנוּ כְּכָל הֲמוֹנָם:
<M e>For they prostrate themselves
<M h> שֶׁהֵם מִשְׁתַּחֲוִים
<M e>to vanity and nothingness,
<M h> לָהֶֽבֶל וָרִיק
<M e>and pray to a god that cannot deliver.
<M h> וּמִתְפַּלְּ֒לִים אֶל אֵל לֹא יוֹשִֽׁיעַ,
<M e>But we bow, prostrate ourselves,
<M h> וַאֲנַֽחְנוּ כּוֹרְ֒עִים וּמִשְׁתַּחֲוִים
<M e>and offer thanks
<M h> וּמוֹדִים
<M e>before the Supreme King of Kings,
<M h> לִפְ֒נֵי מֶֽלֶךְ מַלְ֒כֵי הַמְּ֒לָכִים
<M e>the Holy One blessed is He,
<M h> הַקָּדוֹשׁ בָּרוּךְ הוּא,
<xx><M tex><M e>Who spreads the heavens,
<M h> שֶׁהוּא נוֹטֶה שָׁמַֽיִם
<M e>and establishes the earth,
<M h> וְיוֹסֵד אָֽרֶץ,
<M e>and the seat of His glory is in heaven above,
<M h> וּמוֹשַׁב יְקָרוֹ בַּשָּׁמַֽיִם מִמַּֽעַל,
<M e>and the abode of His invincible might
<M h> וּשְׁ֒כִינַת עֻזּוֹ
<M e>is in the loftiest heights.
<M h> בְּגָבְ֒הֵי מְרוֹמִים,
<M e>He is our God, there is nothing else.
<M h> הוּא אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ אֵין עוֹד,
<M e>Our King is true,
<M h> אֱמֶת מַלְכֵּֽנוּ
<M e>all else is insignificant,
<M h> אֶֽפֶס זוּלָתוֹ
<M e>as it is written in His Torah:
<M h> כַּכָּתוּב בְּתוֹרָתוֹ
<M e>"And You shall know this day
<M h> וְיָדַעְתָּ הַיּוֹם
<M e>and take into Your heart
<M h> וַהֲשֵׁבֹתָ אֶל לְבָבֶֽךָ
<M e>that Adonoy is God
<M h> כִּי יְהֹוָה הוּא הָאֱלֺהִים
<M e>in the heavens above
<M h> בַּשָּׁמַֽיִם מִמַּֽעַל
<M e>and upon the earth below;
<M h> וְעַל הָאָֽרֶץ מִתָּֽחַת
<M e>there is nothing else."<M tnt>
<M h> אֵין עוֹד:
<M t1>We therefore put our hope in You,
<M h> עַל כֵּן נְקַוּה לְךָ
<M e>Adonoy our God,
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>to soon behold the glory of Your might

<M e>in banishing idolatry from the earth,
<M h> לְהַעֲבִיר גִּלּוּלִים מִן הָאָֽרֶץ
<M e>and the false gods will be utterly exterminated
<M h> וְהָאֱלִילִים כָּרוֹת יִכָּרֵתוּן
<M e>to perfect the world
<M h> לְתַקֵּן עוֹלָם
<M e>as the kingdom of Shadai.<M tnt>
<M h> בְּמַלְ֒כוּת שַׁדַּי
<M e>And all mankind will invoke Your Name,
<M h> וְכָל בְּנֵי בָשָׂר יִקְרְאוּ בִשְׁ֒מֶֽךָ,
<M e>to turn back to You,
<M h> לְהַפְנוֹת אֵלֶֽיךָ
<M e>all the wicked of the earth.
<M h> כָּל רִשְׁ֒עֵי אָֽרֶץ,
<xx><M tex><M e>They will realize and know,
<M h> יַכִּֽירוּ וְיֵדְ֒עוּ
<M e>all the inhabitants of the world,
<M h> כָּל יוֹשְׁ֒בֵי תֵבֵל
<M e>that to You, every knee must bend,
<M h> כִּי לְךָ תִכְרַע כָּל בֶּֽרֶךְ
<M e>every tongue must swear [allegiance to You].
<M h> תִּשָּׁבַע כָּל לָשׁוֹן:
<M e>Before You, Adonoy, our God,
<M h> לְפָנֶֽיךָ יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>they will bow and prostrate themselves,
<M h> יִכְרְעוּ וְיִפֹּֽלוּ,
<M e>and to the glory of Your Name give honor.
<M h> וְלִכְ֒בוֹד שִׁמְ֒ךָ יְקָר יִתֵּֽנוּ,
<M e>And they will all accept [upon themselves]
<M h> וִיקַבְּ֒לוּ כֻלָּם
<M e>the yoke of Your kingdom,
<M h> אֶת עֹל מַלְ֒כוּתֶֽךָ,
<M e>and You will reign over them, soon,
<M h> וְתִמְלֺךְ עֲלֵיהֶם מְהֵרָה
<M e>forever and ever.
<M h> לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד,
<M e>For the kingdom is Yours,
<M h> כִּי הַמַּלְ֒כוּת שֶׁלְּ֒ךָ הִיא
<M e>and to all eternity You will reign in glory,
<M h> וּלְ֒עֽוֹלְ֒מֵי עַד תִּמְלוֹךְ בְּכָבוֹד,
<M e>as it is written in Your Torah:
<M h> כַּכָּתוּב בְּתוֹרָתֶֽךָ
<M e>"Adonoy will reign forever and ever."<M tnt>
<M h> יְהֹוָה יִמְלֺךְ לְעֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M e>And it is said:
<M h> <M chaz> וְנֶאֱמַר
<M e>"And Adonoy will be King
<M h> וְהָיָה יְהֹוָה לְמֶֽלֶךְ
<M e>over the whole earth;
<M h> עַל כָּל הָאָֽרֶץ

<M e>and His Name One."<M tnt>
<M h> וּשְׁ֒מוֹ אֶחָד:

<M e>for God is with us.

<M e>To Your old age I am [with You],

<M e>I have made You, and I will carry You,

<M e>I will sustain You and save You.

<@02>Mourner’s Kaddish
<@02>קדיש יתום
<M ex><EM><EN>Although the Kaddish contains no reference to the dead, it has been recited by mourners for many centuries. The tradition of the mourner’s Kaddish began with the following incident: Once, while walking, Rabbi Akiva met a man who had died some time before and was suffering the torments of Purgatory. He pleaded with Rabbi Akiva to go to his home town and teach his son to recite the Kaddish and Borechu, for this would save him from the terrible punishments. Rabbi Akiva and his Court then instituted the practice of mourners reciting the Kaddish, for until then it had been limited to the Chazzan’s reciting it only after the services or after a sermon (See <i>Tana D’vei Eliyahu Zuta,</i> 17: <i>Zohar Parshas Noach</i>).<FL>
<M t1>Exalted and sanctified be His great Name
<M h> יִתְגַּדֵּל וְיִתְקַדֵּשׁ שְׁמֵהּ רַבָּא <FL>
<M e>in the world which He created
<M h> בְּעָלְ֒מָא דִּי בְרָא <FL>
<M e>according to His will
<M h> כִרְ֒עוּתֵהּ <FL>
<M e>and may He rule His kingdom
<M h> וְיַמְלִיךְ מַלְ֒כוּתֵהּ <FL>
<M e>bring forth His redemption
<M h> וְיַצְמַח פּוּרְ֒קָנֵהּ <FL>
<M e>and hasten the coming if His Messiah
<M h> וִיקָרֵב )קֵץ( מְשִׁיחֵהּ <FL>
<M e>in your lifetime and in your days,
<M h> בְּחַיֵּיכוֹן וּבְ֒יוֹמֵיכוֹן <FL>
<M e>and in the lifetime
<M h> וּבְ֒חַיֵּי
<M e>of the entire House of Israel,
<M h> דְכָל בֵּית יִשְׂרָאֵל, <FL>
<M e>speedily and in the near future---
<M h> בַּעֲגָלָא וּבִזְ֒מַן קָרִיב <FL>
<M e>and say Amein.
<M h> וְאִמְ֒רוּ אָמֵן: <FL>
<xx><M tex><M e>May His great Name be blessed

<@02>Six Verses of Remembrance
<@02>שש זכירות
<M ex><EM><EN>According to some authorities it is a <i>mitzvah</i> to recite these six verses of remembrance every day. Those who do so are assured of a share in the World-to-Come.<FL>
<M t1><i>The Exodus</i>
<M h> זכירת יציאת מצרים
<M t2>.<NS>.<NS>.<NS>in order that you remember the day
<M h> לְמַֽעַן תִּזְכֹּר אֶת יוֹם
<M e>you came out of the land of Egypt
<M h> צֵאתְ֒ךָ מֵאֶֽרֶץ מִצְרַֽיִם
<M e>all the days of your life.<M tnt>
<M h> כֹּל יְמֵי חַיֶּֽיךָ:
<M t1><i>The Revelation at Mount Sinai</i>
<M h> זכירת מעמד הר סיני
<M t2>Only beware,
<M h> רַק הִשָּֽׁמֶר לְךָ
<M e>and guard you soul diligently,
<M h> וּשְׁמֹר נַפְשְׁ֒ךָ מְאֹד
<M e>lest you forget the things
<M h> פֶּן תִּשְׁכַּח אֶת הַדְּ֒בָרִים
<M e>which your eyes have seen;
<M h> אֲשֶׁר רָאוּ עֵינֶֽיךָ
<M e>lest they be removed from your heart
<M h> וּפֶן יָסֽוּרוּ מִלְּ֒בָבְ֒ךָ
<M e>all the days of your life;
<M h> כֹּל יְמֵי חַיֶּֽיךָ,
<M e>and make them known to your children
<M h> וְהוֹדַעְתָּם לְבָנֶֽיךָ
<M e>and to your children’s children.
<M h> וְלִבְנֵי בָנֶֽיךָ:
<M e>[That what you witnessed] the day you stood
<M h> יוֹם אֲשֶׁר עָמַֽדְתָּ
<M e>before Adonoy your God at Chorev.<M tnt>
<M h> לִפְ֒נֵי יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֶֽיךָ בְּחֹרֵב:
<xx><M tex><M t1><i>The Attack of Amalek</i>
<M h> <M reg> זכירת מחיית עמלק
<M t2>Remember
<M h> <M reg> זָכוֹר
<M e>what Amalek did to you
<M h> אֵת אֲשֶׁר עָשָׂה לְךָ עֲמָלֵק,
<M e>on the way, as you came out of Egypt!
<M h> בַּדֶּֽרֶךְ בְּצֵאתְ֒כֶם מִמִּצְרָֽיִם:
<M e>How he encountered you on the way,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קָרְ֒ךָ בַּדֶּֽרֶךְ
<M e>and he cut off all the weak ones
<M h> וַיְ֒זַנֵּב בְּךָ כָּל הַנֶּחֱשָׁלִים
<M e>[who were straggling] behind you,
<M h> אַחֲרֶֽיךָ,
<M e>when you were weary and exhausted;
<M h> וְאַתָּה עָיֵף וְיָגֵֽעַ,
<M e>and he did not fear God.<M tnt>
<M h> וְלֺא יָרֵא אֱלֺהִים:
<M e>When Adonoy, Your God, will relieve you
<M h> וְהָיָה בְּהָנִֽיחַ יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֶֽיךָ לְךָ,
<M e>from all your enemies around you,
<M h> מִכָּל אֹיְ֒בֶֽיךָ מִסָּבִיב,
<M e>in the land which Adonoy, your God,
<M h> בָּאָֽרֶץ אֲשֶׁר יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֶֽיךָ
<M e>gives you as a possession to inherit;
<M h> נֹתֵן לְךָ נַחֲלָה לְרִשְׁתָּהּ,
<M e>you shall eradicate the memory of Amalek
<M h> תִּמְחֶה אֶת זֵֽכֶר עֲמָלֵק
<M e>from beneath the heavens. Do not forget.<M tnt>
<M h> מִתַּחַת הַשָּׁמָֽיִם, לֺא תִּשְׁכָּח:
<M t1><i>The Sin of the Golden Calf</i>
<M h> <M reg> זכירת מעשה העגל
<M t2>Remember, do not forget,
<M h> <M reg> זְכֹר אַל תִּשְׁכַּח
<M e>how you provoked
<M h> אֵת אֲשֶׁר הִקְצַֽפְתָּ

<M h> אֶת יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֶֽיךָ בַּמִּדְבָּר:

<M t1><i>The Sabbath</i>
<M h> <M reg> זכירת השבת
<M t2>Remember the Sabbath day to sanctify it.<M tnt>
<M h> <M reg> זָכוֹר אֶת יוֹם הַשַּׁבָּת לְקַדְּ֒שׁוֹ:
<@02>Thirteen Principles of Faith
<@02>שלש עשרה עיקרים
<M ex><EM><EN>Many great medieval scholars formulated articles of faith, among them Rav Saadya Gaon, Rav Yehuda Halevi, Rabbeinu Bachya. Maimonides, the foremost of them all, formulated thirteen principles that have attained wide recognition and enduring fame.<M tnt><FL>
<EM><EN>The thirteen principles fall into three groups: The first five declare the existence of God as the Creator, One, incorporeal, eternal and alone worthy of man’s worship.<FL>
<EM><EN>The next four deal with the Divine revelation of the Torah, the authenticity of prophecy, particularly that of Moses, and the immutability of the Torah.<FL>
<EM><EN>The last four deal with God in history, reward and punishment, belief in the coming of Messiah, and the resurrection of the dead.<FL>
<M t1>1. I believe with complete faith
<M h> <M newbold> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין <M reg> בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<xx><M tex><M e>is the Creator and Guide
<M h> הוּא בוֹרֵא וּמַנְהִיג
<M e>of all created things,
<M h> לְכָל הַבְּ֒רוּאִים
<M e>and He alone has made, does make,
<M h> וְהוּא לְבַדּוֹ עָשָׂה וְעוֹשֶׂה
<M e>and will make all things.
<M h> וְיַעֲשֶׂה לְכָל הַמַּעֲשִׂים:
<M t2>2. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>is unique,
<M h> הוּא יָחִיד
<M e>and there is no uniqueness like His
<M h> וְאֵין יְחִידוּת כָּמֽוֹהוּ
<M e>in any manner;
<M h> בְּשׁוּם פָּנִים
<M e>and that He alone is our God,
<M h> וְהוּא לְבַדּוֹ אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>Who was, is, and will ever be.
<M h> הָיָה הֹוֶה וְיִהְיֶה:
<M t2>3. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>is not corporeal,
<M h> אֵינוֹ גוּף
<M e>and that He is beyond all corporeal concepts,
<M h> וְלֺא יַשִּׂיגֽוּהוּ מַשִּׂיגֵי הַגּוּף
<M e>and there is nothing at all comparable to Him.
<M h> וְאֵין לוֹ שׁוּם דִּמְיוֹן כְּלָל:
<M t2>4. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>is First and Last.
<M h> הוּא רִאשׁוֹן וְהוּא אַחֲרוֹן:
<M t2>5. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>is the only One to Whom it is proper to pray,
<M h> לוֹ לְבַדּוֹ רָאוּי לְהִתְפַּלֵּל
<M e>and to no being beside Him
<M h> וְאֵין לְזוּלָתוֹ
<M e>is it proper to pray.
<M h> רָאוּי לְהִתְפַּלֵּל:
<M tex><M t2>6. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that all the words of the prophets are true.
<M h> שֶׁכָּל דִּבְ֒רֵי נְבִיאִים אֱמֶת:
<M t2>7. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the prophecy of our teacher, Moses,
<M h> שֶׁנְּ֒בוּאַת משֶׁה רַבֵּֽנוּ
<M e>may he rest in peace,
<M h> עָלָיו הַשָּׁלוֹם
<M e>was true,
<M h> הָיְ֒תָה אֲמִתִּית
<M e>and that he was the father of all prophets,
<M h> וְשֶׁהוּא הָיָה אָב לַנְּ֒בִיאִים
<M e>---of those who preceded him,
<M h> לַקּוֹדְ֒מִים לְפָנָיו
<M e>and of those who followed him.
<M h> וְלַבָּאִים אַחֲרָיו:
<M t2>8. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the entire Torah
<M h> שֶׁכָּל הַתּוֹרָה
<M e>which is now in our possession,
<M h> הַמְּ֒צוּיָה עַתָּה בְיָדֵֽינוּ
<M e>is the very one that was given
<M h> הִיא הַנְּ֒תוּנָה
<M e>to our teacher Moses, may he rest in peace.
<M h> לְמשֶׁה רַבֵּֽנוּ עָלָיו הַשָּׁלוֹם:
<M t2>9. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that this Torah will not be exchanged,
<M h> שֶׁזֹּאת הַתּוֹרָה לֺא תְהֵא מֻחְלֶֽפֶת
<M e>and that no additional Torah
<M h> וְלֺא תְהֵא תוֹרָה אַחֶֽרֶת
<M e>[will be given] by the Creator,
<M h> מֵאֵת הַבּוֹרֵא
<M e>blessed is His Name.
<M h> יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ:
<M t2>10. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>knows all the deeds of men
<M h> יוֹדֵֽעַ כָּל מַעֲשֵׂה בְנֵי אָדָם
<M e>and all their thoughts,
<M h> וְכָל מַחְשְׁ֒בוֹתָם
<M e>as it is said,<M tnt>
<M h> שֶׁנֶּאֱמַר
<xx><M tex><M e>"He Who forms all their hearts as one,
<M h> הַיֹּצֵר יַֽחַד לִבָּם
<M e>Who comprehends all their deeds."
<M h> הַמֵּבִין אֶל כָּל מַעֲשֵׂיהֶם:
<M t2>11. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> שֶׁהַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>rewards those who keep His commandments,
<M h> גּוֹמֵל טוֹב לְשׁוֹמְ֒רֵי מִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and punishes those
<M h> וּמַעֲנִישׁ
<M e>who transgress His commandments.
<M h> לְעוֹבְ֒רֵי מִצְוֹתָיו:
<M t2>12. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>in the coming of the Messiah
<M h> בְּבִיאַת הַמָּשִֽׁיחַ
<M e>and even though he may tarry,
<M h> וְאַף עַל פִּי שֶׁיִּתְמַהְמֵֽהַּ
<M e>nevertheless,
<M h> עִם כָּל זֶה
<M e>I yearn every day for his coming.
<M h> אֲחַכֶּה לּוֹ בְּכָל יוֹם שֶׁיָּבוֹא:
<M t2>13. I believe with complete faith
<M h> אֲנִי מַאֲמִין בֶּאֱמוּנָה שְׁלֵמָה
<M e>that there will be a resurrection of the dead
<M h> שֶׁתִּהְיֶה תְּחִיַּת הַמֵּתִים
<M e>at a time that pleases
<M h> בְּעֵת שֶׁיַּעֲלֶה רָצוֹן
<M e>the Creator, blessed is His Name,
<M h> מֵאֵת הַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ שְׁמוֹ
<M e>and His Name will be exalted forever
<M h> וְיִתְעַלֶּה זִכְרוֹ לָעַד
<M e>and to all eternity.
<M h> וּלְ֒נֵֽצַח נְצָחִים:
<M long> לִישׁוּעָתְ֒ךָ קִוּיתִי יְהֹוָה, קִוּיתִי יְהֹוָה לִישׁוּעָתְ֒ךָ, יְהֹוָה לִישׁוּעָתְ֒ךָ קִוּיתִי: לְפֻרְקָנָךְ סַבְּ֒רִית יְהֹוָה, סַבְּ֒רִית יְהֹוָה לְפֻרְקָנָךְ, יְהֹוָה לְפֻרְקָנָךְ סַבָּרִית: <FC>
<@02>The Chapter of Reverence for God
<@02>שיר הכבוד
<M in>Deuteronomy 10:12-11:9<FC>
<M h> <M long> וְעַתָּה‘ יִשְׂרָאֵל ֚מָה יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ שֺׁאֵל מֵֽעִמָּ֑ךְ כִּ֣י אִם-֠לְיִרְאָ֠ה אֶת-יְהֹוָ’ה אֱלֹהֶ”יךָ לָלֶ֤כֶת בְּכָל-דְּרָכָיו‘ וּלְ֒אַֽהֲבָ֣ה אֺתוֹ וְלַֽעֲבֺד‘
