אֶת-הַגְּ֒דֺלֹ֤ת וְאֶת-הַנּֽוֹרָאֺת‘ הָאֵלֶּה אֲשֶׁ֥ר רָאוּ עֵינֶֽיךָ: בְּשִׁבְעִ֣ים נֶפֶשׁ יָֽרְ֒ד֥וּ אֲבֺתֶיךָ מִצְרָ֑יְמָה וְעַתָּה שָֽׂמְ֒ךָ‘ יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ כְּכֽוֹכְ֒בֵ֥י הַשָּׁמַיִם לָרֺֽב: וְאָ֣הַבְתָּ אֵת יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶ֑יךָ וְשָֽׁמַרְתָּ֣ מִשְׁמַרְתּוֹ וְחֻקֺּתָ֧יו וּמִשְׁפָּטָ…יו וּמִצְוֹתָיו כָּל-הַיָּמִֽים: וִֽידַעְתֶּם הַיּוֹם֒ כִּ֣י <NS> | לֹ֣א אֶת-בְּנֵיכֶם אֲשֶׁ֤ר לֹא-יָֽדְ֒עוּ‘ וַֽאֲשֶׁ֣ר לֹֽא-רָאוּ אֶת-מוּסַר יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹֽהֵיכֶ֑ם אֶת-גָּדְלוֹ אֶת-יָדוֹ‘ הַֽחֲזָקָה וּזְ֒רֺעוֹ הַנְּ֒טוּיָֽה: וְאֶת-אֺֽתֺתָיו‘ וְאֶת-מַֽעֲשָׂיו אֲשֶׁ֥ר עָשָׂה בְּת֣וֹךְ מִצְרָ֑יִם לְפַרְעֺ֥ה מֶֽלֶךְ-מִצְרַיִם וּלְ֒כָל-אַרְצֽוֹ: וַֽאֲשֶׁ֣ר עָשָׂה— לְחֵ’יל מִצְרַ”יִם לְסוּסָ֣יו וּלְ֒רִכְבּוֹ אֲשֶׁ’ר הֵצִ”יף אֶת-מֵ֤י יַם-סוּף‘ עַל-פְּנֵיהֶם בְּרָדְ֒פָם אַֽחֲרֵיכֶ֑ם וַיְ֒אַבְּ֒דֵ֣ם יְהֹוָה עַד הַיּ֥וֹם הַזֶּֽה: וַֽאֲשֶׁ֥ר עָשָׂ…ה לָכֶם בַּמִּדְבָּ֑ר עַד-בֺּֽאֲכֶם עַד-הַמָּק֥וֹם הַזֶּֽה: וַֽאֲשֶׁ’ר עָשָׂ”ה לְדָתָ֣ן וְלַֽאֲבִירָם בְּנֵ֣י אֱלִיאָב בֶּן-רְאוּבֵן֒ אֲשֶׁ’ר פָּֽצְ֒תָ֤ה הָאָ’רֶץ‘ אֶת-פִּיהָ וַתִּבְלָעֵ֥ם וְאֶת-בָּֽתֵּיהֶם וְאֶת-אָֽהֳלֵיהֶ֑ם וְאֵ֤ת כָּל-הַיְ֒קוּם‘ אֲשֶׁ֣ר בְּרַגְלֵיהֶם בְּקֶרֶב כָּל-יִשְׂרָאֵֽל: כִּ֤י עֵֽינֵיכֶם‘ הָֽרֺאֺת אֵ…ת כָּל-מַֽעֲשֵׂ֥ה יְהֹוָה הַגָּדֺ֑ל אֲשֶׁר עָשָֽׂה: וּשְׁ֒מַרְתֶּם‘ אֶת-כָּל-הַמִּצְוָה אֲשֶׁ…ר אָֽנֺכִ֥י מְצַוּךָ הַיּ֑וֹם לְמַ֣עַן תֶּֽחֶזְ֒קוּ וּבָאתֶם‘ וִֽירִשְׁתֶּ֣ם אֶת-הָאָרֶץ אֲשֶׁ֥ר אַתֶּ…ם עֺֽבְ֒רִ֥ים שָׁמָּה לְרִשְׁתָּֽהּ: וּלְ֒מַ’עַן תַּֽאֲרִ֤יכוּ יָמִים‘ עַל-הָ֣אֲדָמָה אֲשֶׁר— נִשְׁבַּ’ע יְהֹוָ֧ה לַֽאֲבֺֽתֵיכֶ…ם לָתֵ֥ת לָהֶם וּלְ֒זַרְעָ֑ם אֶ…רֶץ זָבַ֥ת חָלָב וּדְ֒בָֽשׁ:
<M tex><M ex><EM><EN>And now Israel, what does Adonoy, your God, require of you, but to fear Adonoy, your God, to walk in all His ways, and to love Him and to serve Adonoy, your God, with all your heart and with all your soul. To keep the commandments of Adonoy and His decrees, which I command you this day. Behold, the heaven and the highest of heavens belong to Adonoy, your God, the earth and all that is in it. Yet only in your fathers did Adonoy delight, to love them, and He chose their offspring after them, even you among all the peoples as [it is] this day. Circumcise the barrier of your heart, and be stiffnecked no longer. For Adonoy, your God, is God of all powers and the Master of all masters, the Almighty, the Great, the Powerful, the Awesome, Who has no regard for personages and takes no bribes. Who does justice for the orphan and the widow, and loves the stranger, giving him food and clothing. You must love the stranger for you were strangers in the land of Egypt. You must fear Adonoy, your God, serve Him, cleave to Him, and swear by His Name. He is your praise, and He is your God, Who did with you all these great and awesome things that your eyes have seen. With seventy people your fathers descended to Egypt, and now Adonoy, your God, has made you as abundant as the stars of heaven. [Therefore] you shall love Adonoy, your God, and keep His trust, His decrees, His statutes, and His commandments all the days. And you should know this day, that it is not with your children who have not known and who did not experience the chastisement of Adonoy, your God, His mighty hand, and His outstretched arm. His signs and His deeds that He performed in the midst of Egypt, to Pharaoh, the king of Egypt, and to all his land. And what He did to the army of Egypt, to their horses, and to their chariots; how He made the water of the Sea of Reeds drown them as they pursued you, and Adonoy destroyed them to this very day. And what He did for you in the wilderness, until you came into this place. And what He did unto Dathan and Aviram, the sons of Eliav, son of Reuben, when the earth opened her mouth, and swallowed them, and their households, their tents and all the substance that was in their possession in the midst of all Israel. But your eyes have seen all the great deeds of Adonoy, that He performed. You should [therefore] keep all the commandments which I command you this day, so you will be strong, and go in and possess the land, to which you are passing over to possess it. And in order to prolong your days upon the land Adonoy swore to your fathers to give to them and to their offspring; a land flowing with milk and honey.<FL>
<M tex><M in>The following prayer is omitted on Shabbos and Yom Tov<FC>
<M h> <M long> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ יְהֺוָה אֱלֹהַי וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתַי שֶׁתַּחְתּוֹר חֲתִּירָה מִתַּֽחַת כִּסֵּא כְבוֹדֶֽ֒ךָ לְהַחֲזִיר בִּתְ֒שׁוּבָה שְׁלֵמָה לְכָל פּוֹשְׁ֒עֵי עַמְּ֒ךָ בֵּית יִשְׂרָאֵל וּבִכְ֒לָלָם תַּחֲזִירֵֽנִי בִּתְ֒שׁוּבָה שְׁלֵמָה לְפָנֶֽיךָ כִּי יְמִינְ֒ךָ פְשׁוּטָה לְקַבֵּל שָׁבִים וְרוֹצֶה אַתָּה בִּתְ֒שׁוּבָה. אָמֵן, סֶֽלָה:
<M ex><EM><EN>May it be Your will Adonoy, my God, and the God of my fathers, to implant Your love and fear of You in my heart and in the heart of all Israel, Your people, to fear Your Great, Mighty and Awesome Name with all our heart and with all our soul, for You are great and Your Name is awesome. Amein. <i>Selah.</i><FL>
<@02>The Chapter of Repentance
<@02>פרק התשובה
<M in>Deuteronomy 30:1-11<FC>
<M h> <M long> וְהָיָה— כִֽי-יָבֺ’אוּ עָלֶ”יךָ כָּל-הַדְּבָרִ֣ים הָאֵלֶּה הַבְּ֒רָכָה‘ וְהַקְּ֒לָלָה אֲשֶׁ֥ר נָתַתִּי לְפָנֶ֑יךָ וַֽהֲשֵֽׁבֺתָ‘ אֶל-לְבָבֶךָ בְּכָ’ל-הַגּוֹיִם אֲשֶׁ֧ר הִדִּֽיחֲךָ… יְהֹוָ֥ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ שָֽׁמָּה: וְשַׁבְתָּ֞ עַד-יְהֹוָ֤ה אֱלֹהֶ’יךָ‘ וְשָֽׁמַעְתָּ֣ בְקֺלוֹ כְּכֺ…ל אֲשֶׁר-אָֽנֺכִ֥י מְצַוּךָ הַיּ֑וֹם אַתָּ֣ה וּבָנֶיךָ בְּכָל-לְבָֽבְ֒ךָ וּבְ֒כָל-נַפְשֶֽׁךָ: וְשָׁ’ב יְהֹוָ֧ה אֱלֹהֶ…יךָ אֶת-שְׁבֽוּתְ֒ךָ וְרִֽחֲמֶ֑ךָ וְשָׁב וְקִבֶּצְ֒ךָ‘ מִכָּל-הָ֣עַמִּים אֲשֶׁ֧ר הֱפִֽיצְ֒ךָ… יְהֹוָ֥ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ שָֽׁמָּה: אִם-יִֽהְיֶ֥ה נִֽדַּֽחֲךָ בִּקְ֒צֵ֣ה הַשָּׁמָ֑יִם מִשָּׁם יְקַבֶּצְ֒ךָ‘ יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ וּמִשָּׁם יִקָּחֶֽךָ: וֶֽהֱבִֽיאֲךָ֞ יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ אֶל-הָאָ…רֶץ אֲשֶׁר-יָֽרְ֒שׁ֥וּ אֲבֺתֶיךָ וִֽירִשְׁתָּ֑הּ וְהֵיטִֽבְ֒ךָ֥ וְהִרְבְּךָ מֵֽאֲבֺתֶֽיךָ: וּמָ’ל יְהֹוָ֧ה אֱלֹהֶ…יךָ אֶת-לְבָֽבְ֒ךָ וְאֶת-לְבַ֣ב זַרְעֶ֑ךָ לְאַֽהֲבָ֞ה אֶת-יְהֹוָ֧ה אֱלֹהֶ…יךָ בְּכָל-לְבָֽבְ֒ךָ֥ וּבְ֒כָל-נַפְשְׁךָ לְמַ֥עַן חַיֶּֽיךָ: וְנָתַן‘ יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ אֵ֥ת כָּל-הָֽאָלוֹת הָאֵ֑לֶּה עַל-אֺֽיְ֒בֶ֥יךָ וְעַל-שֽׂנְ֒אֶיךָ אֲשֶׁ֥ר רְדָפֽוּךָ: וְאַתָּ֣ה תָשׁוּב וְשָֽׁמַעְתָּ בְּק֣וֹל יְהֹוָ֑ה וְעָשִׂ’יתָ‘ אֶת-כָּל-מִצְוֹתָיו אֲשֶׁ…ר אָֽנֺכִ֥י מְצַוּךָ הַיּֽוֹם: וְהוֹתִֽירְ֒ךָ— יְהֹוָ’ה אֱלֹהֶ”יךָ בְּכֺ֣ל <NS> | מַֽעֲשֵׂ֣ה יָדֶךָ בִּפְ֒רִ’י בִטְנְךָ” וּבִפְ֒רִ֧י בְהֶמְתְּךָ… וּבִפְ֒רִ֥י אַדְ֒מָֽתְ֒ךָ לְטֺבָ֑ה כִּ֣י <NS> | יָשׁ֣וּב יְהֹוָה לָשׂ֤וּשׂ עָלֶ’יךָ‘ לְטוֹב כַּֽאֲשֶׁר-שָׂשׂ עַל-אֲבֺתֶֽיךָ: כִּ֣י תִשְׁמַע בְּקוֹל‘ יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ לִשְׁמֺ֤ר מִצְוֹתָיו‘ וְחֻקֺּתָיו הַכְּ֒תוּבָה בְּסֵ֥פֶר הַתּוֹרָה הַזֶּ֑ה כִּ֤י תָשׁוּב‘ אֶל-יְהֹוָ֣ה אֱלֹהֶיךָ בְּכָל-לְבָֽבְ֒ךָ וּבְ֒כָל-נַפְשֶֽׁךָ:
<M tex><M ex><EM><EN>And it will come to pass when all these things come upon you, the blessing and the curse which I have set before you, that you will take it to heart in the midst of all the nations to which Adonoy, your God, has driven you. Then you will return unto Adonoy, your God, and obey His voice according to everything that I command you this day, you and your children, with all your heart and with all your soul. And then Adonoy, your God, will return your captivity and have compassion upon you; and He will return and gather you from among all the peoples where Adonoy, your God, has scattered you. Even if your scattered ones will be dispersed unto the outermost parts of heaven, from there Adonoy, your God, will gather you, and from there, He will take you. And Adonoy, your God, will bring you into the land which your forefathers possessed, and you will possess it; and He will do good to you and increase you even more than your fathers. Adonoy, your God, will circumcise your heart, and the hearts of your descendants, to love Adonoy, your God, with all your heart and with all your soul, that you may live. Then Adonoy, your God, will set all these curses upon your enemies, and upon those who hate you, who have pursued you. But you will repent and listen to the voice of Adonoy, and perform all His commandments that I command you this day. And Adonoy, your God, will cause you to prosper in all your activities, in the fruit of your womb, in the fruit of your cattle, and the fruit of your soil, for good; for Adonoy will rejoice over you for goodness as He rejoiced over your fathers. For you will then obey the voice of Adonoy, your God, to observe His commandments and His decrees that are written in this Seifer Torah; for you will then return to Adonoy, your God, with all your heart and with all your soul.<FL>
<M in>(The following prayer is not recited on Shabbos and Yom Tov.)<FC>
<M h> <M long> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ יְהֺוָה אֱלֹהַי וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתַי שֶׁתִּטַּע אַהֲבָתְ֒ךָ וְיִרְאָתְ֒ךָ בְּלִבִּי וּבְלֵב כָּל יִשְׂרָאֵל עַמֶּֽךָ לְיִרְאָה אֶת שִׁמְ֒ךָ הַגָּדוֹל הַגִּבוֹר וְהַנּוֹרָא בְּכָל לְבָבֵֽנוּ וּבְ֒כָל נַפְשֵֽׁנוּ, יִרְאַת הָרוֹמְ֒מוּת שֶׁל אֵין סוֹֺף בָּרוּךְ וְיִתעַלֶּה שִׁמְ֒ךָ, כִּי גָדוֹל אַתָּה וְנוֹרָא שְׁמֶֽךָ. אָמֵן, סֶֽלָה:
<M ex><EM><EN>May it be Your will Adonoy, my God, and the God of my fathers, to construct a passage beneath Your Throne of Glory in order to bring back in perfect repentance all the transgressors of Your people, the House of Israel. And among them, bring me back unto You in perfect repentance, for<fj>
<M tex><M ex>Your right hand is outstretched to receive those who repent, for You desire repentance. Amein. <i>Selah.</i><FL>
<@02>The Chapter of Mannah
<@02>תפלת המן
<M in>According to the Jerusalem Talmud, one who recites this Torah chapter every day is assured that he will never lack for food. The prayer preceding the Torah chapter should not be recited on Shabbos or Yom Tov.<FC>
<M h> <M long> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ יְהֺוָה אֱלֹהֵֽינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ שֶׁתַּזְמִין פַּרְנָסָה לְכָל עַמְּ֒ךָ בֵּית יִשְׂרָאֵל וּפַרְנָסַת אַנְ֒שֵׁי בֵיתִי בִּכְ֒לָלָם, בְּנַחַת וְלֹא בְּצַֽעַר, בְּכָבוֹד וְלֹא בְּבִזּוּי, בְּהֶתֵּר וְלֹא בְּאִסּוּר, כְּדֵי שֶׁנּוּכַל לַעֲבֺד עֲבֺדָתֶֽךָ וְלִלְמוֹד תּוֹרָתֶֽךָ, כְּמוֹ שֶׁזַּֽנְּתָּ לַאֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ מָן בַּמִּדְבָּר בְּאֶֽרֶץ צִיָּה וַעֲרָבָה:
<M ex><EM><EN>May it be Your will Adonoy, our God, and God of our fathers, to grant livelihood for all Your people, the House of Israel, and may my livelihood and the livelihood of my household be included among them. May it be granted to us with tranquility and not with suffering, with honor and not with disgrace, legally and not illegally, so that we will be able to serve You and study Your Torah. Grant it to us now as You sustained our ancestors in the wilderness, in a desolate and arid land.<FL>
<M in>Exodus 16:4-36<FC>
<M h> <M long> וַיֺּ֤אמֶר יְהֹוָה‘ אֶל-משֶׁה הִנְ֒נִ’י מַמְטִ֥יר לָכֶ…ם לֶחֶם מִן-הַשָּׁמָ֑יִם וְיָצָ’א הָעָ֤ם וְלָֽקְטוּ‘ דְּבַר-י֣וֹם בְּיוֹמוֹ לְמַ֧עַן אֲנַסֶּ…נוּ הֲיֵלֵ֥ךְ בְּתֽוֹרָתִי אִם-לֹֽא: וְהָיָה‘ בַּיּ֣וֹם הַשִּׁשִּׁי וְהֵכִינוּ אֵ֣ת אֲשֶׁר-יָבִ֑יאוּ וְהָיָ֣ה מִשְׁנֶה עַ֥ל אֲשֶֽׁר-יִלְקְטוּ י֥וֹם <NS> | יֽוֹם: וַיֺּ֤אמֶר משֶׁה‘ וְאַֽהֲרֺן אֶֽל-כָּל-בְּנֵי יִשְׂרָאֵ֑ל עֶרֶב וִֽידַעְתֶּם כִּ֧י יְהֹוָ…ה הוֹצִ֥יא אֶתְ֒כֶם מֵאֶ֥רֶץ מִצְרָֽיִם: וּבֺקֶר וּרְ֒אִיתֶם‘ אֶת-כְּב֣וֹד יְהֹוָה בְּשָׁמְע֥וֹ אֶת-תְּלֻנֺּֽתֵיכֶם עַל-יְהֹוָ֑ה וְנַ֣חְנוּ מָה כִּ֥י תַלִּינוּ עָלֵֽינוּ: וַיֺּ֣אמֶר משֶׁה בְּתֵ֣ת יְהֹוָה— לָכֶ’ם בָּעֶ”רֶב בָּשָׂ֣ר לֶֽאֱכֺל וְלֶ֤חֶם בַּבֺּ’קֶר‘ לִשְׂבֺּעַ בִּשְׁמֺ֤עַ יְהֹוָה‘ אֶת-תְּלֻנֺּ֣תֵיכֶם אֲשֶׁר-אַתֶּ֥ם מַלִּינִם עָלָ֑יו וְנַ֣חְנוּ מָה לֹֽא-עָלֵ֥ינוּ תְלֻנֺּֽתֵיכֶם כִּ֥י עַל-יְהֹוָֽה: וַיֺּ֤אמֶר משֶׁה‘ אֶֽל-אַֽהֲרֺן אֱמֺר אֶל-כָּל-עֲדַת‘ בְּנֵ֣י יִשְׂרָאֵל קִרְ֒בוּ לִפְנֵ֣י יְהֹוָ֑ה כִּ֣י שָׁמַע אֵת תְּלֻנֺּֽתֵיכֶֽם: וַיְ֒הִי כְּדַבֵּ֤ר אַֽהֲרֺן‘ אֶל-כָּל-עֲדַ֣ת בְּנֵֽי-יִשְׂרָאֵל וַיִּפְנוּ אֶל-הַמִּדְבָּ֑ר וְהִנֵּה‘ כְּב֣וֹד יְהֹוָה נִרְאָה בֶּֽעָנָֽן: וַיְדַבֵּ֥ר יְהֹוָה אֶל-משֶׁ֥ה לֵּאמֺֽר: שָׁמַעְתִּי <fj>

עַד-בֺּאָם אֶל-אֶ֣רֶץ נוֹשָׁ֑בֶת אֶת-הַמָּן‘ אָֽכְ֒לוּ עַד-בֺּאָם אֶל-קְצֵה אֶ֥רֶץ כְּנָֽעַן: וְהָעֺמֶר עֲשִׂרִ֥ית הָֽאֵיפָה הֽוּא:
<M tex><M ex><EM><EN>And Adonoy said to Moses, "See, I will make bread rain down from heaven for you; and the people will go out and gather it for each day[’s needs], so that I may test them to see if they will live according to My Torah or not. On the sixth day, they shall prepare what they bring [home], and it will be twice as much as they gather every day." Then Moses and Aaron said to all the Children of Israel, "When evening comes you will know that it was Adonoy Who brought you out of Egypt. And in the morning you will see the glory of Adonoy, since He has heard your complaints against Adonoy. But we---what are we that you should complain against us?"<FL>
<EM><EN>And Moses said, "When Adonoy gives us meat to eat in the evening and a satisfying meal of bread in the morning, Adonoy will have heard your complaints, which you are addressing to Him. What are we? Your complaints are not against us, but against Adonoy." Then Moses said to Aaron, "Tell the entire community of the Children of Israel, ‘Come near before Adonoy, for He has heard your complaints.’<k 2>" When Adonoy spoke to the entire community of the Children of Israel, they turned toward the wilderness, and behold, the glory of Adonoy appeared in the cloud.<FL>
<EM><EN>Adonoy spoke to Moses saying, "I have heard the complaints of the Children of Israel; speak to them, saying, ‘In the afternoon you will eat meat, and in the morning you will have your fill of bread; and you will know that I am Adonoy, your God.’<k 2>" And it was in the evening that flocks of quail rose and covered the encampment; and in the morning there was a layer of dew around the encampment.<FL>
<EM><EN>The layer of dew evaporated, and behold on the surface of the wilderness were thin flakes, as fine as frost on the ground. The Children of Israel saw it and said to one another, "What is this?" For they did not know what it was. Moses said to them, "This is the bread that Adonoy is giving you to eat." "This is what Adonoy has commanded: Every man shall take as much as he needs for food, an <i>omer</i> per person; according to the number of your souls let each man take for the individuals in his tent." The Children of Israel did so; they gathered it, some more, some less. But when then they measured it with an <i>omer,</i> the one who took more did not have extra, and the one who took less was not lacking. Each one had gathered according to his required nourishment. Moses said to them, "Let jo one leave any of it over until morning." But some did not listen to Moses and left part of it over until the morning. It turned wormy and became putrid; and Moses was angry at them; they gathered it each morning, every man according to what he needed. The sun then became hot and it melted.<FL>
<M tex><M ex><EM><EN>On the sixth day [of the week] they gathered a double portion of food, two <i>omers</i> for each person. All the leaders of the community came and reported it to Moses. He said to them, "This is what Adonoy has [already] spoken: tomorrow is a day of rest, Adonoy’s holy Shabbos. Bake what you want to bake, and cook what you want to cook and whatever is left over, put away carefully until morning. They put it away until morning as Moses commanded, and it did not become putrid, and there were no worms in it. Then Moses said, "Eat it today, for today is Adonoy’s Shabbos. Today you will not find [manna] in the field. Six days you shall gather it, but the seventh day is Shabbos; there will be no [manna] on that day." But it happened on the seventh day that some of the people went out to gather [manna] but they found nothing.<FL>
<EM><EN>Adonoy said to Moses, "How long will you refuse to keep My commandments and My teachings? Look, Adonoy has given you the Shabbos; that is why on the sixth day He gave you food for two days. Every man must remain in his place; no man may leave his designated place on the seventh day." So the people rested on the seventh day. The House of Israel named the food <i>manna.</i> It was like white coriander seed and it tasted like dough kneaded with honey. Moses said, "This is what Adonoy has commanded, ‘Fill an <i>omer</i> measure with it as a keepsake for your generations, so they will see the food with which I fed you in the wilderness when I took you out of Egypt." Moses said to Aaron, "Take a jar and place an <i>omer</i> full of manna in it, and place it before Adonoy as a keepsake for your generations." As Adonoy commanded Moses, so did Aaron place it before the Testimony as a keepsake. The Children of Israel ate the manna for forty years until they came to an inhabited land. They ate the manna until they came to the edge of the land of Canaan. The <i>omer</i> is one-tenth of a <i>ephah.</i><FL>
<M h> <M long> אַתָּה הוּא יְהֺוָה לְבַדֶּֽךָ, אַתָּה עָשִֽׂיתָ אֶת הַשָּׁמַֽיִם וּשְׁמֵי הַשָּׁמַֽיִם, הָאָֽרֶץ וְכָל אֲשֶׁר עָלֶֽיהָ, הַיַּמִּים וְכָל אֲשֶׁר בָּהֶם, וְאַתָּה מְחַיֶּה אֶת כֻּלָּם. וְאַתָּה הוּא שֶׁעָשִֽׂיתָ נִסִּים וְנִפְלָאוֹת גְּדוֹלוֹת תָּמִיד עִם אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ. גַם בַּמִּדְבָּר הִמְטַרְתָּ לָהֶם לֶֽחֶם מִן הַשָּׁמַֽיִם וּמִצּוּר הַחַלָּמִישׁ הוֹצֵֽאתָ לָהֶם מַֽיִם, וְגַם נָתַֽתָּ לָהֶם כָּל צָרְכֵיהֶם, וְשִׂמְלָתָם לֹא בָלְתָה מֵעֲלֵיהֶם. כֵּן בְּרַחֲמֶֽיךָ הָרַבִּים וּבַחֲסָדֶֽיךָ הָעֲצוּמִים תְּזוּנֵֽנוּ וּתְפַרְנְ֒סֵֽנוּ וּתְכַלְכְּ֒לֵֽנוּ וְתַסְפִּיק כָּל צָרְכֵֽנוּ וְצָרְכֵי עַמְּ֒ךָ בֵּית יִשְׂרָאֵל הַמְ֒רֻבִּים, בְּמִלּוּי וּבְרֶוַח בְּלִי טֺֽרַח וְעָמָל גָּדוֹל, מִתַּֽחַת יָדְ֒ךָ הַנְּ֒קִיָּה וְלֹא מִתַּֽחַת יְדֵי בָשָׂר וָדָם:
<M tex> <M long> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ יְהֺוָה אֱלֹהַי וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתַי שֶׁתָּכִין לִי וּלְאַנְשֵׁי בֵיתִי כָּל מַחְסוֹרֵֽנוּ, וּלְכָל שָׁעָה וְשָׁעָה מִשָּׁעוֹתֵֽנוּ דֵי סִפּוּקֵֽנוּ, וּלְכָל עֶֽצֶם מֵעֲצָמֵֽינוּ דֵי מִחְיָתֵֽנוּ, כְּיָדְ֒ךָ הַטּוֹבָה וְהָרְ֒חָבָה, וְלֹא כְּמִעוּט מִפְעָלֵֽינוּ וְקֹצֶר חֲסָדֵֽינוּ וּמִזְּעֵיר גְּמוּלוֹתֵֽנוּ. וְיִהְיֶה מְזוֹנוֹתַי וּמְזוֹנוֹת אַנְשֵׁי בֵיתִי וְזַרְעִי וְזֶֽרַע זַרְעִי מְסוּרִים בְּיָדְ֒ךָ וְלֹא בְּיַד בָּשָׂר וָדָם:
<@01>Birkas Hamazon
<@01>ברכת המזון
<M t1><b>Psalm 137</b>
<M h> תהלים קלז
<M in>Psalm 137 is recited before </i>Birkas Hamazon<i> on weekdays<FC>
in memory of the destruction of the Beis Hamikdash<FC>
<M t2>By the rivers of Babylon,
<M h> <M newbold> עַל-נַהֲרוֹת בָּבֶל <M reg>
<M e>there we sat and we also wept,
<M h> שָׁם יָשַֽׁבְנוּ גַּם-בָּכִֽינוּ
<M e>when we remembered Zion.
<M h> בְּזָכְרֵֽנוּ אֶת-צִיּוֹן:
<M e>Upon the willows in its midst,
<M h> עַל-עֲרָבִים בְּתוֹכָהּ
<M e>we hung our harps.
<M h> תָּלִֽינוּ כִּנֹּרוֹתֵֽינוּ:
<M e>For there our captors demanded of us
<M h> כִּי שָׁם שְׁאֵלֽוּנוּ שׁוֹבֵֽינוּ
<M e>words of song,
<M h> דִּבְ֒רֵי-שִׁיר
<M e>and our tormentors asked of us [with] mirth;
<M h> וְתוֹלָלֵֽינוּ שִׂמְחָה
<M e>"Sing to us from the song[s] of Zion."
<M h> שִֽׁירוּ לָֽנוּ מִשִּׁיר צִיּוֹן:
<M e>How shall we sing the song of Adonoy
<M h> אֵיךְ נָשִׁיר אֶת-שִׁיר-יְהֹוָה
<M e>on alien soil?
<M h> עַל אַדְ֒מַת נֵכָר:
<M e>If I ever forget you, Jerusalem,
<M h> אִם-אֶשְׁכָּחֵךְ יְרוּשָׁלָֽםִ
<M e>may my right hand forget [its movement].
<M h> תִּשְׁכַּח יְמִינִי:
<M e>May my tongue cleave to my palate,
<M h> תִּדְבַּק לְשׁוֹנִי לְחִכִּי
<M e>if I remember you not;
<M h> אִם-לֺא אֶזְכְּרֵֽכִי
<M e>if I set not Jerusalem
<M h> אִם-לֺא אַעֲלֶה אֶת-יְרוּשָׁלַֽםִ
<M e>above my highest joy.
<M h> עַל רֹאשׁ שִׂמְחָתִי:
<M e>Remember, Adonoy,
<M h> זְכֹר יְהֹוָה
<M e>to the sons of Edom the day of Jerusalem,
<M h> לִבְ֒נֵי אֱדוֹם אֵת יוֹם יְרוּשָׁלָֽםִ
<M e>[it was they] who said,
<M h> הָאֹמְ֒רִים
<M e>"Raze it, raze it to its very foundation."
<M h> עָֽרוּ עָֽרוּ עַד הַיְ֒סוֹד בָּהּ:
<M e>Daughter of Babylon,
<M h> בַּת-בָּבֶל
<M e>you are the annihilated one;
<M h> הַשְּׁ֒דוּדָה
<M e>fortunate is he who will repay you
<M h> אַשְׁרֵי שֶׁיְּ֒שַׁלֶּם-לָךְ
<M e>for all you have done to us.
<M h> אֶת-גְּמוּלֵךְ שֶׁגָּמַלְתְּ לָֽנוּ:
<M e>Fortunate is he who will take
<M h> אַשְׁרֵי שֶׁיֹּאחֵז
<M e>and dash your little ones against the rock.
<M h> וְנִפֵּץ אֶת-עֹלָלַֽיִךְ אֶל-הַסָּֽלַע:
<M t1><b>Psalm 126</b>
<M h> תהלים קכו
<M in>Psalm 126 is recited on Shabbos, Yom Tov and other festive occasions such as weddings, circumcisions or redemption of the first born.<FC>
<M t2>A Song of Ascents.
<M h> שִׁיר הַמַּעֲלוֹת <M reg>
<M e>When Adonoy brings about
<M h> בְּשׁוּב יְהֹוָה
<M e>the return to Zion
<M h> אֶת-שִׁיבַת צִיּוֹן
<M e>we will have been like dreamers.<M tnt>
<M h> הָיִֽינוּ כְּחֹלְ֒מִים:
<M e>Then will our mouths be filled with laughter,<M tnt>
<M h> אָז יִמָּלֵא שְׂחוֹק פִּֽינוּ
<M e>and our tongue with joyous song.
<M h> וּלְ֒שׁוֹנֵֽנוּ רִנָּה,
<M e>Then will they say among the nations:
<M h> אָז יֹאמְ֒רוּ בַגּוֹיִם
<M e>‘Adonoy has done great things for them.’
<M h> הִגְדִּיל יְהֹוָה לַעֲשׂוֹת עִם-אֵֽלֶּה:
<M e>Adonoy had done great things for us;
<M h> הִגְדִּיל יְהֹוָה לַעֲשׂוֹת עִמָּֽנוּ,
<M e>we will [then] rejoice.
<M h> הָיִֽינוּ שְׂמֵחִים:
<M e>Adonoy! bring back our exiles
<M h> שׁוּבָה יְהֹוָה אֶת-שְׁבִיתֵֽנוּ
<M e>like springs in the desert.<M tnt>
<M h> כַּאֲפִיקִים בַּנֶּֽגֶב:
<M e>Those who sow in tears
<M h> הַזֹּרְ֒עִים בְּדִמְעָה,
<M e>will reap with joyous song.<M tnt>
<M h> בְּרִנָּה יִקְצֹֽרוּ:
<M e>[Though] he walks along weeping,
<M h> הָלוֹךְ יֵלֵךְ וּבָכֹה,
<M e>carrying the bag of seed,
<M h> נֹשֵׂא מֶֽשֶׁךְ-הַזָּֽרַע,
<M e>he will return with joyous song
<M h> בֹּא-יָבֹא בְרִנָּה,
<M e>carrying his sheaves.
<M h> נֹשֵׂא אֲלֻמֹּתָיו:
<M in>When three or more males, aged 13 or older eat together one of them leads the group in reciting the Birkas Hamazon.<FC>
<M in>The leader begins by saying:<FC>
<M t2>"Gentlemen, let us say the blessing:
<M h> רַבּוֹתַי <M reg> נְבָרֵךְ:
<M in>The others respond:<FC>
<M t2>"The Name of Adonoy will be blessed
<M h> <M reg> יְהִי שֵׁם יְהֹוָה מְבֹרָךְ
<M e>from now forever."
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם:
<M in>The leader repeats:<FC>
<M t2>"The Name of Adonoy will be blessed
<M h> יְהִי <M reg> שֵׁם יְהֹוָה מְבֹרָךְ
<M e>from now forever."
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם:
<M in>The leader continues: (the words "our God" are substituted for "Him" and "He" if ten males are in the group):<FC>
<M t2>"With your permission
<M h> בִּרְ֒שׁוּת <M reg>
<M e>our masters and teachers,
<M h> מָרָנָן וְרַבָּנָן וְרַבּוֹתַי
<M e>Let us bless (our God,) Him,
<M h> נְבָרֵךְ ) <M small2> בעשרה <M reg> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ(
<M e>for we have eaten of His bounty."
<M h> שֶׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ:
<M in>The others respond accordingly:<FC>
<M t2>"Blessed is (our God) He
<M h> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> ) <M small2> בעשרה <M reg> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ(
<M e>for we have eaten of His bounty
<M h> שֶֽׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ
<M e>and through His goodness we live."
<M h> וּבְ֒טוּבוֹ חָיִֽינוּ:
<M in>The leader repeats:<FC>
<M t2>"Blessed is (our God) He
<M h> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> ) <M small2> בעשרה <M reg> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ(
<M e>for we have eaten of His bounty
<M h> שֶֽׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ
<M e>and through His goodness we live."
<M h> וּבְ֒טוּבוֹ חָיִֽינוּ:
<M in>If there are at least 10 men, add:<FC>
<M t2>"Blessed is He and blessed is His Name."
<M h> <M reg> בָּרוּךְ הוּא וּבָרוּךְ שְׁמוֹ:
<M t1>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם
<M e>Who nourishes the entire world
<M h> הַזָּן אֶת הָעוֹלָם כֻּלּוֹ
<M e>with His goodness,
<M h> בְּטוּבוֹ
<M e>with favor, with kindness, and with mercy.<M tnt>
<M h> בְּחֵן בְּ֒חֶֽסֶד וּבְ֒רַחֲמִים
<M e>He provides food for all flesh,<M tnt>
<M h> הוּא נוֹתֵן לֶֽחֶם לְכָל בָּשָׂר
<M e>for His kindness endures forever.
<M h> כִּי לְעוֹלָם חַסְדּוֹ
<M e>And through His great goodness,
<M h> וּבְ֒טוּבוֹ הַגָּדוֹל
<M e>we have never lacked
<M h> תָּמִיד לֺא חָסַר לָֽנוּ
<M e>and we will not lack food
<M h> וְאַל יֶחְסַר לָֽנוּ מָזוֹן
<M e>forever and ever,
<M h> לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד
<M e>for the sake of His great Name.
<M h> בַּעֲבוּר שְׁמוֹ הַגָּדוֹל
<M e>For He is Almighty
<M h> כִּי הוּא אֵל
<M e>Who nourishes<M tnt> and maintains all,
<M h> זָן וּמְ֒פַרְנֵס לַכֹּל
<M e>does good to all, and prepares nourishment
<M h> וּמֵטִיב לַכֹּל וּמֵכִין מָזוֹן
<M e>for all His creatures which He has created.
<M h> לְכָל בְּרִיּוֹתָיו אֲשֶׁר בָּרָא.
<M e>As it is said:
<M h> כָּאָמוּר,
<M e>You open Your hand
<M h> פּוֹתֵֽחַ אֶת-יַדֶֽךָ
<M e>and satisfy the desire of every living being.
<M h> וּמַשְׂבִּֽיעַ לְכָל-חַי רָצוֹן:
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>Who nourishes all.<M tnt>
<M h> הַזָּן אֶת הַכֹּל:
<M t1>We thank You, Adonoy, our God,
<M h> <M newbold> נוֹדֶה <M reg> לְּךָ יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>for Your parceling out as a heritage
<M h> עַל שֶׁהִנְחַֽלְתָּ
<M e>to our fathers,
<M h> לַאֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ
<M e>a land<M tnt> which is
<M h> אֶֽרֶץ
<M e>desirable, good, and spacious;
<M h> חֶמְדָּה טוֹבָה וּרְ֒חָבָה
<M e>for Your bringing us out, Adonoy, our God,
<M h> וְעַל שֶׁהוֹצֵאתָֽנוּ יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>from the land of Egypt,
<M h> מֵאֶֽרֶץ מִצְרַֽיִם
<M e>and redeeming us from the house of bondage;
<M h> וּפְ֒דִיתָֽנוּ מִבֵּית עֲבָדִים
<M e>for Your covenant
<M h> וְעַל בְּרִיתְ֒ךָ
<M e>which You sealed in our flesh;
<M h> שֶׁחָתַֽמְתָּ בִּבְ֒שָׂרֵֽנוּ
<M e>for Your Torah<M tnt> which You taught us;
<M h> וְעַל תּוֹרָתְ֒ךָ שֶׁלִּמַּדְתָּֽנוּ
<M e>for Your statutes
<M h> וְעַל חֻקֶּֽיךָ
<M e>which You made known to us;
<M h> שֶׁהוֹדַעְתָּֽנוּ
<M e>for the life, favor, and kindness
<M h> וְעַל חַיִּים חֵן וָחֶֽסֶד
<M e>which You granted us;
<M h> שֶׁחוֹנַנְתָּֽנוּ
<M e>and for the provision of food
<M h> וְעַל אֲכִילַת מָזוֹן
<M e>with which You nourish and maintain us

<M e>constantly, every day, at all times

<M e>and in every hour.
<M h> וּבְ֒כָל שָׁעָה:

<AF 6>On Chanukah and Purim add:<FC>
<M in> If you forgot to say <M hh> עַל הַנִּסִּים <M ee> , you may include it when you reach <M hh> הָרַחֲמָן <M ee> on page 246 by saying: <M hh> הָרַחֲמָן הוּא יַעֲשֶׂה-לָּנוּ נִדִּים וְנִפְלָאוֹת כְּמוֹ שֶׁעָשָׂה לַאֲבוֹתֵינוּ בַּיָּמִים הָהֵם בַּזְּמַן הַזֶּה. <M ee> and then continue on Chanukah with: <M hh> בִּימֵי מַתִּתְיָהוּ <M ee> , and on Purim with: <M hh> בִּימֵי מָרְדְּכַי וְאֶסְתֵּר <M ee> . <FL>

<M es>for the redemption, for the mighty deeds,

<M in>On Chanukah:<FC>
<M ts>In the days of Matisyahu,
<M hs> בִּימֵי מַתִּתְיָֽהוּ <FL>
<M es>son of Yochanan the High Priest,
<M hs> בֶּן יוֹחָנָן כֹּהֵן גָּדוֹל <FL>
<M es>the Hasmonean and his sons,
<M hs> חַשְׁמוֹנָאִי וּבָנָיו <FL>
<M es>when the evil Greek kingdom rose up
<M hs> כְּשֶׁעָמְ֒דָה מַלְ֒כוּת יָוָן הָרְ֒שָׁעָה <FL>
<M es>against Your people Israel
<M hs> עַל עַמְּ֒ךָ יִשְׂרָאֵל <FL>

<M hs> לְהַשְׁכִּיחָם תּוֹרָתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M es>and to turn them away
<M hs> וּלְ֒הַעֲבִירָם <FL>
<M es>from the statutes of Your will---
<M hs> מֵחֻקֵּי רְצוֹנֶֽךָ, <FL>
<M es>You, in Your abundant mercy,
<M hs> וְאַתָּה בְּרַחֲמֶֽיךָ הָרַבִּים <FL>
<M es>stood by them in their time of distress,
<M hs> עָמַֽדְתָּ לָהֶם בְּעֵת צָרָתָם <FL>
<M es>You defended their cause,
<M hs> רַֽבְתָּ אֶת רִיבָם <FL>
<M es>You judged their grievances,
<M hs> דַּֽנְתָּ אֶת דִּינָם <FL>
<M es>You avenged them.
<M hs> נָקַֽמְתָּ אֶת נִקְ֒מָתָם <FL>
<M es>You delivered the mighty
<M hs> מָסַֽרְתָּ גִבּוֹרִים <FL>
<M es>into the hands of the weak,
<M hs> בְּיַד חַלָּשִׁים <FL>
<M es>many into the hands of the few,
<M hs> וְרַבִּים בְּיַד מְעַטִּים <FL>
<M es>defiled people into the hands of the undefiled,
<M hs> וּטְ֒מֵאִים בְּיַד טְהוֹרִים <FL>
<M es>the wicked into the hands of the righteous,
<M hs> וּרְ֒שָׁעִים בְּיַד צַדִּיקִים <FL>
<M es>and insolent [sinners] into the hands of
<M hs> וְזֵדִים בְּיַד <FL>
<M es>diligent students of Your Torah.
<M hs> עוֹסְ֒קֵי תוֹרָתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M es>And You made Yourself
<M hs> וּלְ֒ךָ עָשִֽׂיתָ <FL>
<M es>a great and sanctified name in Your world.
<M hs> שֵׁם גָּדוֹל וְקָדוֹשׁ בְּעוֹלָמֶֽךָ <FL>
<M es>And for Your people, Israel,
<M hs> וּלְ֒עַמְּ֒ךָ יִשְׂרָאֵל <FL>
<M es>You performed a great deliverance
<M hs> עָשִֽׂיתָ תְּשׁוּעָה גְדוֹלָה <FL>
<M es>and redemption unto this very day.
<M hs> וּפֻרְקָן כְּהַיּוֹם הַזֶּה <FL>
<M es>Afterwards, Your sons entered
<M hs> וְאַחַר כַּךְ בָּֽאוּ בָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M es>the Holy of Holies of Your Abode,
<M hs> לִדְ֒בִיר בֵּיתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M es>cleaned Your Temple,
<M hs> וּפִנּוּ אֶת הֵיכָלֶֽךָ <FL>
<M es>purified Your Sanctuary,
<M hs> וְטִהֲרוּ אֶת מִקְדָּשֶֽׁךָ <FL>
<M es>and kindled lights
<M hs> וְהִדְלִֽיקוּ נֵרוֹת <FL>
<M es>in the Courtyards of Your Sanctuary,
<M hs> בְּחַצְ֒רוֹת קָדְשֶֽׁךָ <FL>
<M es>and designated these eight days of Chanukah
<M hs> וְקָבְ֒עוּ שְׁמוֹנַת יְמֵי חֲנֻכָּה אֵֽלּוּ <FL>
<M es>to thank and praise Your great Name.
<M hs> לְהוֹדוֹת וּלְ֒הַלֵּל לְשִׁמְ֒ךָ הַגָּדוֹל: <FL>
<M in>On Purim:<FC>
<M ts>In the days of Mordechai and Esther
<M hs> בִּימֵי מָרְדְּכַי וְאֶסְתֵּר <FL>

<M hs> לְפֶסַח: חַג הַמַּצּוֹת הַזֶּה <FL>
<M es>the <i>Festival of Sukkos</i>
<M hs> לְסֻכּוֹת: חַג הַסֻּכּוֹת הַזֶּה <FL>
<M es>the <I>Festival of Shmini Atseres</I>
<M hs> לש"ע וש"ת: שְׁמִינִי עֲצֶֽרֶת הַחַג הַזֶּה
<M es><i>Remebrance</i>
<M hs> לר"ה: הַזִּכָּרוֹן הַזֶּה
<M es>Remember us Adonoy, our God,
<M hs> זָכְ֒רֵֽנוּ יְהֹוָה אֱלֹהֵֽינוּ <FL>
<M es>on this day for well-being;
<M hs> בּוֹ לְטוֹבָה, <FL>
<M es>be mindful of us on this day for blessing,
<M hs> וּפָקְ֒דֵֽנוּ בוֹ לִבְ֒רָכָה, <FL>
<M es>and deliver us for good life.
<M hs> וְהוֹשִׁיעֵֽנוּ בוֹ לְחַיִּים טוֹבִים, <FL>
<M es>In accord with the promise of deliverance
<M hs> וּבִדְ֒בַר יְשׁוּעָה <FL>
<M es>and compassion,
<M hs> וְרַחֲמִים <FL>
<M es>spare us and favor us,
<M hs> חוּס וְחָנֵּֽנוּ, <FL>
<M es>have compassion on us and deliver us;
<M hs> וְרַחֵם עָלֵֽינוּ וְהוֹשִׁיעֵֽנוּ, <FL>
<M es>for to You our eyes are directed
<M hs> כִּי אֵלֶֽיךָ עֵינֵֽינוּ, <FL>
<M es>because You are the Almighty
<M hs> כִּי אֵל <FL>
<M es>Who is King, Gracious, and Merciful.
<M hs> מֶֽלֶךְ חַנּוּן וְרַחוּם אָֽתָּה: <FL>
<M ex> <EM> <EN> If you forgot to say <M hh> רְצֵה <M ee> or <M hh> יַעֲלֶה וְיָבֹא <M ee> and became aware of it </i> before <i> starting the fourth blessing ( <M hh> הַטּוֹב וְהַמֵּטִיב <M ee> ), or even if you are in doubt, see pages 249-250 for the appropriate blessing. <FL>
<EM> <EN> If you reminded yourself </i> after <i> you had already begun the fourth blessing </i> and have said <i> : <M hh> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה ה' <M ee> , then you must repeat the entire Birkas Hamazon. These laws apply only to Shabbos, and the Festival days of Pesach, Shavuos and Sukkos. On Chol Ha-Moed or on Rosh Chodesh days that do not fall on Shabbos, you need not repeat the Birkas Hamazon even though you began the blessing of <M hh> הַטּוֹב וְהַמֵּטִיב <M ee> . <FL>
<M t1>Rebuild Jerusalem, city of the Holy Sanctuary,
<M h> <M newbold> וּבְ֒נֵה <M reg> יְרוּשָׁלַֽיִם עִיר הַקֹּֽדֶשׁ
<M e>speedily, in our days.
<M h> בִּמְ֒הֵרָה בְיָמֵֽינוּ
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>Builder of Jerusalem in His mercy. Amein.<M tnt>
<M h> בּוֹנֵה בְרַחֲמָיו יְרוּשָׁלָֽיִם, אָמֵן:
<M t1>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>the Almighty, our Father, our King,
<M h> הָאֵל אָבִֽינוּ, מַלְכֵּֽנוּ,
<M e>our Mighty One, our Creator, our Redeemer,
<M h> אַדִּירֵֽנוּ בּוֹרְ֒אֵֽנוּ, גּוֹאֲלֵֽנוּ,
<M e>our Maker, our Holy One, Holy One of Jacob,
<M h> יוֹצְ֒רֵֽנוּ, קְדוֹשֵֽׁנוּ קְדוֹשׁ יַעֲקֹב,
<M e>our Shepherd, Shepherd of Israel,
<M h> רוֹעֵנוּ רוֹעֵה יִשְׂרָאֵל,
<M e>the King, Who is good and beneficent to all.
<M h> הַמֶּֽלֶךְ הַטּוֹב, וְהַמֵּטִיב לַכֹּל,
<M e>Every single day He has done good,
<M h> שֶׁבְּ֒כָל יוֹם וָיוֹם הוּא הֵטִיב,
<M e>does good, and will do good to us.
<M h> הוּא מֵטִיב, הוּא יֵיטִיב לָנוּ,
<M e>He has rewarded us, He rewards us,
<M h> הוּא גְמָלָֽנוּ, הוּא גוֹמְ֒לֵֽנוּ,
<M e>He will reward us forever with
<M h> הוּא יִגְמְלֵֽנוּ לָעַד
<M e>favor, kindness, and compassion,
<M h> לְחֵן וּלְ֒חֶֽסֶד וּלְ֒רַחֲמִים
<M e>relief, rescue, and success,
<M h> וּלְ֒רֶוַח הַצָּלָה וְהַצְלָחָה
<M e>blessing, deliverance, and consolation,
<M h> בְּרָכָה וִישׁוּעָה, נֶחָמָה,
<M e>maintenance, sustenance, compassion,
<M h> פַּרְנָסָה וְכַלְכָּלָה, וְרַחֲמִים,
<M e>life, peace, and everything good;
<M h> וְחַיִּים וְשָׁלוֹם, וְכָל טוֹב,
<M e>and of all good things
<M h> וּמִכָּל טוּב
<M e>may He never deprive us.<M tnt>
<M h> לְעוֹלָם אַל יְחַסְּ֒רֵֽנוּ:
<M t1>The Merciful One will reign over us
<M h> <M newbold> הָרַחֲמָן, <M reg> הוּא יִמְלוֹךְ עָלֵֽינוּ
<M e>forever and ever.
<M h> לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד,
<M e>The Merciful One will be blessed
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, הוּא יִתְבָּרֵךְ
<M e>in heaven and on earth.
<M h> בַּשָּׁמַֽיִם וּבָאָֽרֶץ,
<M e>The Merciful One will be praised
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, הוּא יִשְׁתַּבַּח
<M e>for all generations,
<M h> לְדוֹר דּוֹרִים,
<M e>He will be glorified through us
<M h> וְיִתְפָּאֵר בָּֽנוּ
<M e>forever and for all eternity;
<M h> לָעַד וּלְ֒נֵֽצַח נְצָחִים,
<M e>and He will be honored through us
<M h> וְיִתְהַדַּר בָּֽנוּ
<M e>for time everlasting.
<M h> לָעַד וּלְ֒עוֹלְ֒מֵי עוֹלָמִים,
<M e>May the Merciful One
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן,
<M e>maintain us with honor.
<M h> הוּא יְפַרְנְ֒סֵֽנוּ בְּכָבוֹד,
<M e>The Merciful One will break the yoke
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן הוּא יִשְׁבּוֹר עֻלֵּֽנוּ
<M e>(of oppression) from our necks
<M h> מֵעַל צַוּארֵֽנוּ
<M e>and lead us upright
<M h> וְהוּא יוֹלִיכֵֽנוּ קוֹמְ֒מִיּוּת
<M e>to our land.
<M h> לְאַרְצֵֽנוּ,
<M e>May the Merciful One send us
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, הוּא יִשְׁלַח לָֽנוּ
<M e>abundant blessing to this house,
<M h> בְּרָכָה מְרֻבָּה בַּבַּֽיִת הַזֶּה
<M e>and upon this table
<M h> וְעַל שֻׁלְחָן זֶה
<M e>at which we have eaten.
<M h> שֶׁאָכַֽלְנוּ עָלָיו,
<M e>The Merciful One will send us
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, הוּא יִשְׁלַח לָֽנוּ
<M e>Elijah the prophet,
<M h> אֶת אֵלִיָּֽהוּ הַנָּבִיא
<M e>who is remembered for good,
<M h> זָכוּר לַטּוֹב,
<M e>who will announce to us
<M h> וִיבַשֶּׂר לָֽנוּ
<M e>good tidings, deliverances,
<M h> בְּשׂוֹרוֹת טוֹבוֹת יְשׁוּעוֹת
<M e>and consolations.
<M h> וְנֶחָמוֹת:
<M in>When eating at your parents’ table, say:<FC>
<M t2>May the Merciful One bless
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, <M reg> הוּא יְבָרֵךְ
<M e>my father, my teacher,
<M h> אֶת אָבִי מוֹרִי
<M e>the master of this house,
<M h> בַּֽעַל הַבַּֽיִת הַזֶּה,
<M e>and my mother, my teacher,
<M h> וְאֶת אִמִּי מוֹרָתִי
<M e>the mistress of this house;
<M h> בַּעֲלַת הַבַּֽיִת הַזֶּה,
<M e>them, their household,
<M h> אוֹתָם וְאֶת בֵּיתָם
<M e>their children
<M h> וְאֶת זַרְעָם
<M e>and all that is theirs.
<M h> וְאֶת כָּל אֲשֶׁר לָהֶם

<M t2>May the Merciful One bless
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, <M reg> הוּא יְבָרֵךְ
<M e>me, my spouse, my children,
<M h> אוֹתִי וְאֶת אִשְׁתִּי וְאֶת זַרְעִי
<M e>and all that is mine;
<M h> וְאֶת כָּל אֲשֶׁר לִי,
<M in>A guest says:<FC>
<M t2>May the Merciful One bless
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן, <M reg> הוּא יְבָרֵךְ
<M e>the host
<M h> אֶת בַּֽעַל הַבַּֽיִת הַזֶּה,
<M e>and the hostess,
<M h> וְאֶת אִשְׁתּוֹ בַּעֲלַת הַבַּֽיִת הַזֶּה,
<M e>them, their household, their children
<M h> אוֹתָם וְאֶת בֵּיתָם וְאֶת זַרְעָם
<M e>and all that is theirs.
<M h> וְאֶת כָּל אֲשֶׁר לָהֶם
<M t2>May<M tnt> it be God’s will that the
<M h> <M newbold> יְהִי רָצוֹן <M reg>
<M e>host not be shamed
<M h> שֶׁלֺּא יֵבוֹשׁ בַּֽעַל הַבַּֽיִת
<M e>in this world
<M h> בָּעוֹלָם הַזֶּה
<M e>or humiliated in the World to Come.
<M h> וְלֺא יִכָּלֵם לָעוֹלָם הַבָּא
<M e>May he have great success
<M h> וְיִצְלַח מְאֹד
<M e>with all his possessions.
<M h> בְּכָל נְכָסָיו
<M e>May his properties and ours prosper
<M h> וְיִהְיוּ נְכָסָיו וּנְכָסֵֽינוּ מֻצְלָחִים
<M e>and be located close to town.
<M h> וּקְרוֹבִים לָעִיר
<M e>May no evil force have power over
<M h> וְאַל יִשְׁלֺט שָׂטָן
<M e>his endeavors
<M h> לֺא בְמַעֲשֵׂי יָדָיו
<M e>or our endeavors.
<M h> וְלֺא בְמַעֲשֵׂי יָדֵֽינוּ
<M e>May no opportunity present itself before him
<M h> וְאַל יִזְדַּקֵּר לֺא לְפָנָיו
<M e>or before us
<M h> וְלֺא לְפָנֵֽינוּ
<M e>to contemplate
<M h> שׁוּם דְּבַר הִרְהוּר
<M e>[committing any] sin,
<M h> חֵטְא
<M e>transgression or iniquity
<M h> וַעֲבֵרָה וְעָוֹן
<M e>from now forever.
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם:
<M t1>Ours and all that is ours---
<M h> אוֹתָֽנוּ וְאֶת כָּל אֲשֶׁר לָֽנוּ,
<M e>just as our forefathers were blessed---
<M h> כְּמוֹ שֶׁנִּתְבָּרְ֒כוּ אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ,
<M e>Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob---
<M h> אַבְרָהָם יִצְחָק וְיַעֲקֹב:

<M e>and "With everything";<M tnt>
<M h> כֹּל,

<M h> כֵּן יְבָרֵךְ אוֹתָֽנוּ
<M e>all of us together, with a perfect blessing
<M h> כֻּלָּֽנוּ יַֽחַד, בִּבְ֒רָכָה שְׁלֵמָה,
<M e>and let us say Amein.

<M h> בַּמָּרוֹם
<M e>may there be invoked upon them

<M e>and upon us, [the] merit
<M h> וְעָלֵֽינוּ זְכוּת,
<M e>to insure peace,
<M h> שֶׁתְּ֒הֵא לְמִשְׁמֶֽרֶת שָׁלוֹם,

<M h> וְנִשָּׂא בְרָכָה מֵאֵת יְהֹוָה
<M e>and kindness
<M h> וּצְ֒דָקָה
<M e>from the God of our deliverance;
<M h> מֵאֱלֺהֵי יִשְׁעֵֽנוּ,
<M e>and may we find favor and understanding
<M h> וְנִמְצָא חֵן וְשֵֽׂכֶל טוֹב
<M e>in the eyes of God and man.

<M h> אֶת סֻכַּת דָּוִד הַנּוֹפָֽלֶת:
<M t1>May the Merciful One make us worthy

<M e>of the days of the Messiah
<M h> לִימוֹת הַמָּשִֽׁיחַ

<M es>to His king,<M tnt>)
<M h> מַלְכּוֹ,

<M e>to David and his descendants forever.<M tnt>
<M h> לְדָוִד וּלְ֒זַרְעוֹ עַד עוֹלָם:
<M e>He Who makes peace in His high heavens
<M h> עֹשֶׂה שָׁלוֹם בִּמְ֒רוֹמָיו,
<M e>may He make peace for us
<M h> הוּא יַעֲשֶׂה שָׁלוֹם עָלֵֽינוּ
<M e>and for all Israel,
<M h> וְעַל כָּל יִשְׂרָאֵל,
<M e>and say, Amein.
<M h> וְאִמְ֒רוּ אָמֵן:
<M t1>Fear Adonoy, [you] His holy ones,
<M h> יְראוּ אֶת יְהֹוָה קְדוֹשָׁיו,
<M e>for those who fear Him suffer no deprivation.
<M h> כִּי אֵין מַחְסוֹר לִירֵאָיו:
<M e>Young lions may feel want and hunger,
<M h> כְּפִירִים רָשׁוּ וְרָעֵֽבוּ,
<M e>but those who seek Adonoy,
<M h> וְדוֹרְ֒שֵׁי יְהֹוָה
<M e>will not be deprived of any good thing.<M tnt>
<M h> לֺא יַחְסְ֒רוּ כָל טוֹב:
<M e>Give thanks to Adonoy, for He is good,
<M h> הוֹדוּ לַיהוָֹה כִּי טוֹב,
<M e>for His kindness endures forever.<M tnt>
<M h> כִּי לְעוֹלָם חַסְדּוֹ:
<M e>You open Your hand
<M h> פּוֹתֵֽחַ אֶת יָדֶֽךָ,
<M e>and satisfy the desire of every living being.<M tnt>
<M h> וּמַשְׂבִּֽיעַ לְכָל חַי רָצוֹן:
<M e>Blessed is the man who trusts in Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ הַגֶּֽבֶר אֲשֶׁר יִבְטַח בַּיהוָֹה,
<M e>so that Adonoy is his security.<M tnt>
<M h> וְהָיָה יְהֹוָה מִבְטַחוֹ:
<M e>I was young and I have grown old,
<M h> נַֽעַר הָיִֽיתִי גַם זָקַֽנְתִּי
<M e>yet I have never seen
<M h> וְלֺא רָאִֽיתִי
<M e>a righteous man forsaken,
<M h> צַדִּיק נֶעֱזָב,
<M e>nor his children begging for bread.<M tnt>
<M h> וְזַרְעוֹ מְבַקֵּשׁ לָֽחֶם:
<M e>Adonoy will give strength to His people,
<M h> יְהֹוָה עוֹז לְעַמּוֹ יִתֵּן,
<M e>Adonoy will bless His people with peace.<M tnt>
<M h> יְהֹוָה יְבָרֵךְ אֶת עַמּוֹ בַּשָּׁלוֹם:

<M e>to His people Israel with love
<M h> לְעַמּוֹ יִשְׂרָאֵל בְּאַהֲבָה

<M h> <M reg> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>our God, King of the universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Creator of numerous living things
<M h> בּוֹרֵא נְפָשׁוֹת רַבּוֹת
<M e>and what they lack,
<M h> וְחֶסְרוֹנָן,
<M e>for all that You have created
<M h> עַל כָּל מַה שֶׁבָּרָֽאתָ
<M e>in order to sustain the life of every being.
<M h> לְהַחֲיוֹת בָּהֶם נֶפֶשׁ כָּל חָי,
<M e>Blessed [is He Who] is
<M h> בָּרוּךְ
<M e>the Life of the Worlds.
<M h> חֵי הָעוֹלָמִים:
<lp><M fn><M fnt>Upon the redemption and return to Zion, the harshness of the exile will seem to the Jews like a terrible dream.---<i>Radak</i><FL>
<EM><EN>The splendor of the return to Zion will be like the realization of an impossible dream.---<i>Seporno</i><FL>
<M fnt>In the Talmud (<i>Maseches Berachos</i> 31a) Rabbi Shimon bar Yochai rules that a Jew is forbidden to fill his mouth with laughter in this world until the time comes when all nations declare: "Adonoy has done great things for them"---as the verse states: <M hh><M ee>, <i>then</i>: only then, when God’s love for us is universally recognized, may we experience total exultation.<FL>
<M fnt>Just as springs of water can transform an arid desert into a fertile oasis, so will we be transformed, and flourish when God delivers us from exile.---<i>Rashi</i><FL>
<M fnt>A person who plants in desert-like soil is always fearful that his crops will not grow. If a spring of water should suddenly appear on his land, his joy will know no bounds. So great will our joy be at the ultimate redemption that will follow the oppression of exile.---<i>Radak</i><FL>
<M fnt>The righteous find <i>favor</i> in the eyes of God and are nourished because of their merit. Those who are not so worthy and do not find favor, are provided for through God’s beneficent <i>kindness</i>; while even the least worthy are recipients of God’s <i>mercy.</i>--- <i>Maharal</i> in <i>Nesivos<i> Olom</i><FL>
<M fnt>This citation from <i>Psalms</i> 136:25 indicates that God’s kindness and compassion are universal, relating to all flesh, including animals.---<i>Avudraham.</i><FL>
<M fnt>"Nourishes" refers to food, "maintains" refers to clothing and "does good" refers to shelter. These are the basic needs of man, all of which God provides.---<i>Etz Yosef</i><FL>
<M fnt>The first blessing of the <i>Birkas Hamazon</i> was composed by Moses in appreciation for the manna which God provided for the Jews in the desert.<FL>
<EM><EN>The second blessing, beginning with "Let us thank You," was composed by Joshua in gratitude for the privilege of entering the Promised Land.<FL>
<EM><EN>The third blessing, beginning with "Have mercy," was composed by David who conquered Jerusalem, and by Solomon who built the Temple.<FL>
<EM><EN>The fourth blessing "Who is good and beneficent to all" was composed by Rabban Gamliel the Elder and his court in Yavneh in gratitude to God for preserving the bodies of the victims of the Roman massacre at Betar, and for being enabled to bring them to proper burial.---<i>Maseches Berachos</i> 48b<FL>
<M fnt>The land is mentioned even before the Exodus from Egypt because God demonstrated His extraordinary concern for the Jewish people at the very beginning of their history; first by the promise He gave to the Patriarchs concerning the Land of Israel and then, with the fulfillment of that promise, once He redeemed them from Egypt to enter the Land.---<i>S.R. Hirsch</i><FL>
<M fnt>"Torah" refers to laws which are comprehensible to the human intellect; it is therefore <i>taught.</i> "Statutes" (<M hh><M ee>) are beyond human understanding and are therefore merely <i>made known</i> to man, for man cannot comprehend them. <i>Eyun Tefilloh</i><FL>
<M fnt>Deuteronomy 8:10<FL>
<M fnt>"Tend us" by providing the basic necessities of life such as bread and water; "nourish" us with an enriched diet including foods such as fruits and vegetables.---<i>Etz Yosef</i><FL>
<M fnt>"Maintain us" with food and shelter; "sustain us" by providing our needs on a regular basis, not on a feast or famine cycle; and "relieve us" by giving us ample means to live comfortably.---<i>Etz Yosef</i><FL>
<M fnt>May we not be "ashamed" in this world due to poverty and may we not be "humiliated" in the World-to-Come, because of our transgressions. Poverty often brings shame which in turn might cause a person to lose faith.---<i>Etz Yosef</i><FL>
<M fnt>Even though prayers for personal needs are not recited on Shabbos, this particular prayer does contain such a request, because it is so closely interwoven with the commandment to rest on Shabbos. Since we are commanded to make Shabbos a day of sacred rest, we ask that our repose not be desecrated by distress or misfortune.---<i>Avudraham</i><FL>
<M fnt>It is unusual for one to answer Amein after his own blessing. This blessing ends with Amein because it marks the end of the three blessings, authority for which is derived from <i>Deuteronomy</i> (8:10) and separates them from the next blessing which is Rabbinic in origin.---<i>Maseches Berachos</i> 45b<FL>
<M fnt>Many people are granted the bounties of life but are unable to enjoy them. We first invoke God’s blessing for all the good things in life and then ask Him to grant us the privilege of enjoying them.---<i>Iyun Tefilloh.</i><FL>
<M fnt>This blessing is quoted from the talmud (<i>Maseches Berachos</i> 46a). It has been omitted in most Siddurim. The Mishnah Berura (201:5) takes issue with its omission. We have incorporated it in this edition.<FL>
<M fnt>Abraham was blessed "in all things." <i>Genesis</i> 24:1<FL>
<M fnt>Isaac said: "I have partaken from everything." <i>Genesis</i> 27:33<FL>
<M fnt>Jacob said: "I have everything." <i>Genesis</i> 33:11<FL>
<M fnt>During weekdays when we feel the darkness of exile we say: "God gives deliverance to His king," thus acknowledging His preparation for the time of redemption. On Shabbos and Yom Tov which are reminiscent of the time of the Messiah, when God will be a tower of deliverance, we state it as a fact.<FL>
<M fnt>II Samuel 22:51<FL>
<M fnt>Psalms 34:10-11<FL>
<M fnt>Psalms 136:1<FL>
<M fnt>Psalms 145:16<FL>
<M fnt>Jeremiah 17:7<FL>
<M fnt>Psalms 37:25<FL>
<M fnt>Psalms 29:11<FL>
<M fnt>According to some authorities, "And for the sustenance" is added to the blessing.<FL>

<M in>Before putting up a Mezuzah, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us to attach a mezuzah.
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ לִקְבּֽוֹעַ מְזוּזָה:
<M in>Upon erecting a protective fence around a roof or porch, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ
<M e>to erect a [protective] barrier.
<M h> לַעֲשׂוֹת מַעֲקֶה:
<M in>Before immersing metal or glass utensils in a Mikveh, say:<FC>
<M ex>[This applies only to vessels manufactured by or purchased from a non-Jew, and are used for the preparation or in the consumption of food or drink.]<FL>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us about immersing vessels.
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ עַל טְבִילַת כֵּלִים:
<M in>Separating the challah from the dough:<FC>
<M ex>[When you prepare a batch of dough that is at least 3 lbs. 10.7 ounces, you must remove a <I>kazayis</I> piece of dough and recite the above blessing. This piece is then burned. If the dough weighs at least 2 lbs, 10 ounces but less than 3 lbs, 10.7 ounces, the <I>kazayis</I> piece is removed but the blessing is not recited.]<FL>
<M in>Before separating the challah from the dough, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,

<M e>and commanded us
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ
<M e>to separate challah from the dough.
<M h> לְהַפְרִישׁ חַלָּה מִן הָעִסָּה:
<@01>Berachos Said Before Eating or Drinking
<@01>ברכות הנהנין
<M in>Before eating anything made of wheat, barley, rye, oats, spelt or rice, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who created various kinds of nourishment.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא מִינֵי מְזוֹנוֹת:
<M in>Before drinking wine or grape juice say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the vine.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הַגָּֽפֶן:
<M in>Before eating tree-grown fruits say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who created the fruit of the tree.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הָעֵץ:
<M in>Before eating earth-grown produce (vegetables) say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the earth.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הָאֲדָמָה:
<M in>Before eating meat, fish, milk, eggs, cheese, mushrooms,<FC>
and before drinking all liquids except wine and grape juice, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>by Whose word all things came to be.
<M h> שֶׁהַכֹּל נִהְיֶה בִּדְבָרוֹ:
<M in>Before tasting any fruit or vegetable for the first time in the season, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who has kept us alive and sustained us
<M h> שֶׁהֶחֱיָֽנוּ וְקִיְּ֒מָֽנוּ
<M e>and brought us to this time.
<M h> וְהִגִּיעָֽנוּ לַזְּ֒מַן הַזֶּה:
<M ex>[This blessing is also said when purchasing a new suit or dress.]<FL>
<@01>Berachos Said Upon Witnessing Phenomenal Sights
<@01>ברכות הראיה
<M in>When seeing shooting stars, a comet, or witnessing a hurricane or lightning say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who makes the work of Creation.
<M h> עוֹשֵׂה מַעֲשֵׂה בְרֵאשִׁית:
<M in>Upon hearing thunder, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>for His strength and His power fill the universe.
<M h> שֶׁכֹּחוֹ וּגְבוּרָתוֹ מָלֵא עוֹלָם:
<M in>When seeing a rainbow say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who remembers the covenant,
<M h> זוֹכֵר הַבְּרִית
<M e>is faithful to His covenant
<M h> וְנֶאֱמָן בִּבְרִיתוֹ
<M e>and fulfills His word.
<M h> וְקַיָּם בְּמַאֲמָרוֹ:
<M in>When seeing great seas, or tall mountains which are famous for their great height, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who makes the work of Creation.
<M h> עוֹשֵׂה מַעֲשֵׂה בְרֵאשִׁית:
<M in>Upon seeing a place where you had experienced a life-saving miracle, you should say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who performed a miracle for me at this place.
<M h> שֶׁעָֽשָׂה לִּי נֵס בַּמָּקוֹם הַזֶּה:
<M in>Upon seeing a place where your parents or ancestors were miraculously saved, say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who performed a miracle
<M h> שֶׁעָֽשָׂה נֵס
<M e>for my mother/my father
<M h> לְאָבִי/לְאִמִּי
<M e>at this place.
<M h> בַּמָּקוֹם הַזֶּה:

<@01>Marriage Service
<@01>ברכות אירוסין ונשואין
<M in>The following berachos are said under the marriage canopy<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the vine.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הַגָּֽפֶן:
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who has sanctified us
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָֽׁנוּ
<M e>with His commandments
<M h> בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ
<M e>regarding forbidden sexual relationships
<M h> עַל הָֽעֲרָיוֹת,
<M e>and forbade to us
<M h> וְאָֽסַר לָֽנוּ
<M e>betrothed women,
<M h> אֶת הָאֲרוּסוֹת,
<M e>and permitted to us [those women]
<M h> וְהִתִּיר לָֽנוּ
<M e>who are married to us
<M h> אֶת הַנְּשׂוּאוֹת לָֽנוּ
<M e>by means of the <i>chupah</i> and consecration.
<M h> עַל-יְדֵי חֻפָּה וְקִדּוּשִׁין.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>Who sanctified His people Israel
<M h> מְקַדֵּשׁ עַמּוֹ יִשְׂרָאֵל
<M e>through the <i>chupah</i> and consecration.
<M h> עַל-יְדֵי חֻפָּה וְקִדּוּשִׁין:
<M in>Both the groom and the bride drink from the cup.<FC>
The groom then consecrates his bride to him with a ring,<FC>
in the presence of two appropriate witnesses, and says:<FC>
<M t2>You are hereby
<M h> הֲרֵי אַתְּ
<M e>consecrated to me
<M h> מְקֻדֶּֽשֶׁת לִי
<M e>with this ring
<M h> בְּטַבַּֽעַת זוּ,
<M e>according to the rite of
<M h> כְּדַת
<M e>Moses and Israel.
<M h> מֹשֶׁה וְיִשְׂרָאֵל:
<M in>The kesubah (marriage contract) is read,<FC>
after which the groom presents it to the bride.<FC>
A second cup of wine is poured, and the following "Seven Berachos" are recited.<FC>
<M t1>1. Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the vine.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הַגָּֽפֶן:
<M in>After Birkas Hamazon the "Seven Berachos" begin here,<FC>
and are followed by number 1 above.<FC>
<M t2>2. Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who created everything for His glory.
<M h> שֶׁהַכֹּל בָּרָא לִכְבוֹדוֹ:
<M t1>3. Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Former of man.
<M h> יוֹצֵר הָאָדָם:
<M t1>4. Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who formed man (Adam) in His image,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר יָצַר אֶת הָאָדָם בְּצַלְמוֹ,
<M e>in the image of His likeness;
<M h> בְּצֶּֽלֶם דְּמוּת תַּבְנִיתוֹ,
<M e>and fashioned for him out of his very self
<M h> וְהִתְקִין לוֹ מִמֶּֽנּוּ
<M e>a building (a wife: Eve) for eternity.
<M h> בִּנְיַן עֲדֵי עַד.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה,
<M e>Former of Man.
<M h> יוֹצֵר הָאָדָם:
<M t1>5. May the barren one<M tnt> be happy and exult
<M h> שׂוֹשׂ תָּשִׂישׂ וְתָגֵל הָעֲקָרָה,
<M e>with the ingathering of her children
<M h> בְּקִבּוּץ בָּנֶֽיהָ
<M e>into her midst with joy.
<M h> לְתוֹכָהּ בְּשִׂמְחָה.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה,
<M e>Who gladdens Zion through her children.
<M h> מְשַׂמֵּֽחַ צִיּוֹן בְּבָנֶֽיהָ:
<M t1>6. Grant abundant joy
<M h> שַׂמֵּֽחַ תְּשַׂמַּח
<M e>to these beloved companions,
<M h> רֵעִים הָאֲהוּבִים,
<M e>as You gladdened Your created being
<M h> כְּשַׂמֵּחֲךָ יְצִירְךָ
<M e>in the Garden of Eden of old.
<M h> בְּגַן עֵֽדֶן מִקֶּֽדֶם.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה,
<M e>Who gladdens groom and bride.
<M h> מְשַׂמֵּֽחַ חָתָן וְכַלָּה:
<M t1>7. Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who created happiness and joy,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר בָּרָא שָׂשׂוֹן וְשִׂמְחָה,
<M e>groom and bride, exultation, song,
<M h> חָתָן וְכַלָּה, גִּילָה רִנָּה,
<M e>pleasure, delight, love, brotherhood,
<M h> דִּיצָה וְחֶדְוָה, אַהֲבָה וְאַחֲוָה,
<M e>peace and companionship.
<M h> וְשָׁלוֹם וְרֵעוּת.
<M e>Soon, Adonoy, our God, may there be heard
<M h> מְהֵרָה יְהוָֹה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ יִשָּׁמַע
<M e>in the cities of Judah
<M h> בְּעָרֵי יְהוּדָה
<M e>and in the streets of Jerusalem
<M h> וּבְחוּצוֹת יְרוּשָׁלָֽיִם,
<M e>the sound of happiness and the sound of joy,
<M h> קוֹל שָׂשׂוֹן, וְקוֹל שִׂמְחָה,
<M e>the sound of the groom
<M h> קוֹל חָתָן
<M e>and sound of the bride,
<M h> וְקוֹל כַּלָּה,
<M e>the sound of grooms’ jubilation
<M h> קוֹל מִצְהֲלוֹת חֲתָנִים
<M e>from their <I>chupah,</I>
<M h> מֵחֻפָּתָם,
<M e>and of the youths from their feasts of song.
<M h> וּנְעָרִים מִמִּשְׁתֵּה נְגִינָתָם.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה,
<M e>Who gladdens the groom with the bride.
<M h> מְשַׂמֵּֽחַ חָתָן עִם הַכַּלָּה:
<@01>Birchas Hamazon for Sheva Berachos
<@01>ברכת המזון לשבע ברכות
<M in>The leader begins:<FC>
<M t2>Gentlemen, let us say the blessing.
<M h> רַבּוֹתַי נְבָרֵךְ:
<M in>The others respond:<FC>
<M t2>The Name of Adonoy will be blessed
<M h> יְהִי שֵׁם יְיָ מְבֹרָךְ
<M e>from now forever.
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם:
<M in>The leader repeats:<FC>
<M t2>The Name of Adonoy will be blessed
<M h> יְהִי שֵׁם יְיָ מְבֹרָךְ
<M e>from now forever.
<M h> מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם:
<M in>and proceeds:<FC>
<M t2>Banish sorrow and fury too
<M h> דְּוַי הָסֵר וְגַם חָרוֹן,
<M e>and then the mute will exult in song.
<M h> וְאָז אִלֵּם בְּשִׁיר יָרוֹן,
<M e>Guide us in the paths of righteousness.
<M h> נְחֵֽנוּ בְּמַעְגְּ֒לֵי צֶֽדֶק,
<M e>Heed the blessing of the children of Jeshurun
<M h> שְׁעֵה בִּרְכַּת )בְּנֵי יְשֻׁרוּן(
<M e>(and) the sons of Aaron.<M tnt>

<M t1>With your permission
<M h> בִּרְשׁוּת
<M e>our masters and teachers,
<M h> מָרָנָן וְרַבָּנָן וְרַבּוֹתַי
<M e>let us bless our God,
<M h> נְבָרֵךְ אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>in Whose abode is joy<M tnt>
<M h> שֶׁהַשִּׁמְחָה בִּמְעוֹנוֹ
<M e>for we have eaten of His bounty.
<M h> )וְ(שֶׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ:
<M in>The others respond:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed is our God
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>in Whose abode is joy
<M h> שֶׁהַשִּׁמְחָה בִּמְעוֹנוֹ
<M e>for we have eaten of His bounty
<M h> )וְ(שֶׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ
<M e>and through His goodness we live.
<M h> וּבְטוּבוֹ חָיִֽינוּ:
<M in>The leader repeats:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed is our God,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ
<M e>in Whose abode is joy
<M h> שֶׁהַשִּׁמְחָה בִּמְעוֹנוֹ
<M e>[and] we have eaten of His bounty
<M h> )וְ(שֶׁאָכַֽלְנוּ מִשֶּׁלּוֹ
<M e>and through His goodness we live.
<M h> וּבְטוּבוֹ חָיִֽינוּ:
<M in>Recite Birchas Hamazon which begins on page 000.<FC>
<M fn><M fnt>The barren one refers to Jerusalem.
<M fnt>The blessing of the children of Jeshurun refers to the blessings recited by all Jews, whereas the blessings of the sons of Aaron refers to the special <I>Birkas Kohanim,</I> mentioned in Numbers, 6:24-26.
<M fnt>The phrase "in Whose abode is joy" is recited only when the meal is conducted with the decorum of sanctity, without the commingling of men and women. For there is no joy in God’s abode when commingling takes place.
<@01>Service at a Circumcision
<@01>סדר ברית מילה
<M in>Upon the arrival of the child, all those present at the service rise and say:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed is he that comes!
<M h> בָּרוּךְ הַבָּא:
<M in>The Mohel takes the child, and placing it upon a designated seat<FC>
which is called the Throne of Elijah and he says:<FC>
<M t2>This is the Throne of Elijah,
<M h> זֶה הַכִּסֵּא שֶׁל אֵלִיָּֽהוּ הַנָּבִיא
<M e>may he be remembered for good.
<M h> זָכוּר לַטּוֹב:
<M e>For Your deliverance I have hoped, Adonoy.
<M h> לִישׁוּעָתְךָ קִוּיתִי יְהוָֹה:
<M e>I have longed for Your deliverance, Adonoy;
<M h> שִׂבַּרְתִּי לִישׁוּעָתְךָ יְהוָֹה,
<M e>and I have fulfilled Your commandments.
<M h> וּמִצְוֹתֶֽיךָ עָשִׂיתִי:
<M e>Elijah, messenger of the circumcision!
<M h> אֵלִיָֽהוּ מַלְאַךְ הַבְּרִית,
<M e>Behold, yours is now before you,
<M h> הִנֵּה שֶׁלְךָ לְפָנֶֽיךָ,
<M e>stand at my right hand and support me.
<M h> עֲמוֹד עַל יְמִינִי וְסָמְכֵֽנִי.
<M e>I have longed for Your deliverance.
<M h> שִׂבַּֽרְתִּי לִישׁוּעָתְךָ יְהוָֹה.
<M e>I am happy with Your word
<M h> שָׂשׂ אָנֹכִי עַל אִמְרָתֶֽךָ,
<M e>like one who finds great gain.
<M h> כְּמוֹצֵא שָׁלָל רָב.
<M e>Great is the peace
<M h> שָׁלוֹם רָב
<M e>of those who love Your Torah,
<M h> לְאֹהֲבֵי תוֹרָתֶֽךָ,
<M e>and there is no stumbling for them.
<M h> וְאֵין לָֽמוֹ מִכְשׁוֹל,
<M e>Fortunate is he whom You choose
<M h> אַשְׁרֵי תִּבְחַר
<M e>and bring near,
<M h> וּתְקָרֵב
<M e>that he may dwell in Your courts.
<M h> יִשְׁכּוֹן חֲצֵרֶֽיךָ,
<M in>All those present respond:<FC>
<M t2>May we be satisfied
<M h> נִשְׂבְּעָה
<M e>with the goodness of Your House,
<M h> בְּטוּב בֵּיתֶֽךָ,
<M e>the holy place of Your Sanctuary.
<M h> קְדוֹשׁ הֵיכָלֶֽךָ:
<M in>Before the Mohel performs the circumcision, the father of the child says:<FC>
<M t2>Behold, I am prepared and ready
<M h> הִנְנִי מוּכָן וּמְזוּמָן
<M e>to fulfill the positive commandment
<M h> לְקַיֵּם מִצְוַת עֲשֵׂה
<M e>commanded me by the Creator, blessed is He,
<M h> שֶׁצִוּנִי הַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ
<M e>to circumcise my son.
<M h> לָמוֹל אֶת בְּנִי:
<M in>The Mohel takes the child and proclaims:<FC>
<M t2>The Holy One, blessed is He, said
<M h> אָמַר הַקָּדוֹשׁ בָּרוּךְ הוּא
<M e>to our father, Abraham,
<M h> לְאַבְרָהָם אָבִֽינוּ,
<M e>"Walk before me and be perfect."
<M h> הִתְהַלֵּךְ לְפָנַי וֶהְיֵה תָמִים.
<M e>Behold, I am prepared and ready
<M h> הִנְנִי מוּכָן וּמְזֻמָּן
<M e>to fulfill the positive commandment
<M h> לְקַיֵּם מִצְוַת עֲשֵׂה
<M e>that the Creator, blessed is He,
<M h> שֶׁצִּוּנוּ הַבּוֹרֵא יִתְבָּרַךְ
<M e>commanded us to circumcise.
<M h> לָמוֹל:
<M in>The Mohel places the child upon the knees of the Sandek,<FC>
and before performing the actual circumcision, he says:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָֽׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ
<M e>concerning the circumcision.
<M h> עַל הַמִּילָה:
<M in>As the Mohel performs the act of circumcision the father of the child says:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּשָֽׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us to bring him
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ לְהַכְנִיסוֹ
<M e>into the covenant of our father, Abraham.
<M h> בִּבְרִיתוֹ שֶׁל אַבְרָהָם אָבִֽינוּ:
<M in>All those present proclaim:<FC>
<M t2>Amein!
<M h> אָמֵן.
<M e>Even as he has entered into the covenant,
<M h> כְּשֵׁם שֶׁנִּכְנַס לַבְּרִית,
<M e>so may he enter into the [study of] Torah,
<M h> כֵּן יִכָּנֵס לְתּוֹרָה
<M e><I>chupah</I> [the nuptial canopy], and good deeds.
<M h> וּלְחֻפָּה וּלְמַעֲשִׂים טוֹבִים:
<M in>One of the distinguished relatives or guests is given the honor<FC>
of reciting the following Berachos:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the vine.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הַגָּֽפֶן:
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified [Isaac] the beloved one,
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדַּשׁ יְדִיד
<M e>from birth,
<M h> מִבֶּֽטֶן,
<M e>and set Your statute in his flesh,
<M h> וְחוֹק בִּשְׁאֵֽרוֹ שָׂם,
<M e>and sealed his offspring
<M h> וְצֶאֱצָאָיו חָתַם
<M e>with the sign of the holy covenant.
<M h> בְּאוֹת בְּרִית קֽוֹדֶשׁ,
<M e>Therefore, on this account,
<M h> עַל כֵּן בִּשְׂכַר זֹאת,
<M e>living Almighty, our Portion, our Rock,
<M h> אֵל חַי חֶלְקֵֽנוּ צוּרֵֽנוּ,
<M e>give the command to rescue
<M h> צַוּה לְהַצִּיל
<M e>the beloved soul within our flesh
<M h> יְדִידוּת שְׁאֵרֵֽנוּ
<M e>from destruction,
<M h> מִשַּֽׁחַת.
<M e>for the sake of His covenant
<M h> לְמַֽעַן בְּרִיתוֹ
<M e>that He has set in our flesh.
<M h> אֲשֶׁר שָׂם בִּבְשָׂרֵֽנוּ.
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,

<@01>Redemption of the Firstborn
<@01>סדר פדיון הבן
<M ex><EM><EN>The first born male child must be redeemed on the thirty-first day of his birth. If, however, the father is a <I>Kohein</I> or a Levite, or the mother a daughter of a <I>Kohein</I> or a Levite, they are exempt from the duty of redemption. Should the thirty-first day fall on a Shabbos or Yom Tov, the service is postponed until the next day.<FL>
<M in>The father, presenting his child to the Kohein,<FC>
makes the following declaration:<FC>
<M t2>This, my first born son,
<M h> זֶה בְּנִי בְּכוֹרִי
<M e>is the first issue of his mother’s womb,
<M h> וְהוּא פֶּטֶר רֶחֶם לְאִמוֹ,
<M e>and the Holy One, blessed is He
<M h> וְהַקָדוֹשׁ בָּרוּךְ הוּא
<M e>has commanded to redeem him,
<M h> צִוָה לִפְדוֹתוֹ,
<M e>as it is said:
<M h> שֶׁנֶאֱמַר,
<M e>"And those that are to be redeemed of them,
<M h> וּפְדוּיָו
<M e>from a month old shall you redeem them,
<M h> מִבֶּן חוֹדֶשׁ תִּפְדֶה
<M e>according to your estimation,
<M h> בְּעֶרְכְּךָ
<M e>for the money of five silver <I>shekalim,</I>
<M h> כֶּסֶף חֲמֵשֶׁת שְׁקָלִים
<M e>of the <I>shekel</I> of the Sanctuary
<M h> בְּשֶׁקֶל הַקוֹדֶשׁ
<M e>which is equal to twenty <I>geirah.</I>"<M tnt>
<M h> עֶשְׂרִים גֵרָה הוּא.
<M e>And it is said:
<M h> וְנֶאֱמַר,
<M e>"Sanctify unto me all the firstborn,
<M h> קַדֶשׁ לִי כָל בְּכוֹר
<M e>whatsoever opens the womb
<M h> פֶּטֶר כָּל רֶחֶם
<M e>among the Children of Israel,
<M h> בִּבְנֵי יִשְׂרָאֵל
<M e>both of man and of beast is Mine."<M tnt>
<M h> בָּאָדָם וּבַבְּהֵמָה, לִי הוּא:
<M in>The father then places before the </I>Kohein<I> silver dollars in the amount of five</I>shekalim<I> which is equal to five silver dollars, or according to some </I>Poskim<I> seven silver dollars, and the </I>Kohein<I> asks:<FC>
<M t2>"Which do you prefer,
<M h> מַה בָּעִית טְפֵי
<M e>to give me your firstborn son
<M h> לִיתֵּן לִי בִּנְךָ בְּכוֹרֶךָ
<M e>who is the first issue of his mother’s womb,
<M h> שֶׁהוּא פֶּטֶר רֶחֶם לְאִמוֹ,
<M e>or would you rather redeem him
<M h> אוֹ בָּעִית לִפְדוֹתוֹ
<M e>for five <I>shekalim,</I>
<M h> בְּעַד חָמֵשׁ סְלָעִים
<M e>as you are required to do by the Torah?"
<M h> כְּדִמְחֻיַּבְתָּ מִדְאוֹרַיְיתָא:
<M in>The father replies:<FC>
<M t2>I wish to redeem my son
<M h> חָפֵץ אֲנִי לִפְדוֹת אֶת בְּנִי
<M e>and here is the value of his redemption
<M h> וְהֵילָךְ דְמֵי פִדְיוֹנוֹ
<M e>which I am required to give
<M h> כְּדִמְחֻיַּבְתִּי
<M e>according to the Torah.
<M h> מִדְאוֹרַייְתָא:
<M in>While holding the silver dollars, the father says these two Berachos:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְשָׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us concerning
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ
<M e>the redemption of the [firstborn] son.
<M h> עַל פִּדְיוֹן הַבֵּן:
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who has kept us alive and sustained us
<M h> שֶׁהֶחֱיָנוּ וְקִיְמָנוּ
<M e>and brought us to this time.
<M h> וְהִגִיעָנוּ, לַזְמַן הַזֶה:
<M in>The Kohein accepts the silver dollars,<FC>
and holding it over the head of the child, says:<FC>
<M t2>This is instead of that,
<M h> זֶה תַּחַת זֶה
<M e>this is in exchange for that,
<M h> זֶה חִלּוּף זֶה
<M e>this is pardoned for that.
<M h> זֶה מָחוּל עַל זֶה.
<M e>May this child enter into life,
<M h> וְיִכָּנֵס זֶה הַבֵּן לְחַיִּים,
<M e>into the [study of] Torah,
<M h> לְתּוֹרָה
<M e><I>chupah</I> [the nuptial canopy] and good deeds.
<M h> וּלְחֻפָּה וּלְמַעֲשִׂים טוֹבִים,
<M e>Amein.
<M h> אָמֵן:
<M in>The Kohein places his right hand upon the head of the child<FC>
and blesses him:<FC>
<M t2>May God make you
<M h> יְשִׂמְךָ אֱלֺהִים
<M e>as Ephraim and Menashe.
<M h> כְּאֶפְרַיִם וְכִמְנַשֶּׁה.
<M e>Adonoy bless you and guard you.
<M h> יְבָרֶכְךָ יְהוָֹה וְיִשְׁמְרֶֽךָ.
<M e>Adonoy shine His countenance upon you
<M h> יָאֵר יְהוָֹה פָּנָיו אֵלֶֽיךָ
<M e>and be gracious unto you.
<M h> וִיחֻנֶּֽךָּ.
<M e>Adonoy turn His countenance toward you
<M h> יִשָּׁא יְהוָֹה פָּנָיו אֵלֶֽיךָ
<M e>and grant you peace.
<M h> וְיָשֵׂם לְךָ שָׁלוֹם.
<M e>Adonoy is your guardian;
<M h> יְהוָֹה שֹׁמְרֶֽךָ
<M e>Adonoy is your shelter at your right hand.
<M h> יְהוָֹה צִלְּךָ עַל יַד יְמִינֶֽךָ.
<M e>For length of days
<M h> כִּי אוֹרֶךְ יָמִים
<M e>and years of life and peace,
<M h> וּשְׁנוֹת חַיִּים וְשָׁלוֹם
<M e>will He add to you.
<M h> יוֹסִֽיפוּ לָךְ.
<M e>Adonoy will guard you from all evil,
<M h> יְהוָֹה יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל רָע,
<M e>He will preserve your soul.
<M h> יִשְׁמוֹר אֶת נַפְשֶֽׁךָ:
<M in>The Kohein hands the child to the father.<FC>
The Kohein then takes a cup of wine and says:<FC>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם,
<M e>Who creates the fruit of the vine.
<M h> בּוֹרֵא פְּרִי הַגָּֽפֶן:

<@01>The Travelers’ Prayer
<@01>תפלת הדרך
<M e><M t1>May it be Your will
<M h> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְפָנֶֽיךָ,
<M e>Adonoy, our God, and God of our fathers,
<M h> יְהוָֹה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ וֵאלֺהֵי אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ,
<M e>that you lead us to peace,
<M h> שֶׁתּוֹלִיכֵֽנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם,
<M e>incline our footsteps to peace,
<M h> וְתַצְעִידֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם,
<M e>guide us to peace,
<M h> וְתַדְרִיכֵֽנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם,
<M e>and cause us to reach our desired destination
<M h> וְתַגִיעֵֽנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵֽנוּ
<M e>for life, for joy and for peace.
<M h> לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם,
<M e>Rescue us from the grasp of every foe,
<M h> וְתַצִּילֵֽנוּ מִכַּף כָּל אוֹיֵב
<M e>ambush, bandits, and vicious animals
<M h> וְאוֹרֵב וְלִסְטִים וְחַיּוֹת רָעוֹת
<M e>along the way,
<M h> בַּדֶרֶךְ
<M e>and from all forms of punishment
<M h> וּמִכָּל מִינֵי פוּרְעָנִיוֹת
<M e>that rage upon the world.
<M h> הַמִּתְרַגְשׁוֹת לָבוֹא לָעוֹלָם.
<M e>Send blessing in all our work,
<M h> וְתִשְׁלַח בְּרָכָה בְּמַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵינוּ.
<M e>and grant us favor, kindness, and compassion
<M h> וְתִתְּנֵנוּ לְחֵן וּלְחֶסֶד וּלְרַחֲמִים
<M e>in Your eyes,
<M h> בְּעֵינֶֽךָ
<M e>and in the eyes of all who see us.
<M h> וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רוֹאֵֽינוּ.
<M e>Hear the sound of our supplication,
<M h> וְתִשְׁמַע קוֹל תַּחֲנוּנֵֽינוּ,
<M e>for You are Almighty
<M h> כִּי אֵל
<M e>Who hears prayer and supplication.
<M h> שׁוֹמֵעַ תְּפִלָה וְתַחֲנוּן אָתָּה:
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהוָֹה,
<M e>Who hears prayer.
<M h> שׁוֹמֵעַ תְּפִלָּה:
<M in>Recite these verses three times:<FC>
<M t2>"And Jacob went on his way,
<M h> וְיַעֲקֹב הָלַךָ לְדַרְכוֹ,
<M e>and angels of God met him.
<M h> וִַיּפְגְּעוּ בוֹ מַלְאֲכֵי אֱלֺהִים.
<M e>And Jacob said when he saw them,
<M h> וַיֹּֽאמֶר יַעֲקֹב כַּאֲשֶׁר רָאָם,
<M e>‘This is God’s host.’
<M h> מַחֲנֵה אֱלֺהִים זֶה,
<M e>And he called
<M h> וַיִּקְרָא
<M e>the name of the place <I>Machanayim.</I>"<M tnt>
<M h> שֵׁם הַמָּקוֹם הַהוּא מַחֲנָֽיִם:
<M in>Recite these verses three times:<FC>
<M t2>For Your deliverance, I hope, Adonoy.<M tnt>

<M e>I hope, Adonoy, for Your deliverance.

<M t2>Behold, I send an angel before you,
<M h> הִנֵּה אָנֹכִי שֹׁלֵחַ מַלְאָךְ לְפָנֶֽיךָ

<@01>Mincha

<@01>תפלת מעריב
Counting the Omer
ספירת העומר
<M ex><EM><EN>The Omer is counted from the second night of Pesach until the night before Shavuos. The counting of forty-nine days (seven weeks) between the Festival of Pesach and Shavuos (the Feast of Weeks), connects the exodus from Egypt with the festival of the giving of the Torah. Just as one who awaits a most intimate friend on a certain day counts the days in eager anticipation of his arrival, so do we count the days from our liberation till the day we receive the Torah, which is the culmination and fulfillment of our freedom.<FL>
<EM><EN>It is proper to count the Omer at the beginning of the night, usually after the Maariv Service, and the Omer should be counted while standing.<FL>
<M t2>I am prepared and ready to perform
<M h> <M reg> הִנְ֒נִי מוּכָן וּמְזֻמָּן לְקַיֵּם
<M e>the affirmative command to count the Omer,
<M h> מִצְוַת עֲשֵׂה שֶׁל סְפִירַת הָעֹֽמֶר
<M e>as it is written in the Torah,
<M h> כְּמוֹ שֶׁכָּתוּב בַּתּוֹרָה.
<M e>"And you shall count for yourselves,
<M h> וּסְפַרְתֶּם לָכֶם
<M e>from the day after the day of rest,
<M h> מִמָּחֳרַת הַשַּׁבָּת
<M e>from the day you bring
<M h> מִיּוֹם הֲבִיאֲכֶם
<M e>the <i>omer</i> as the wave-offering,
<M h> אֶת עֹֽמֶר הַתְּ֒נוּפָה
<M e>seven complete weeks shall there be;
<M h> שֶֽׁבַע שַׁבָּתוֹת תְּמִימוֹת תִּהְיֶֽינָה:
<M e>until the day following the seventh week
<M h> עַד מִמָּחֳרַת הַשַּׁבָּת הַשְּׁ֒בִיעִית
<M e>shall you count fifty days;
<M h> תִּסְפְּ֒רוּ חֲמִשִּׁים יוֹם
<M e>and you shall bring a
<M h> וְהִקְרַבְתֶּם
<M e>new meal-offering unto Adonoy."
<M h> מִנְחָה חֲדָשָׁה לַיהוָֹה:
<M e><M t1>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהֹוָה
<M e>our God, King of the universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם
<M e>Who sanctified us with His commandments
<M h> אֲשֶׁר קִדְּ֒שָֽׁנוּ בְּמִצְוֹתָיו
<M e>and commanded us to count the Omer.
<M h> וְצִוּנוּ עַל סְפִירַת הָעֹֽמֶר:
<M long> <EN> 1. הַיּוֹם יוֹם אֶחָד בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 2. הַיּוֹם שְׁנֵי יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 3. הַיּוֹם שְׁלשָׁה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 4. הַיּוֹם אַרְבָּעָה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 5. הַיּוֹם חֲמִשָּׁה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 6. הַיּוֹם שִׁשָּׁה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 7. הַיּוֹם שִׁבְעָה יָמִים שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 8. הַיּוֹם שְׁמוֹנָה יָמִים שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד וְיוֹם אֶחָד בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
<EN> 9. הַיּוֹם תִּשְׁעָה יָמִים שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד וּשְׁנֵי יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
01. הַיּוֹם עֲשָׂרָה יָמִים שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד וּשְׁלשָׁה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
11. הַיּוֹם אַחַד עָשָׂר יוֹם שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד וְאַרְבָּעָה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
21. הַיּוֹם שְׁנֵים עָשָׂר יוֹם שֶׁהֵם שָׁבֽוּעַ אֶחָד וַחֲמִשָּׁה יָמִים בָּעֹֽמֶר: <FR>
