<M t2>The Merciful One, may He return for us
<M h> הָרַחֲמָן הוּא יַחֲזִיר לָנוּ
<M e>the service of the Beis Hamikdash in its place
<M h> עֲבוֹדַת בֵּית הַמִּקְדָּשׁ לִמְקוֹמָה
<M e>speedily in our days, Amein, <i>Selah.</i>
<M h> בִּמְהֵרָה בְּיָמֵֽינוּ אָמֵן סֶֽלָה:
<M in>Psalm 67<FC>
<M t2>To Him, Who grants victory:<M tnt>
<M h> לַמְ֒נַצֵּֽחַ
<M e>a psalm with instrumental music, a song.
<M h> בִּנְגִינוֹת מִזְמוֹר שִׁיר:
<M e>[May] God favor us and bless us,
<M h> אֱלֺהִים יְחָנֵּֽנוּ וִיבָרְ֒כֵֽנוּ
<M e>[may He] cause His countenance to shine
<M h> יָאֵר פָּנָיו
<M e>among us forever;
<M h> אִתָּֽנוּ סֶֽלָה:
<M e>[so] that Your way become known on earth,
<M h> לָדַֽעַת בָּאָֽרֶץ דַּרְכֶּֽךָ
<M e>[and] Your deliverance among all nations.
<M h> בְּכָל גּוֹיִם יְשׁוּעָתֶֽךָ:
<M e>Peoples will thank You, God,
<M h> יוֹדֽוּךָ עַמִּים אֱלֺהִים
<M e>all the peoples will thank You.
<M h> יוֹדֽוּךָ עַמִּים כֻּלָּם:
<M e>Nations will rejoice and sing
<M h> יִשְׂמְ֒חוּ וִירַנְּ֒נוּ לְאֻמִּים
<M e>when You judge the peoples justly,
<M h> כִּי תִשְׁפּוֹט עַמִּים מִישׁוֹר
<M e>and lead the nations upon the earth forever.
<M h> וּלְאֻמִּים בָּאָֽרֶץ תַּנְחֵם סֶֽלָה:
<M e>Peoples will thank You, God,
<M h> יוֹדֽוּךָ עַמִּים אֱלֺהִים
<M e>all the peoples will thank You.
<M h> יוֹדֽוּךָ עַמִּים כֻּלָּם:
<M e>The earth will have yielded its produce;
<M h> אֶֽרֶץ נָתְ֒נָה יְבוּלָהּ
<M e>God, our God, will have blessed us.
<M h> יְבָרְ֒כֵֽנוּ אֱלֺהִים אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ:
<M e>God will bless us,
<M h> יְבָרְ֒כֵֽנוּ אֱלֺהִים
<M e>and they will fear Him---
<M h> וְיִירְ֒אוּ אוֹתוֹ
<M e>all [men even from] the ends of the earth.
<M h> כָּל אַפְסֵי אָֽרֶץ:
<M t1>Please, by the force of Your great right hand,
<M h> אָֽנָּא בְּכֹֽחַ גְּדֻלַּת יְמִינְ֒ךָ
<M e>release the bound one.
<M h> תַּתִּיר צְרוּרָה:
<M e>Accept the prayer of Your people;
<M h> קַבֵּל רִנַּת עַמְּ֒ךָ
<M e>strengthen us, purify us, awesome One!
<M h> שַׂגְּ֒בֵֽנוּ טַהֲרֵֽנוּ נוֹרָא:
<M e>Please mighty One---
<M h> נָא גִבּוֹר
<M e>those who seek Your unity---
<M h> דּוֹרְ֒שֵׁי יִחוּדְ֒ךָ
<M e>preserve them like the apple [of Your eye.]
<M h> כְּבָבַת שָׁמְרֵם:
<M e>Bless them,
<M h> בָּרְכֵם
<M e>purify them, have mercy on them;
<M h> טַהֲרֵם רַחֲמֵם
<M e>Your benevolent righteousness
<M h> צִדְקָתְ֒ךָ
<M e>[may You] always bestow upon them.
<M h> תָּמִיד גָּמְלֵם:
<M e>Mighty, Holy One
<M h> חֲסִין קָדוֹשׁ
<M e>in Your abundant goodness
<M h> בְּרֹב טוּבְ֒ךָ
<M e>lead Your community.
<M h> נַהֵל עֲדָתֶֽךָ:
<M e>Unique One, Exalted, turn to Your people
<M h> יָחִיד גֵּאֶה לְעַמְּ֒ךָ פְּנֵה
<M e>who are mindful of Your holiness.
<M h> זוֹכְ֒רֵי קְדֻשָּׁתֶֽךָ:
<M e>Accept our prayer and hear our cry,
<M h> שַׁוְעָתֵֽנוּ קַבֵּל וּשְׁמַע צַעֲקָתֵֽנוּ
<M e>[You] Who knows hidden thoughts.
<M h> יוֹדֵֽעַ תַּעֲלוּמוֹת:
<M e>Blessed [is His] Name,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ שֵׁם
<M e>Whose glorious Kingdom
<M h> כְּבוֹד מַלְכוּתוֹ
<M e>is forever and ever.
<M h> לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M t1>Master of the universe,
<M h> רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל עוֹלָם
<M e>You commanded us
<M h> אַתָּה צִוּיתָֽנוּ
<M e>through the hands of Your servant, Moses,
<M h> עַל יְדֵי משֶׁה עַבְדֶּֽךָ
<M e>to count the Omer
<M h> לִסְפֹּר סְפִירַת הָֽעֹמֶר
<M e>in order to purify us
<M h> כְּדֵי לְטַהֲרֵֽנוּ
<M e>from our evil and defilement.
<M h> מִקְּ֒לִפּוֹתֵֽינוּ וּמִטֻּמְאוֹתֵֽינוּ
<M e>As You have written in Your Torah:
<M h> כְּמוֹ שֶׁכָּתַֽבְתָּ בְּתוֹרָתֶֽךָ
<M e>"And you shall count for yourselves,
<M h> וּסְפַרְתֶּם לָכֶם
<M e>from the day after the day of rest,
<M h> מִמָּחֳרַת הַשַּׁבָּת
<M e>from the day you bring
<M h> מִיּוֹם הֲבִיאֲכֶם
<M e>the <i>omer</i> as the wave-offering,
<M h> אֶת עֹֽמֶר הַתְּ֒נוּפָה
<M e>seven complete weeks, shall there be;
<M h> שֶֽׁבַע שַׁבָּתוֹת תְּמִימוֹת תִּהְיֶֽינָה
<M e>until the day following the seventh week
<M h> עַד מִמָּחֳרַת הַשַּׁבָּת הַשְּׁ֒בִיעִית
<M e>shall you count fifty days,"
<M h> תִּסְפְּ֒רוּ חֲמִשִּׁים יוֹם
<M e>in order to cleanse
<M h> כְּדֵי שֶׁיִּטָּהֲרוּ
<M e>the souls of Your people Israel
<M h> נַפְשׁוֹת עַמְּ֒ךָ יִשְׂרָאֵל
<M e>from their impurities.
<M h> מִזֻּהֲמָתָם:
<M e>Therefore, may it be Your will,
<M h> וּבְכֵן יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ
<M e>Adonoy, our God, and God of our fathers,
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ וֵאלֺהֵי אֲבוֹתֵֽינוּ
<M e>that in the merit of the Omer
<M h> שֶׁבִּזְכוּת סְפִירַת הָעֹֽמֶר
<M e>which I counted today,
<M h> שֶׁסָּפַֽרְתִּי הַיּוֹם
<M e>may any defect I have caused be rectified.
<M h> יְתֻקַּן מַה שֶּׁפָּגַֽמְתִּי בִּסְפִירָה
<M e>
<M h> <M small> )פלונית השייכת לאותו הלילה( <M reg>
<M e>May I be purified and sanctified
<M h> וְאֶטָּהֵר וְאֶתְקַדֵּשׁ
<M e>with sublime holiness,
<M h> בִּקְדֻשָּׁה שֶׁל מַֽעְלָה
<M e>and thereby
<M h> וְעַל יְדֵי זֶה
<M e>may abundant bounty be bestowed
<M h> יֻשְׁפַּע שֶֽׁפַע רַב
<M e>upon all the worlds.
<M h> בְּכָל הָעוֹלָמוֹת
<M e>May it rectify our being,
<M h> וּלְתַקֵּן אֶת נַפְשׁוֹתֵֽינוּ
<M e>our spirit and our souls
<M h> וְרוּחוֹתֵֽינוּ וְנִשְׁמוֹתֵֽינוּ
<M e>from every baseness and defect,
<M h> מִכָּל סִיג וּפְגָם
<M e>and may it purify us and sanctify us
<M h> וּלְטַהֲרֵֽנוּ וּלְקַדְּ֒שֵֽׁנוּ
<M e>with Your sublime holiness.
<M h> בִּקְדֻשָּׁתְ֒ךָ הָעֶלְיוֹנָה
<M e>Amen, Selah.
<M h> אָמֵן סֶֽלָה:
<lp><M fn><M fnt><i>Psalm</i> 67 is recited because the seven verses which follow the introductory verse contain 49 words corresponding to the seven weeks (49 days) that link Pesach to the giving of the Torah on Shavuos.<FL>
<@01>Prayer Before Retiring at Night
<@01>קריאת שמע על המטה
<M in>The following is Omitted on the Shabbat and Festivals.</I><FC>
<M t2>Master of the universe!
<M h> רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל-עוֹלָם <FL>
<M e>I hearby forgive
<M h> הֲרֵינִי מוֹחֵל <FL>
<M e>anyone who has angered me,
<M h> לְכָל-מִי שֶׁהִכְעִיס וְהִקְנִיט אוֹתִי <FL>
<M e>or sinned against me,
<M h> אוֹ שֶׁחָטָא כְּנֶגְדִי <FL>
<M e>either physically or financially,
<M h> בֵּין בְּגוּפִי בֵּין בְּמֶמוֹנִי <FL>
<M e>against my honor or anything that is mine,
<M h> בֵין בִּכְבוֹדִי בֵין בְכָל אֲשֶׁר לִי <FL>
<M e>whether accidentally or intentionally,
<M h> בֵין בְּאוֹנֶס בֵּין בְּרָצוֹן <FL>
<M e>inadvertently or deliberately,
<M h> בֵּין בְּשׁוֹגֵג בֵּין בְּמֵזִיד <FL>
<M e>by speech or by deed,
<M h> בֵין בְּדִבּוּר בֵּין בְּמַעֲשֶׂה <FL>
<M e>in this incarnation
<M h> בֵּין בְּגִלְגוּל זֶה <FL>
<M e>or in any other
<M h> בֵּין בְּגִלְגּוּל אַחֵר <FL>
<M e>any Israelite [is forgiven],
<M h> לְכָל-בַּר יִשְׂרָאֵל <FL>
<M e>may no man be punished on my account.
<M h> וְלֹא יֵעָנֵשׁ שׁוּם אָדָם בְסִבָּתִי <FL>
<M e>May it be Your will,
<M h> יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>Adonoy, my God and God of my fathers,
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֹהַי וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתַי <FL>
<M e>that I shall sin no more
<M h> שֶׁלֹּא אֶחְטֶא עוֹד <FL>
<M e>nor repeat my sins,
<M h> וְלֹא אֶחֱזוֹר בָּהֶם <FL>
<M e>neither shall I again anger You
<M h> וְלֹא אָשׁוּב עוֹד לְהַכְעִיסֶךָ <FL>
<M e>nor do what is wrong in Your eyes.
<M h> וְלֹא אֶעֱשֶׂה הָרַע בְּעֵינֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>The sins I have committed,
<M h> וּמַה-שֶׁחָטָֽאתִי <FL>
<M e>erase in your abounding mercies,
<M h> מְהוֹק בְּרַחֲמֶֽיךָ הָרַבִּים <FL>
<M e>but not through suffering or severe illnesses.
<M h> וְלֹא עַל יְדֵי יִסּוּרִים וָחֳלֶיִם רָעִים: <FL>
<M e>May they be acceptable
<M h> יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן <FL>
<M e>the words of my mouth
<M h> אִמְרֵי-פִי <FL>
<M e>and the thoughts of my heart, before You
<M h> וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבִּי לְפָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>Adonoy, my Rock and my Redeemer.
<M h> יְהֹוָה צוּרִי וְגֹאֲלִי: <FL>
<M t2>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> <M newbold> בָּרוּךְ <M reg> אַתָּה יְהֹוָה <FL>
<M e>our God, King of the Universe,
<M h> אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ מֶֽלֶךְ הָעוֹלָם <FL>
<M e>Who causes the fetters of sleep to fall
<M h> הַמַּפִּיל חֶבְלֵי שֵׁנָה <FL>
<M e>upon my eyes,
<M h> עַל עֵינָי <FL>
<M e>and slumber upon my eyelids.
<M h> וּתְנוּמָה עַל עַפְעַפָּי: <FL>
<M e>And illuminates the pupil of the eye.
<M h> וּמֵאִיר לְאִישׁוֹן בַּת עָיִן. <FL>
<M e>May it be Your will,
<M h> וִיהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּ֒פָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>Adonoy, my God and God of my fathers
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהַי וֵאלֺהֵי אֲבוֹתַי <FL>
<M e>to make me lie down in peace,
<M h> שֶׁתַּשְׁכִּיבֵֽנִי לְשָׁלוֹם <FL>
<M e>and to raise me (again)
<M h> וְתַעֲמִידֵֽנִי <FL>
<M e>to good life and peace,
<M h> לְחַיִים טוֹבִים וּלְשָׁלוֹם <FL>
<M e>and grant me my portion in Your Torah,
<M h> וְתֵן חֶלְקֵי בְּתוֹרָתֶךָ <FL>
<M e>make us accustomed to do Your commands,
<M h> וְתַרְגִילֵנוּ לִדְבַר מִצְוָה <FL>
<M e>and let us not become accustomed to sin,
<M h> וְעַל תַּרְגִילֵנוּ לִדְבַר עַבֵרָה <FL>
<M e>Do not bring us
<M h> וְאַל תְּבִיאֵֽנוּ <FL>
<M e>into the grasp of sin,
<M h> לֹא לִידֵי חֵטְא <FL>
<M e>Do not cause us to be tested,
<M h> וְלֹא לִידֵי נִסָּיוֹן <FL>
<M e>or brought to disgrace.
<M h> וְלֹא לִידֵי בִזָּיוֹן <FL>
<M e>May I be ruled by the Good Inclination
<M h> יִשׁלֹט בִּי יֵצֵר הַטוֹב <FL>
<M e>and let me not be ruled over
<M h> וְאַל יִשְׁלֹט <FL>
<M e>by the Evil Inclination.
<M h> יֵֽצֶר הָרָע <FL>
<M e>Protect me from Satan,
<M h> וְתַצִילֵנוּ מִשָׂטָן <FL>
<M e>from an evil mishap and from illnesses.
<M h> וּמִפֶגַע רָע וּמֵחָלָיִם רָעִים <FL>
<M e>Let my thoughts not terrify me---
<M h> וְאַל יְבַהֲלֽוּנִי רַעְיוֹנַי <FL>
<M e>nor evil dreams
<M h> וַחֲלוֹמוֹת רָעִים <FL>
<M e>or evil fancies (disturb me),
<M h> וְהַרְהוֹרִים רָעִים <FL>
<M e>and may my bed be perfect before You.<M tnt>
<M h> וּתְהֵא מִטָּתִי שְׁלֵמָה לְפָנֶֽיךָ: <FL>
<M e>And light up my eyes
<M h> וְהָאֵר עֵינַי <FL>
<M e>lest I sleep the sleep of death,
<M h> פֶּן אִישַׁן הַמָּֽוֶת. <FL>
<M e>Blessed are You, Adonoy,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְהֹוָה <FL>
<M e>Who illuminates the whole world
<M h> הַמֵּאִיר לָעוֹלָם כֻּלּוֹ <FL>
<M e>with His glory.
<M h> בִּכְבוֹדוֹ: <FL>
<M in>If one has prayed </I>Ma’ariv<I> and with it recited Sh’ma earlier than the ideal time for the evening Sh’ma, he should repeat all of it here. Some people have the custom of reciting all three paragraphs here every night.<FC>
<M t2>Almighty, faithful King
<M h> אֵל מֶֽלֶךְ נֶאֱמָן: <FL>
<M e>Hear, Israel
<M h> <M newbold> שְׁמַע <M reg> יִשְׂרָאֵל <FL>
<M e>Adonoy is our God
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ <FL>
<M e>Adonoy is One
<M h> יְהֹוָה אֶחָד: <FL>

<M t2>Blessed [is His] Name,
<M h> בָּרוּךְ שֵׁם
<M e>Whose glorious Kingdom
<M h> כְּבוֹד מַלְכוּתוֹ
<M e>is forever and ever.
<M h> לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד:
<M t2>And you shall love Adonoy, your God
<M h> <M newbold> וְאָהַבְתָּ <M reg> אֵת יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>with all your heart
<M h> בְּכָל-לְבָבְ֒ךָ <FL>
<M e>and with all your soul
<M h> וּבְכָל-נַפְשְׁ֒ךָ <FL>
<M e>and with all your possessions.
<M h> וּבְכָל-מְאֹדֶֽךָ: <FL>
<M e>And these words
<M h> וְהָיוּ הַדְּ֒בָרִים הָאֵֽלֶּה <FL>
<M e>which I command you today
<M h> אֲשֶׁר אָנֹכִי מְצַוּךָ הַיּוֹם <FL>
<M e>shall be upon your heart.
<M h> עַל-לְבָבֶֽךָ: <FL>
<M e>And you shall teach them sharply
<M h> וְשִׁנַּנְתָּם <FL>
<M e>to your children,
<M h> לְבָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>and you shall discuss them
<M h> וְדִבַּרְתָּ בָּם <FL>
<M e>when you sit in your house,
<M h> בְּשִׁבְתְּ֒ךָ בְּבֵיתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M e>and when you travel on the road,
<M h> וּבְלֶכְתְּ֒ךָ בַדֶּֽרֶךְ <FL>
<M e>and when you lie down and when you rise.
<M h> וּבְשָׁכְבְּ֒ךָ וּבְקוּמֶֽךָ: <FL>
<M e>And you shall bind them for a sign
<M h> וּקְשַׁרְתָּם לְאוֹת <FL>
<M e>upon your hand,
<M h> עַל-יָדֶֽךָ <FL>
<M e>and they shall be for <i>totafos</i>
<M h> וְהָיוּ לְטֹטָפֹת
<M e>between your eyes.
<M h> בֵּין עֵינֶֽיךָ: <FL>
<M e>And you shall write them
<M h> וּכְתַבְתָּם <FL>
<M e>upon the doorposts of your house
<M h> עַל-מְזֻזוֹת בֵּיתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M e>and upon your gateways.
<M h> וּבִשְׁעָרֶֽיךָ: <FL>
<M ex><EM><EN>If one has prayed <i>Maariv</i> and with it recited Shema earlier than the ideal time for the evening Shema, he should repeat all of it here. Some people have the custom of reciting all three paragraphs here every night.<FL>
<M t2>May the pleasantness of my Master, our God,
<M h> <M newbold> וִיהִי נֹֽעַם <M reg> אֲדֹנָי אֱלֺהֵֽינוּ <FL>
<M e>be upon us,<M tnt>
<M h> עָלֵֽינוּ <FL>
<M e>and the work of our hands establish for us
<M h> וּמַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵֽינוּ כּוֹנְ֒נָה עָלֵֽינוּ. <FL>
<M e>and the work of our hands may He establish.
<M h> וּמַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵֽינוּ כּוֹנְ֒נֵֽהוּ: <FL>
<M e>He who dwells
<M h> ישֵׁב <FL>
<M e>in the shelter of the Supreme One,
<M h> בְּסֵֽתֶר עֶלְיוֹן. <FL>
<M e>under the protection of Shadai He will abide.
<M h> בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן: <FL>
<M e>I say of Adonoy,
<M h> אֹמַר לַיהוָֹה <FL>
<M e>"[He is] my refuge and my stronghold,
<M h> מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי. <FL>
<M e>my God in Whom I trust.
<M h> אֱלֺהַי אֶבְטַח-בּוֹ: <FL>
<M e>For He will save you from the snare-trap,
<M h> כִּי הוּא יַצִּילְ֒ךָ מִפַּח יָקוּשׁ <FL>
<M e>from destructive pestilence.
<M h> מִדֶּֽבֶר הַוּוֹת: <FL>
<M e>With His wings He will cover you
<M h> בְּאֶבְרָתוֹ יָֽסֶךְ לָךְ <FL>
<M e>and beneath His wings, you will find refuge;
<M h> וְתַֽחַת-כְּנָפָיו תֶּחְסֶה. <FL>
<M e>His truth is a shield, a full shield.
<M h> צִנָּה וְסֹחֵרָה אֲמִתּוֹ: <FL>
<M e>You will not fear the terror of night,
<M h> לֺא-תִירָא מִפַּֽחַד לָֽיְלָה. <FL>
<M e>nor the arrow that flies by day,

<M h> קִוּיתִי יְהֹוָה לִישׁוּעָתְ֒ךָ <FL>
<M e>Adonoy, for Your deliverance I hope.
<M h> יְהֹוָה לִישׁוּעָתְ֒ךָ קִוּיתִי <FL>
<M t2>In the Name of Adonoy, God of Israel:
<M h> <M newbold> בְּשֵׁם <M reg> יְהֹוָה אֱלֺהֵי יִשְׂרָאֵל <FL>
<M e>at my right [hand] Michael,
<M h> מִימִינִי מִיכָאֵל <FL>
<M e>at my left [hand] Gabriel,
<M h> וּמִשְּׂ֒מֹאלִי גַבְרִיאֵל <FL>
<M e>before me Uriel,
<M h> וּמִלְּ֒פָנַי אוֹרִיאֵל <FL>
<M e>behind me Raphael,
<M h> וּמֵאֲחוֹרַי רְפָאֵל <FL>
<M e>and above my head, the Presence of Almighty.
<M h> וְעַל רֹאשִי שְׁכִינַת אֵל: <FL>
<M t2>A song of ascents
<M h> <M newbold> שִׁיר הַמַּעֲלוֹת <M reg> <FL>
<M e>Fortunate are all who fear Adonoy,
<M h> אַשְׁרֵי כָּל-יְרֵא יְהֹוָה <FL>
<M e>who walk in His ways.
<M h> הַהֹלֵךְ בִּדְרָכָיו: <FL>
<M e>When you eat of the toil of your hands
<M h> יְגִֽיעַ כַּפֶּֽיךָ כִּי תֹאכֵל <FL>
<M e>you are fortunate and it is good with you.
<M h> אַשְׁרֶֽיךָ וְטוֹב לָךְ: <FL>
<M e>Your wife will be like a fruitful vine
<M h> אֶשְׁתְּ֒ךָ כְּגֶֽפֶן פֹּרִיָּה <FL>
<M e>in the innermost parts of your house;
<M h> בְּיַרְכְּ֒תֵי בֵיתֶֽךָ <FL>
<M e>your children like olive plants
<M h> בָּנֶֽיךָ כִּשְׁתִלֵי זֵיתִים <FL>
<M e>around your table.
<M h> סָבִיב לְשֻׁלְחָנֶֽךָ: <FL>
<M e>Behold! thus shall be blessed the man
<M h> הִנֵּה כִי-כֵן יְבֹֽרַךְ גָּֽבֶר <FL>
<M e>who fears Adonoy.
<M h> יְרֵא יְהֹוָה: <FL>
<M e>Adonoy bless you from Zion!
<M h> יְבָרֶכְךָ יְהֹוָה מִצִּיּוֹן <FL>
<M e>and [may you] see the good of Jerusalem
<M h> וּרְאֵה בְּטוּב יְרוּשָׁלָֽםִ <FL>
<M e>all the days of your life!
<M h> כֹּל יְמֵי חַיֶּֽיךָ: <FL>
<M e>May you [live to] see
<M h> וּרְאֵה-
<M e>your children’s children!
<M h> בָנִים לְבָנֶֽיךָ <FL>
<M e>Peace upon Israel!<M tnt>
<M h> שָׁלוֹם עַל-יִשְׂרָאֵל: <FL>
<M in>To be said three times:<FC>
<M t2>Tremble and do not sin;
<M h> <M newbold> רִגְזוּ <M reg> וְאַל תֶּחֱטָֽאוּ <FL>
<M e>commune with your hearts upon your bed,
<M h> אִמְרוּ בִלְבַבְכֶם עַל מִשְׁכַּבְכֶם <FL>
<M e>and be silent, selah!<M tnt>
<M h> וְדֹֽמּוּ סֶֽלָה: <FL>
<M t2>Master of the Universe Who reigned
<M h> <M newbold> אֲדוֹן <M reg> עוֹלָם אֲשֶׁר מָלַךְ. <FL>
<M e>before any creature was created.
<M h> בְּטֶֽרֶם כָּל יְצִיר נִבְרָא: <FL>
<M e>At the time when all was made by His will,
<M h> לְעֵת נַעֲשָׂה בְחֶפְצוֹ כֹּל. <FL>
<M e>then was His Name proclaimed King.
<M h> אֲזַי מֶֽלֶךְ שְׁמוֹ נִקְרָא: <FL>
<M e>And after all things shall cease to be
<M h> וְאַחֲרֵי כִּכְלוֹת הַכֹּל. <FL>
<M e>the Awesome One will reign alone.
<M h> לְבַדּוֹ יִמְלֺךְ נוֹרָא: <FL>
<M e>He was, He is,
<M h> וְהוּא הָיָה וְהוּא הֹוֶה. <FL>
<M e>and He shall be in glory.
<M h> וְהוּא יִהְיֶה בְּתִפְאָרָה: <FL>
<M e>He is One, and there is no second
<M h> וְהוּא אֶחָד וְאֵין שֵׁנִי. <FL>
<M e>to compare to Him, to associate [with Him].
<M h> לְהַמְשִׁיל לוֹ לְהַחְבִּֽירָה: <FL>
<M e>Without beginning, without end,
<M h> בְּלִי רֵאשִׁית בְּלִי תַכְלִית. <FL>
<M e>power and dominion are His.
<M h> וְלוֹ הָעֹז וְהַמִּשְׂרָה: <FL>
<M e>He is my God and my ever-living Redeemer,
<M h> וְהוּא אֵלִי וְחַי גּוֹאֲלִי. <FL>
<M e>the Rock of my destiny in times of distress.
<M h> וְצוּר חֶבְלִי בְּעֵת צָרָה: <FL>
<M e>He is my flag and my refuge;
<M h> וְהוּא נִסִּי וּמָנוֹס לִי. <FL>
<M e>He is the portion of my cup on the day I call.
<M h> מְנָת כּוֹסִי בְּיוֹם אֶקְרָא: <FL>
<M e>Into His hand I entrust my spirit
<M h> בְּיָדוֹ אַפְקִיד רוּחִי. <FL>
<M e>[both] when I sleep and when I awaken.
<M h> בְּעֵת אִישַׁן וְאָעִֽירָה: <FL>
<M e>And with my spirit my body [too],
<M h> וְעִם רוּחִי גְּוִיָּתִי. <FL>
<M e>Adonoy is with me, I shall not fear.
<M h> יְהֹוָה לִי וְלֺא אִירָא: <FL>
<lp><M fn><M fnt>The word "bed" is used here figuratively for one’s future generations. See Rashi to <i>Genesis</i> 47:31; It was said of our forefather Jacob that "his bed was perfect: indicating that all his offspring were pure and steadfast.---<I>Iyun T’filoh</I><FL>
<M fnt>In this closing sentence of Psalm 90, Moses prays that the Divine Presence rest on the Jewish nation exclusively.<FL>
<M fnt>David prays first that the service Jewry performs in the Sanctuary, the sacrificial offerings, and the general performance of <i>mitzvos</i> be willingly accepted by God. Then he prays that even the work we do for our own needs be acceptable before Gold.---<I>Iyun T’Filoh</I>
<M fnt>The first mention of <i>work</i> refers to the actual endeavors of our hands, whereas the second mention of <i>work</i> refers to what was achieved by our hands.---<i>Iyun Tefilloh</i><FL>
<M fnt>"It" refers to "arrow," "pestilence," and "plague" of the previous verse.<FL>
<M fnt>You will only <i>see</i> the destruction but you will not be harmed by it.<FL>
<M fnt>Psalm 3 was sung by David when, at the age of 65, he had to flee his son Absalom.<FL>
<M fnt>David is confident of God’s help, because God has always smitten his enemies.---<i>Radak</i><FL>
